"This, however, is a very hard problem to solve and will take many years before we see useful fusion reactors built.","Aya, lameɛna, d ugur imi tewɛer mliḥ tifin n tifrat-is wa laqen aṭas n iseggasen i wakken ad nwali imsedmaren n uẓiẓẓref ttwabnan."
The steel needle floats on top of the water because of surface tension.,Tisegnit n wuzzal tettali deg waman ɣef tmentilt n tussda n tjumma.
Surface tension happens because the water molecules at the surface of the water are strongly attracted to each other more than they are to the air molecules above them.,Tussda n tjumma tettili-d acku ibelkimen n waman deg tjumma n waman ttemyijbaden gar-asen ugar n wacḥal ttemyijbaden d ibelkimen yellan s ufella. .

"Because the bottom of the blade is slightly curved, as the blade tilts to one side or the other, the edge which is in contact with the ice also curves.","Acku alqaɛ n lmus iɛewej-d cituḥ ɣer daxel, ɣef wayen xas immal ɣer tama neɣ ɣer tayeḍ alqaɛ i yettemlalen d ugris yettmal daɣen."
"This causes the skater to turn. If the skates tilt to the right, the skater turns right, if the skates tilt to the left, the skater turns left.","Aya iberran win itteḥnucuḍen. ma sebaḍ mmalen zelmeḍ, ad yemmal yid-sen ɣer zelmeḍ, ma mmalen ɣer yeffus, ad yemmal yid-sen ɣer yeffus."
"To return to their previous energy level, they must get rid of the extra energy they got from the light.","I wakken ad uɣalen ɣer weswir-nsen iɛeddan n sḥed, ilaq fell-asen ad ḍeqren sḥed n zzyada i asen-d-fka tafat."
"They do this by emitting a tiny particle of light called a ""photon"".","Xedmen aya s ussufeɣ n yiwen ubelkim i wumi qqaren ""afuṭun""."
"Scientists call this process ""stimulated emission of radiation"" because the atoms are stimulated by the bright light, causing the emission of a photon of light, and light is a type of radiation.","Imassanen ssawalen i ukala-agi ""aceyyeɛ n ufeǧeǧǧ s usendeh"" acku ibelkamen ttwasenḍen s tafat, i ɣef i d-iḍeṛṛu uceyyeɛ n ufuṭun n tafat, wa afeǧaǧǧ d tawsit n tafat."
"The next picture shows the atoms emitting photons. Of course, in reality photons are a lot smaller than those in the picture.","Tugna d-iteddun teskanay-d ibelkamen ttceyyiɛen ifuṭunen, iban, di tidet ifuṭṭunen deqs i meqrit ma ad tent-srewseḍ d wid n tugna."
Photons are even smaller than the stuff that makes up atoms!,Ifuṭnen meẓẓiyit ula ɣef iferdisen i yettemsalen ibelkimen!
After hundreds of hours of operation the filament in the bulb eventually burns out and the light bulb no longer works.,"Deffir kra n timḍiwin n tsaɛtin n useqdec, di taggara lxiḍ n teftilt ireq wa taftilt ur tettceɛil ara."
The light bulb then needs replacing. It is necessary to be careful in replacing the light bulb.,Taftilt dinna ilaq ad tettwabeddel. ilaq leḥder deg ubeddel-ines.
"First, the switch for the light fixture needs to be turned off or the cable disconnected.","Di tazwara, ilaq taqeffalt n tafat ad tili texsi, neɣ agatu yettwakkes-d."
This is because electricity flowing into the socket where the metallic part of bulb sits can give you a severe electric shock if you touch the inside of the socket or the metal base of the bulb while it is still partly in the socket.,Acku trisiti i yettazalen deg uḥric amɣuzan n tɣanimt uɣur teqqen teftilt izmer ad ak-id-iwwet s deqqa taẓṛuṛant meqqren mi ara tgred afus-ik ɣer daxel n tɣanimt neɣ ad tmasseḍ aḥric amɣuzan n teftilt mi ara tili mazal teqqen xas s cwiṭ ɣer tɣanimt.
"The major organ of the circulatory system is the heart, which pumps the blood.","Agman agejdan n unagraw uwnis d ul, i d tassufut n idamen."
Blood goes away from the heart in tubes called arteries and comes back to the heart in tubes called veins. The smallest tubes are called capillaries.,Idamen ttruḥun deg wul daxel n ijeɛbuben qqaren-asn iceryanen wa ttuɣalen-d s ul deg ijeɛbuben isemawen-nsen iẓuran. imecṭaḥ akk deg-sen ssawalen-asen anzaḍen n idamen.
A triceratops' teeth would have been able to crush not only leaves but even very tough branches and roots.,Tuɣmas n utrisiratubs zemrent ad fẓent mačči siwa iferrawen maca ula d ifurkan d iẓuran untimen.
"Some scientists think Triceratops ate cycads, which are a type of plant that was common in the Cretaceous.","Kra n yimussnawen ɣilen d akken Itrisiratubsen ččan isikaden, d anaw n yimɣi yellan d amagnu di tallit n Ukritasi."
"These plants look like a small palm tree with a crown of sharp, spiky leaves.","Imɣan-agi ttbanen-d am tezdayt tamecṭuḥt s yiferrawen uqḍiεen, ibedden am yisennanen."
A Triceratops could have used its strong beak to strip off the leaves before eating the trunk.,Atrisiratubs yessexdem ahat aqamum-is iǧehden i wakken ad yeqleε iferrawen-nni uqbel ad yečč ajgu.
"Other scientists argue that these plants are very poisonous so it is unlikely that any dinosaur ate them, even though today the sloth and other animals like the parrot (a descendant of the dinosaurs) can eat poisonous leaves or fruit.","Imussnawen niḍen sfuklen d akken imɣan-agi sεan ssem mliḥ dɣa ur cukken yečča-ten udinuẓur, xas akken ass-a amaṛxu d yiɣerṣiwen am ubabaɣayu (ccetla n udinuẓur) zemren ad ččen iferrawen neɣ igumma semmumen."
"How would Io's gravity pull on me? If you stood on the surface of Io, you would weigh less than you do on Earth.","Amek yezmer ad iyi-d-yejbed uzimaṣ n Iu? Ma yella tbeddeḍ ɣef tjumma n Iu, taẓayt-ik ad tenqes ɣef mi telliḍ ɣef Umaḍal."
"A person who weighs 200 pounds (90kg) on Earth would weigh about 36 pounds (16kg) on Io. So the gravity, of course, pulls less on you.","Amdan iweznen 200 n yibawden (90kg) ɣef Umaḍal ad yewzen tamudi n 36 n yibawden (16kg) ɣef Iu. Ihi uzimaṣ, s tidet, yejabbad-ik-id ciṭ kan."
"The Sun doesn't have a crust like the Earth that you can stand on. The whole Sun is made out of gases, fire, and plasma.","Iṭij ur yesεi ara tajumma ɣef wacu ad tbeddeḍ am Umaḍal. Iṭij s timmad-is yettwaxdem s wurrigen, times, d blasma."
The gas becomes thinner as you go farther from the center of the Sun.,Urrig yettuɣal d axfifan skud tettbeεεideḍ ɣef tlemmast n Yiṭij.
"The outer-part we see when we look at the Sun is called the photosphere, which means ""ball of light"".","Aḥric n beṛṛa i nettwali mi nettmuqul s Iṭij isem-is futusfer, anamek-is ""takurt n tafat""."
"About three thousand years later, in 1610, Italian astronomer Galileo Galilei used a telescope to observe that Venus has phases, just as the moon does.","Sakkin tamudi n kraḍ n yigiman n yiseggasen, di 1610, asnetray aṭelyani Galileu Galiley yessexdem atiliskub i wakken ad iẓer d akken Fenus tesεa tiswiεin, am wagur."
Phases happen because only the side of Venus (or of the Moon) facing the Sun is lighted. The phases of Venus supported the theory of Copernicus that the planets go around the Sun.,Tiswiεin ttilint-d acku siwa idis n Fenus (neɣ win n wagur) iwehhan ɣer Yiṭij iceεlen. Tiswiεin n Fenus ddant akked tiẓri n Kubernikus i d-yeqqaren d akken imtiwgen ttezzin i Yiṭij.
"Then, a few years later in 1639, an English astronomer named Jeremiah Horrocks observed a transit of Venus.","Sakkin, seld n kra n yiseggasen di 1639, asnetray Aglizi isem-is Jeremya Hurruk iwala aεeddi n Fenus."

"This fleet was led by Olaf Trygvasson, a Norwegian with ambitions to reclaim his country from Danish domination.","Tanawt-agi aqeṛṛuy-is d Ulaf Trigbasun, Anurwiǧi s usirem n tukksa n tmurt-is seg uɣmaṛ Adanmarki."
"After initial military setbacks, Ethelred was able to agree to terms with Olaf, who returned to Norway to try to gain his kingdom with mixed success.","Mbeɛd iɛewwiqen imezwura n tserdast, Etelred imsefham akked Ulaf, i yuɣalen ɣer Nurwiǧ iwakken ad iɛṛeḍ ad d-yerbeḥ tagelda-s s rrbeḥ imeckuken."
Hangeul is the only purposely invented alphabet in popular daily use. The alphabet was invented in 1444 during the reign of King Sejong (1418 – 1450).,Hangul d agemmay aywan i d-snulfan s demma i usexdem aɣeṛfan n yal ass. King Sejong was the fourth king of the Joseon Dynasty and is one of the most highly regarded.,Agellid Seyung d agellid wis ukkuẓ n Uzrar Ageldan Juseun yerna d yiwen seg wid i wumi rran azal meqqren.
"He originally named the Hangeul alphabet Hunmin Jeongeum, which means ""the correct sounds for the instruction of the people"".","Isem-is di tazwara Agemmay Hangul Hunmin Jeugeum, anamek-is ""imesla iṣeḥḥan i uselmed n yemdanen""."
There are many theories to how Sanskrit came into existence. One of them is about an Aryan migration from the west into India who brought their language with them.,Llant aṭaṣ n teẓṛiyin ɣef wamek i d-yussa Usanskrit ɣer tudert. Sanskrit is an ancient language and is comparable to the Latin language spoken in Europe.,Asanskrit d tutlayt taqburt yerna tettemcabi ɣer tutlayt Talatinit i ttmeslayen deg Tuṛuft.
"The earliest known book in the world was written in Sanskrit. After the compilation of Upanishads, Sanskrit just faded due to hierarchy.","Adlis amenzu yettwassnen akk deg umaḍal yettwajerred s Usanskrit. Seld asdukel n Yiubanicaden, Asanskrit iɣab lateṛ-is ɣef ljjal n umyellel."
"Sanskrit is a very complex and rich language, which has served to be the source for many modern Indian languages, just like Latin is the source for European languages like French and Spanish.","Asanskrit d tutlayt iṣeεben nezzeh yerna d tanesbaɣurt, d ayen i tt-yeǧǧan ad tili d aɣbalu n waṭas n tutlayin Tihendiyin tattrarin, am Tlatinit i yellan d aɣbalu n tutlayin Tuṛufin am Tefransist d Tesbanyulit."
"With the battle for France over, Germany began to get ready to invade the island of Britain.","Imi yefra umennuɣ n Franṣa, Lalman tebda tettheggay iman-is i wakken ad tenbez tigzirin n Briṭanya."
"Germany code-named the attack “Operation Sealion”. But the Royal Navy was still much stronger than the German Navy (“Kriegsmarine”) and could have destroyed any invasion fleet sent across the English Channel.,"Maca Taredsa Tageldant mazal-itt d tuntimt ugar ɣef Tegriwa Talalmanit (""Kriegsmarine"") yerna tella tezmer ad tesdegdeg yal tinawin n unbaz ad ceggεen izegren Ilel Aglizi."

"Submarines are ships designed to travel underwater, and remain there for an extended amount of time.","Tineṭṭabin d iɣeṛṛuba sugnen i wakken ad inigen ddaw n waman, yerna ad qqimen din akud ɣezzifen."
Submarines were used in World War I and World War II. Back then they were very slow and had a very limited shooting range.,Tineṭṭabin ttwasxedment di Trad Amaḍlan I d Trad Amaḍlan II. Di tallit-nni ttmurḍusent mliḥ yerna sεant annar n ujbad bu tilas.

German submarines were called U-Boats. The Germans were very good at navigating and operating their submarines.,Tineṭṭabin Tilalmaniyin qqaren-asent Iɣeṛṛuba-U. Ilalmaniyen snen mliḥ assilel akked uselḥu n tneṭṭabin-nsen.

"Yes! King Tutankhamun, sometimes referred to as ""King Tut"" or ""The Boy King"", is one of the most well known ancient Egyptian kings in modern times.","Ih! There are varying estimates for how many people speak Hindi. "Hindi and Urdu are similar in vocabulary but different in script; in everyday conversations, speakers of both languages can usually understand each other.","Tahendit d Turdut ttemcabint deg umawal maca mgaradent deg tira; deg udiwenni n yal ass, imsiwal n tutlayin-agi di snat zemren ad msefhamen gar-asen."

The Drukgyal Dzong is a ruined fortress and Buddhist monastery in the upper part of the Paro District (in Phondey Village).,Adrukgyal Dzung d agadir ihudden d ufakan Abuddi deg uḥric n ufella n Ugmam Baru (di Taddart Bundi).

Sikhism is a religion from the Indian sub-continent. It originated in the Punjab region during the 15th century from a sectarian split within the Hindu tradition.,Asixism d asɣan seg umenẓaw n wadda n Lhend. Iban-d deg temnaḍt n Bunjab deg tasut tis 15 seg beṭṭu n usɣan s daxel n unsay Ahindi.

"Sikhs call their religion Gurmat, which is Punjabi for ""way of the guru"". The guru is a fundamental aspect of all Indian religions but in Sikhism has taken on an importance that forms the core of Sikh beliefs.","Isixiyen ssawalen i usɣan-nsen Gurmat, anamek-is s Ubunjabi ""tamamekt n uguru"". The Indus Valley Civilization was a Bronze Age civilisation in the northwest Indian subcontinent encompassing most of modern-day Pakistan and some regions in northwest India and northeast Afghanistan.,Taɣeṛma n Uẓaɣar Indus d taɣeṛma n Tallit n Ubṛunz deg umenzaw Ahendi n ugafa i d-ijemεen tuget n Bakistan n tura d kra n temnaḍin n Lhend n ugafa amalu d Afɣanistan n ugafa asamar.

Some people believe that experiencing many artificially induced lucid dreams often enough can be very exhausting.,Kra n yimdanen ɣilen d akken tirmiyin n uxlaq n tirga yukin aṭas n tikkal d ayen yessefcalen mačči d kra.

"With fewer REMs per night, this state in which you experience actual sleep and your body recovers becomes infrequent enough to become a problem.","S kra n REM deg yiḍ, lḥala-agi anda teṭṭseḍ s tidet yerna anda tesgunfuy tfekka-k tettuɣal teεweq ddeqs-is i wakken ad yili uɣbel."

"The theory then established the idea that the Maori people migrated from Polynesia in a Great Fleet and took New Zealand from the Moriori, establishing an agricultural society.","Tamuɣli-agi umbeɛd tefka-d tikti id-iqqaren belli agdud n Mawri iguǧǧ si Bulinizya di tṛemmuɛt tameqqrant n teflugin dɣa kksen-asen Zilanda Tamaynut i Imuryuriten, anda id-sekren timetti tamɣigrant."
"However, new evidence suggests that the Moriori were a group of mainland Maori who migrated from New Zealand to the Chatham Islands, developing their own distinctive, peaceful culture.","Akken ibɣu yili, anzaten imaynuten skanen-d belli Imuryuriten llan d agraw deg ugdud n Mawri i yeguǧǧen si Zilanda Tamaynut ɣer Tegzirin n Čatam, anda snernan idles-nsen yemgaraden di lehna."
There was also another tribe on the Chatham islands these were Maori who migrated away from New Zealand.,Tella daɣen teqbilt niḍen di tegzirin n Čatam d imdanen n Mawri i yeguǧǧen si Zilanda Tamaynut.
"They called themselves the Moriori there were a few skirmishes and in the end, the Moriori were wiped out","Semman i yimman-nsen Imuryuriten llan kra imenɣiyen dɣa ɣer taggara, Imuryuriten negren"
Individuals who had been involved for several decades helped us appreciate our strengths and passions while candidly assessing difficulties and even failures.,Imdanen ittekkin aṭas n iseggasen ḥuman-aɣ ad nefk azal i tezmert-neɣ akked wacu neḥemmel yarna xedmen aktazal i wuguren akked ula d lexṣaṛat s tidett.
"While listening to individuals share their individual, family, and organizational stories, we gained valuable insight into the past and some of the personalities who influenced for good or ill the culture of the organization.","S usmeḥses i tmicuha n yemdanen, n twacult-nsen, akked tuddsa-nsen, nḥella-d tamusni isɛan azal ɣef yezri akked kra n ṭbiɛat i yesɛan tazrirt ilhan neɣ n diri ɣef idles n tuddsa."
"While understanding one’s history does not assume understanding of culture, it does at least help people gain a sense of where they fall within the history of the organization.","Xas akken afham n umezruy n yiwen mačči d afham n yidles, ittḥami imdanen anda ma ulac ad d-afen iman-nsen daxel n umezruy n tuddsa."
"While assessing the successes and becoming aware of failures, individuals and the whole of the participating persons discover more deeply the values, mission, and driving forces of the organization.","Deg uktazal n tarnawin akked ufiqi i lexṣaṛat, imdanen akked wid akk ittekkin ttafen-d s telqey imenzayen, tuɣdaṭ akked lebɣi txeddem tuddsa."
"In this instance, recalling previous instances of entrepreneurial behavior and resulting successes helped people to be open to new changes and new direction for the local church.","Deg umedya-agi, asmekti s imedyaten iɛeddan n lexdayem id-iglan s ternawin iḥuma imdanen ad ldin tiwwura i ubeddel akked ibardan imaynuten i tmezdayt tadigant."
"Such success stories lessened the fears of change, while creating positive inclinations toward change in the future.","Timicuha n tarnawt am ta-gi senqasent tigdi n ubeddel, slalayent-d lmil ilhan ɣer ubeddel deg imal."
Convergent thinking patterns are problem solving techniques that unite different ideas or fields to find a solution.,Udmawen n twengimt imiqṛaben d titwilin n ferru n wuguren i yesdukkulen tiktiwin neɣ annaren yemgaraden i tifin n tifrat.
"The focus of this mindset is speed, logic and accuracy, also identification of facts, reapplying existing techniques, gathering information.","Ṣṣenf-agi n ttexmam ittkel ɣef tazla, tameẓla akked tiseddi, daɣen aɛqal n tedyanin, aɛiwed n usexdem n tetwilin yellan yakan, ajmaɛ n yisallen."
"The most important factor of this mindset is: there is only one correct answer. You only think of two answers, namely right or wrong.","Ayen isɛan azal yakk di ttexmam-agi: tella kan yiwet n tririt iṣeḥḥan. Ad txemmemeḍ kan ɣef snat n tririyin, tin iṣeḥḥan neɣ tin icḍen."
This type of thinking is associated with certain science or standard procedures.,Ṣṣenf-agi n twengimt iqqen ɣer kra n tussna neɣ tsekkirin tinawayin.
"People with this type of thinking have logical thinking, are able to memorize patterns, solve problems and work on scientific tests.","Imdanen isɛan ṣṣenf-agi n twengimt sɛan tawengimt iṛeznen, zemren ad cfun i wunuɣen, ad frun iɣeblan yarna ad xedmen ɣef tirmitin n tussna."
Humans are by far the most talented species in reading the minds of others.,Imdanen d ṣenf n terwiḥin i yufraren akk di leqṛaya n tiktiwin n wiyiḍ.
"That means we are able to successfully predict what other humans perceive, intend, believe, know or desire.","Lmaɛna-s nezmer ad nfiq d acu fehmen, bɣan ad d-inin, ɣidden, ẓṛan neɣ bɣan yemdanen niḍen."
"Among these abilities, understanding the intention of others is crucial. It allows us to resolve possible ambiguities of physical actions.","Ger ti-gi, afiqi n leqsed n wiyiḍ isɛa azal d agejdan. Ittḥami di ferru n teqnuẓin i zemrent ad d xedment lexdayem n tfekka."
"For example, if you were to see someone breaking a car window, you would probably assume he was trying to steal a stranger’s car.","Amedya, lukan ad twaliḍ yiwen ittruẓ ṭaq n tkeṛṛust, ahat ad tɣiddeḍ ibɣa ad tt-yaker."
He would need to be judged differently if he had lost his car keys and it was his own car that he was trying to break into.,Ad tḥekmeḍ fell-as akken niḍen lukan d ttittin i yettu tisura n tkeṛṛust-is yarna d takeṛṛust-is i wuɣuṛ ittɛaṛaḍ ad ikcem.
"MRI is based on a physics phenomenon called nuclear magnetic resonance (NMR), which was discovered in the 1930s by Felix Bloch (working at Stanford University) and Edward Purcell (from Harvard University).","Radyu n Urgagi n Dkir tebna ɣef yiwet n tumant n tfizikt qqaren-as argagi n dkir ulawan, i d-yufa Feliks Bluk deg iseggasen n 1930 (mi yexeddem di Tesdawit n Stanfurd) akked Edward Bursel (n Tesdawit n Harbard)."
"In this resonance, magnetic field and radio waves cause atoms to give off tiny radio signals.","Deg urgagi-agi, annar n dkir akked lemwaji n ṛadyu deggiren ibelkimen ad d-ḍeggṛen licarat n ṛadyu timecṭaḥ."
"In the year 1970, Raymond Damadian, a medical doctor and research scientist, discovered the basis for using magnetic resonance imaging as a tool for medical diagnosis.","Deg useggas n 1970, Raymund Damadyan, d amejjay yarna d amusnaw n unadi, yufa-d lsas i usexdem n ṛadyu n urgagi n dkir d allal deg usennefru asejjan."
"Four years later a patent was granted, which was the world's first patent issued in the field of MRI.","Ukkuz n iseggasen umbeɛd iffeɣ-d uselkin n isnulfu, i yellan d amezwaru di ddunit deg unnar n ṛadyu n urgagi n dkir."
"In 1977, Dr. Damadian completed the construction of the first “whole-body” MRI scanner, which he called the ”Indomitable”.","Di 1977, Duktur Damadyan isellek lebni n ṛadyu n urgagi n dkir tamezwarut i ""tfekka s lekmal"", iwumi isemma ""tin ur nettneɣlab""."
Asynchronous communication encourages time for reflection and reaction to others.,Taywalt s uṛaǧu tettak akud i uxemmem akked tririt i wiyiḍ.
It allows students the ability to work at their own pace and control the pace of instructional information.,Tettaǧǧa inelmaden ad xedmen s ttawil-nsen yarna ad xtiṛen lemɣawla s wayes ad d-ttasen isallen n uselmed.
"In addition, there are fewer time restrictions with the possibility of flexible working hours. (Bremer, 1998)","Yarna, ulac aṭas n tilas n wakud rnu-as swayeɛ n uxeddim zemrent ad aẓent. (Bremer, 1998)"
The use of the Internet and the World Wide Web allows learners to have access to information at all times.,Asexdem n anternet akked Uẓeṭṭa Ameqqṛan n Ddunit iǧǧa inelmaden zemren ad d-afen isallen di yal lweqt.
"Students can also submit questions to instructors at any time of day and expect reasonably quick responses, rather than waiting until the next face-to-face meeting.","Inelmaden zemren ad ceyyɛen iseqsiyen i iselmaden melmi isen-ihwa deg wass yarna ur tettɛeṭṭil ara tririt, xiṛ ma rǧan arma d timlilit id-itteddun n wudem s udem."
The postmodern approach to learning offers the freedom from absolutes. There is no one good way to learn.,Tamuɣli mbeɛd-tatrarit n leqraya tefka tilelli seg umagdaz. Mačči yiwet n tarrayt ilhan n leqraya i yellan.
"In fact, there is not one good thing to learn.Learning takes place in the experience between the learner and the knowledge presented.","Di tidett, mačči yiwet n tɣawsa i yelhan i uḥfaḍ. Aḥfad ittili di tirmit ger unelmad akked tmussni id-ittuqeddmen."
"Our current experience with all the do-it-yourself and information presenting, learning-based television shows illustrates this point.","Tirmit-neɣ n tura akked tedwilin n tiliẓri yaɛnan aselmed akked tedwilin n xdem-it i yiman-ik akked uqeddem n isallen, tettawṣaf-d taneqqiḍt-agi."
So many of us find ourselves watching a television show that informs us of a process or experience in which we will never participate or apply that knowledge.,Aṭas deg-neɣ nettaf-d iman-neɣ nettwali tadwilt n tiliẓri iɣ-d-ittakken isallen ɣef tɣawsa neɣ tirmit d awezɣi ad nttekki deg-s neɣ ad nsexdem tamusni-nni.
"We will never overhaul a car, build a fountain in our backyard, travel to Peru to examine ancient ruins, or remodel our neighbour's house.","D awezɣi ad nɛiwwed i tkeṛṛust, ad nebnu aceṛcuṛ n waman di tmazirt, ad ninig ɣer Biru iwakken ad nesleḍ rmim aqdim, neɣ ad nɛiwwed i uxxam n lǧaṛ."
"Thanks to undersea fiber optic cable links to Europe and broadband satellite, Greenland is well connected with 93% of the population having internet access.","Imi illa lxiḍ iɛeddan s yilel iqqnen ɣer Uruba akked igensawen, Grinland teqqen akken iwata ɣer anternet imi 93% n imezdaɣ-is sɛan anternet."
"Your hotel or hosts (if staying in a guesthouse or private home) will likely have wifi or an internet connected PC, and all settlements have an internet cafe or some location with public wifi.","Asensu-nek neɣ imesterḥeb-ik (ma telliḍ di texxamt n inebgawen neɣ deg uxxam uslig) iban ad isɛu awifi neɣ aselkim isɛan anternet, yarna akk ixxamen n wejmaɛ seɛɛun taxxamt n iselkimen neɣ amekkan isɛan awifi."
"As mentioned above, though the word ""Eskimo"" remains acceptable in the United States, it is considered pejorative by many non-U.S. Arctic peoples, especially in Canada.","Amek i d-nnan uksawen-a, ɣas akken awal ""Eskimu"" yettwaqbel deg Yiwunak-Yedduklen, yettwaḥsab d ayen n dir sɣur waṭas n yegduden war Imarikaniyen n Artik, akka am Kanada."
"While you may hear the word used by Greenlandic Natives, its use should be avoided by foreigners.","Ɣas akken tzemrem ad teslem awal-a yettwasexdem ar Ineṣliyen n Gruenland, asexdem-ines ilaq ara ad tesxedmen ibeṛṛaniyen."
"The native inhabitants of Greenland call themselves Inuit in Canada and Kalaalleq (plural Kalaallit), a Greenlander, in Greenland.","Imezdaɣ ineṣliyen n Grinland ssawalen iman-nsen Inuwit deg Kanada akked Kalaalleq (asget Kalaallit), Agrinlander, deg Grinland."
"Crime, and ill-will toward foreigners in general, is virtually unknown in Greenland. Even in the towns, there are no ""rough areas.""","S umata, ulac timenɣa akked lkarh n ibaṛṛaniyen di Grinland. Ula di temdinin, ulac ""timnaḍin iwaɛṛen."""
Cold weather is perhaps the only real danger the unprepared will face.,Lḥal asemmaḍ d amihi n tidett awḥid i yezmer ad iqabel win ur s-negmin ara.
"If you visit Greenland during cold seasons (considering that the further north you go, the colder it will be), it is essential to bring warm enough clothing.","Ma terziḍ ɣer Grinland di tallit taṣemmaḍt (imi simmal tettaliḍ s agafa, simmal ittismiḍ lḥal), ilaq ad tawiḍ iselsa iḥman."
The very long days in the summer can lead to problems getting sufficient sleep and associated health issues.,Ussan ɣezzifen deg unebdu zemren ad d-glun s wuguren n yiḍes akked wuguren n tdawsa icudden ɣer way-agi.
"During the summer, also watch out for the Nordic mosquitoes. Although they do not transmit any diseases, they can be irritating.","Deg unebdu, ḥader nnamus n ugafa. Xas akken ur isenṭaḍ ara lehlakat, isefqaɛ."
"While San Francisco's economy is linked to it being a world-class tourist attraction, its economy is diversified.","Xas akken tadamsa n San Fransisku teqqen ɣer imukan-is n tteḥwas isɛan tamekkant tamaḍlant, tadamsa-nes tesɛa tanḍa."
"The largest employment sectors are professional services, government, finance, trade, and tourism.","Innaren n uxeddim imeqqṛanen yakk d imeẓla imsudar, anabaḍ, tadrimt, tanezzut, akked tteḥwas."
"Its frequent portrayal in music, films, literature and popular culture has helped make the city and its landmarks known throughout the world.","Awṣaf-is iqwan di tezlatin, isura, tasekla akked yidles aɣeṛfan iḥuma tamdint akked izumal-is ad ttwasnen di ddunit maṛṛa."
"San Francisco has developed a large tourist infrastructure with numerous hotels, restaurants, and top-notch convention facilities.","San Fransisku tebna izadaɣen imeqqranen i iḥewwasen akked waṭas n isensa, isečča, akked izadaɣen n iseqquma n uswir amezwaru."
"San Francisco is also one of the best places in the nation for other Asian cuisine: Korean, Thai, Indian, and Japanese.","San Fransisku daɣen d yiwen seg imukan imawayen di tmurt i lmakla n Asya: Takurit, Taṭaylandit, Tahendit, akked Tjabunit."
Traveling to Walt Disney World represents a major pilgrimage for many American families.,Tirza ɣer Umaḍal n Walt Disney tettuneḥsab d lḥiǧǧ ameqqṛan ɣer waṭas n twaculin Timarikaniyin.
"The ""typical"" visit involves flying into Orlando International Airport, busing to an on-site Disney hotel, spending about a week without leaving Disney property, and returning home.","""Amedya"" n tirza-agi d affug ɣer Unafag Agreɣlan n Urlandu, tuṭṭfa n lkaṛ arma d asensu n Disney, asɛeddi n wazal n ddurt mebla tuffɣa seg wayla n Disney, akked tuɣalin ɣer uxxam."
"There are infinite variations possible, but this remains what most people mean when they talk of ""going to Disney World"".","Illa waṭas n lxilaf izemren ad yili, maca d ay-agi i yebɣa ad d-iqsed umur ameqqran n imdanen s ""ṛṛwaḥ ɣer Umaḍal n Disney""."
Many tickets sold online through auction websites such as eBay or Craigslist are partially used multi-day park-hopper tickets.,Atas seg itikiyen ittnuzen deg anternet di tansiwin am iBay neɣ Kragzlist kra deg-sen ttusexdamen d itikiyen n wekcam n waṭas n wussan ur nettwasexdam ara s waṭas.
"While this is a very common activity, it is prohibited by Disney: the tickets are non-transferable.","Xas akken ccɣel-agi imucaɛ, ittwagdel sɣuṛ Disney: itikiyen ur ttembeddalen ara."
Any camping below the rim in Grand Canyon requires a backcountry permit.,Yal asdar seddaw n yiri Grand Kanyun ilaq-as ttesriḥ n deffir n tmurt.
"Permits are limited to protect the canyon, and become available on the 1st day of the month, four months prior to the start month.","Tesriḥ sɛan afellay akken ad ḥaṛben ɣef kanyun, ad ilin ass 1 n waggur, kuẓ n wagguren weqbel n waggur n tawada."
"Thus, a backcountry permit for any start date in May becomes available on 1 Jan.","Sakkin, ttesriḥ n unekcum ɣer deffir n tmurt i yal azemz n tazwara n Mayu yettili deg 1 n Yennayer."
"Space for the most popular areas, such as the Bright Angel Campground adjacent to Phantom Ranch, generally fill up by the requests received on first date they are opened to reservations.","Imekwan mucaɛen, am Brayt Anjil Kamgrund yellan ɣer tama n Fantum Ranč, ttacaṛen s umata s issutren i sen-yettawḍen ass amenzu anda ldin yeḥrazen."
"There are a limited number permits reserved for walk-in requests available on a first come, first served basis.","Yella wemḍan afellay n ttesriḥ i yettwajemɛen i isutren n yimir kan, s umenzay n win d-yewḍen d amenzu, ara yawin damezwaru."
Entering Southern Africa by car is an amazing way to see all the region's beauty as well as to get to places off the normal tourist routes.,Akcam n Tefriqt n Unẓul s tkeṛṛust d tarrayt igerzen iwakken ad twaliḍ akk cbaḥa n temnaḍt-agi akked daɣen i ṛṛwaḥ ɣer imukan akkin i yiberdan nummen iḥewwasen.
This can be done in a normal car with careful planning but a 4x4 is highly advised and many locations are only accessible with a high wheel base 4x4.,Aya-gi izmer ad ittwaxdem s tkeṛṛust kan akka akked uheggi lɛali maca takeṛṛust 4x4 tlaq mliḥ yarna aṭas n imukan tteḥwiǧin takeṛṛust 4x4 s ṛwadi tiɛlayanin.
Keep in mind while planning that although Southern Africa is stable not all neighboring countries are.,Mi ara tiliḍ tettheggiḍ ay-agi cfu belli xas akken Tafriqt n Unẓul terked mačči d lḥala n yakk timura is-d-izzin.
Visa requirements and costs vary from nation to nation and are affected by the country you come from.,Cuṛuṭ n lbiza akked suma ittemxalaf si tmurt ɣer tayeḍ aɛlaḥsab n tmurt ansi ara d-tṛuḥeḍ.
Each country also has unique laws requiring what emergency items need to be in the car.,Yal tamurt daɣen tesɛa aṣaḍuf weḥdes yaɛnan tiɣawsiwin n usellek n teṛwiḥin i yelaq ad ilint di tkeṛṛust.
"Victoria Falls is a town in the western portion of Zimbabwe, across the border from Livingstone, Zambia, and near Botswana.","Bikturya Fulz d tamdint deg uḥric n umalu n Zimbabwi, akkin i tlisa n Libinstun, Zambya, tama n Butswana."
"The town lies immediately next to the falls, and they are the major attraction, but this popular tourist destination offers both adventure seekers and sightseers plenty of opportunities for a longer stay.","Tamdint tezga-d tama n uceṛcuṛ, amekkan agejdan id-ijebbden iḥewwasen, maca amekkan-agi imucaɛen n iḥewwasen ittak-d i wid ittnadin aqemmeṛ akked imerraḥen aṭas n tegnatin i iɣimi aṭas n lweqt."
"In the rainy season (November to March), the water volume will be higher and the Falls will be more dramatic.","Di tallit n igefran (Unbir arma d Meɣres), aswir n waman ittaɛlay dɣa aceṛcuṛ ad d-iban isexlaɛ."
You are guaranteed to get wet if you cross the bridge or walk along the trails winding near the Falls.,Neḍmen-ik ad tellexseḍ ma tzegreḍ s tqenṭeṛt neɣ telḥiḍ deg ibardan idewṛen tama n uceṛcuṛ.
"On the other hand, it is precisely because the volume of water is so high that your viewing of the actual Falls will be obscured—by all the water!","Si tama niḍen, s sebba n uswir n waman aɛlayan tamuɣli-nek n uceṛcuṛ-nni ad tettusdeṛɣel - s waman-nni akk!"
"Tomb of Tutankhamun (KV62). KV62 may be the most famous of the tombs in the Valley, the scene of Howard Carter's 1922 discovery of the almost intact royal burial of the young king.","Aẓekka n Tutanxamun (KB62). KB62 ahat d aẓekka imucaɛen yakk deg iẓekwan n Uzaɣar-agi, amekkan anda i d-yufa Huward Karter di 1922 aẓekka ageldan n ugellid ilemẓi qṛib ulac acu t-yuɣen."
"Compared to most of the other royal tombs, however, the tomb of Tutankhamun is barely worth visiting, being much smaller and with limited decoration.","Mi ara twaliḍ amur ameqqran n iẓekwan igeldanen niḍen, akken ibɣu yili, aẓekka n Tutanxamun ur yuklal ara ad terzuḍ ɣur-s, imi imecṭuḥ mliḥ yarna ur ittucebbeḥ ara mliḥ."
Anyone interested in seeing evidence of the damage to the mummy done during attempts to remove it from the coffin will be disappointed as only the head and shoulders are visible.,Yal win ibɣan ad iwali anza n lemḍaṛṛa is-iḍṛan i tmumitt-agi mi ttɛaṛaḍen ad tt-id-kksen si lekfen ad issers iman-is imi ḥala aqeṛṛuy-is akked tuyat-is id-ittbanen.
"The fabulous riches of the tomb are no longer in it, but have been removed to the Egyptian Museum in Cairo.","Igerrujen illan deg uẓekka-agi ulac-iten deg-s, wwin-ten ɣer Usalay n Maṣer di Lqahira."
Visitors with limited time would be best to spend their time elsewhere.,Iḥewwasen ur nesɛi ara aṭas n lweqt axiṛ-asen ad sɛeddin lweqt-nsen anda niḍen.
"Phnom Krom, 12 km southwest of Siem Reap. This hilltop temple was built at the end of the 9th century, during the reign of King Yasovarman.","Bnum Krum, 12 km ɣer unẓul-amalu n Syem Rib. Afakan-agi illan di tiɣilt ittwabna di taggara n lqaṛn wis 9, di leḥkem n Ugellid Yazubarman."
The gloomy atmosphere of the temple and the view over the Tonle Sap lake make the climb to the hill worthwhile.,Tebrek isɛa ufakan-agi akked imeẓri n temda n Tunel Sab erran talleyt n tiɣilt-agi tesɛa azal.
A visit to the site can be conveniently combined with a boat trip to the lake.,Tirza ɣer umekkan-agi tezmer ad tettusdukkel akked umerreḥ s teflugt di temda.
The Angkor Pass is needed to enter the temple so do not forget to bring your passport along when heading to Tonle Sap.,Ttesriḥ n Angkur ilaq i ukcam ɣer ufakan ɣef ay-a ur ttettu ara ad d-tawiḍ amsineg yid-k mi ara d-taseḍ ɣer Tunel Sab.
"Jerusalem is the capital and largest city of Israel, though most other countries and the United Nations do not recognize it as Israel's capital.","Urcalim d tamannaɣt yarna d tamdint tameqqrant yakk n Israyil, xas akken amur ameqqran n tmura niḍen akked Leǧnas Idduklen ur stɛerfen ara yis d tamannaɣt n Israyil."
The ancient city in the Judean Hills has a fascinating history spanning thousands of years.,Tamdint taqdimt di Tɣaltin n Judi tesɛa amezruy isedhacen ikkan d luluf n iseggasen.
"The city is holy to the three monotheistic religions - Judaism, Christianity and Islam, and serves as a spiritual, religious, and cultural center.","Tamdint d taqedsant ɣer krad n deyanat n yiwen n uṛebbit - Tayahudit, Tamasiḥit akked Tneslemt, yarna tettuneḥsab d agens n ṛṛuḥ, n deyana, akked yidles."
"Due to the religious significance of the city, and in particular the many sites of the Old City area, Jerusalem is one of the main tourist destinations in Israel.","S sebba n wazal adeyani i tesɛa temdint-agi, akked abaɛda aṭas n imukan n Temdint Taqdimt, Urcalim d yiwen seg imukan n umerreḥ igejdanen di Israyil."
"Jerusalem has many historic, archeological and cultural sites, along with vibrant and crowded shopping centers, cafés, and restaurants.","Urcalim tesɛa aṭas n imukan imazrayen, isenziken akked idelsanen, akked igensawen isenzanen ittačaṛen, leqhawi, akked imukan n wučči."
Ecuador requires that Cuban citizens receive an invitation letter prior to entering Ecuador through international airports or frontier admission points.,Ikwadur tḥettem i yiɣeṛman n Kuba ad ten-taweḍ tebratt n unaɛṛuḍ uqbel ad kecmen ɣer Ikwadur deg inafagen igreɣlanen neɣ di tneqqiḍin n unekcum ɣef tlisa.
"This letter must be legalized by the Ecuadorian Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and comply with certain requirements.","Tabratt-agi ilaq ad tettuselken sɣuṛ Uneɣlaf n Lecɣal n Baṛṛa n Ikwadur, yarna ad tqadeṛ kra n ccuṛuṭ."

"Seeing the sites and wildlife of the Galapagos is best done by boat, just as Charles Darwin did it in 1835.","Timẓṛa n imukan akked tudert taweḥcit n Galabagus telha axiṛ s teflugt, am akken itt-yexdem Čarl Darwin di 1835."
Over 60 cruise ships ply the Galapagos waters - ranging in size from 8 to 100 passengers.,Kter n 60 n teflugin n tteḥwas i yettawin aratu deg waman n Galabagus - ittawin si 8 ɣer 100 n yemdanen.

"A traveller with piles of money might consider a round the world flight, broken up with stays in many of these hotels.","Aḥewwas isɛan taṛemmuɛt n yedrimen izmer ad ibɣu ad ixdem affug ara d-izzin i ddunit, ara ibḍun s tɣimiyin deg aṭas n isensa-agi."
A hospitality exchange network is the organization that connects travelers with locals in the cities they are going to visit.,Aẓeṭṭa n usterḥeb d tuddsa isemlalayen iḥewwasen akked imezdaɣ idiganen n temdinin wuɣuṛ ara rzun.

Couchsurfing was founded in January 2004 after computer programmer Casey Fenton found a cheap flight to Iceland but did not have a place to stay.,Kawčsurfin tettusnulfa-d di Yennayer 2004 mbeɛd mi d-yufa umsihel Kazey Fentun affug iṛexsen ɣer Island maca ur d-yufi ara anda ara yens.

"Written words are often easier to understand than spoken words, also. This is especially true of addresses, which are often difficult to pronounce intelligibly.","Awalen yuran s umata sehlen akter i ufham ɣef wawalen ittwanṭqen. Aya-gi yaɛna abaɛda tansiwin, ittiwɛiṛen s umata i lmenṭeq."
"Many entire nations are completely fluent in English, and in even more you can expect a limited knowledge - especially among younger people.","Aṭas n tmura hedrent Taglizit akken igerrez, yarna deg uṭun imeqqṛen akter n tmura tzemreḍ ad tafeḍ ciṭ n tmussni deg-s - abaɛda ɣer yelmeẓyen."
"Imagine, if you will, a Mancunian, Bostonian, Jamaican and Sydneysider sitting around a table having dinner at a restaurant in Toronto.","Xayel-d, ma tebɣiḍ, Amankuni, Abustuni, Ajamayki akked umezdaɣ n Sidni qqimen ɣer ṭabla setten imensi di ṛasṭuṛa di Ṭuruntu."
"They're regaling each other with stories from their hometowns, told in their distinct accents and local argot.","Ḥekkun-d timicuha n tmura-nsen, s lmenṭeq-nsen yemgaraden akked lehduṛ-nsen idiganen."
"Buying food in supermarkets is usually the cheapest way to get fed. Without cooking opportunities, choices are however limited to ready-made food.","Tiɣin n lmakla deg wagens asenzan s umata d tarrayt iṛxisen yakk i lmakla. Mebla tignatin n usebbi, lxetyaṛ i yellan d lmakla iheggan kan."
Increasingly supermarkets are getting a more varied section of ready-made food. Some even provide a microwave oven or other means to heat food.,Simmal ttilin deg igensan isenzanen imukan isɛan lxetyaṛat akteṛ n lmakla iheggan. Kra sɛan ula d afuṛnu ileḥḥun s lemwaji timecṭaḥ neɣ allalen niḍen i useḥmu n lmakla.
"In some countries or types of stores there is at least one on-site restaurant, often a rather informal one with affordable prices.","Di kra n tmura neɣ kra n leṣnaf n tḥuna tettili anda ma ulac yiwet n ṛasṭuṛa, s umata war-tunṣibt s sumat yarxisen."
Make and carry copies of your policy and your insurer's contact details with you.,Xdem-d yarna awi talsuffɣin n tsertit-ik akked isallen yaɛnan ṭamen-ik akkid-k.
They need to show the insurer's e-mail address and international phone numbers for advice/authorizations and making claims.,Ilaq ad seknen imayl n ṭamen akked wuṭunen n tilifun igreɣlanen i naṣayeḥ/ttesriḥat akked ucetki.
"Have another copy in your luggage and online (e-mail to yourself with attachment, or stored in the ""cloud"").","Eǧǧ talsuffeɣt niḍen di leḥwal-ik akked deg anternet (ceyyeɛ imayl i yiman-ik s ufaylu-agi, neɣ ejmeɛ-it di ""taguyt"")."
"If traveling with a laptop or tablet, store a copy in its memory or disc (accessible without the internet).","Ma tettinigeḍ s uselkim neɣ tetablitt, ejmeɛ-it di ccfawat-is neɣ deg uḍebsi (iwejden mebla anternet)."
Also give policy/contact copies to traveling companions and relatives or friends back home willing to help.,Yernu efk talsuffɣin n tsertit/isallen i imdukkal n tteḥwas akked wid ik-ittilin neɣ imdukkal-ik di tmurt-ik i yebɣan ad ɛiwnen.
"Moose (also known as elk) aren't inherently aggressive, but will defend themselves if they perceive a threat.","Muz (ittwassnen daɣen s yisem n elk) ur ttawḍen ara, maca ttḥuddun iman-nsen ma hulfan i umihi."
"When people don't see moose as potentially dangerous, they may approach too closely and put themselves at risk.","Ma yili lɣaci ur ḥsiben ara muz d amihaw, zemren ad aẓen ɣur-s mliḥ s wakka ad d-afen iman-nsen deg umihi."
"Drink alcoholic drinks with moderation. Alcohol affects everyone differently, and knowing your limit is very important.","Sew iɣisem s ṛzana. Iɣisem isɛa tazrirt s wudem yemgaraden ɣef yal yiwen, s wakka tamusni n tlisa-nek isɛa mliḥ azal."
Possible long term health events from excessive drinking can include liver damage and even blindness and death. The potential danger is increased when consuming illegally produced alcohol.,Uguren n tdawsa s teɣzi n wakud n waṭas n tissit izmer ad tili gar-asen lemḍaṛṛa n tassa akked ula d tideṛɣelt d lmut. Amihi ittimɣuṛ s tissit n iɣisem ittwaxedmen s wudem aruzrif.
"Illegal spirits can contain various dangerous impurities including methanol, which can cause blindness or death even in small doses.","Iɣisem aruzrif izmer ad isɛu ifardisen imihawen yemgaraden gar-asen mitanul, i yezemren ad d-yeglu s tdeṛɣelt neɣ lmut xas s tkemmicin timecṭaḥ."
"Eyeglasses can be cheaper in a foreign country, especially in low-income countries where labour costs are lower.","Nwaḍeṛ zemrent ad ilint ṛxisent di tmurt tabaṛṛanit, abaɛda di tmura isɛan tijeṛniḍin timecṭaḥ anda lexlaṣ n ixeddamen yeṛxes."
"Consider getting an eye exam at home, especially if insurance covers it, and bringing the prescription along to be filed elsewhere.","Xemmem ad txedmeḍ akayad n wallen di tmurt-ik, abaɛda ma tɣumm-it ṭmana, umbeɛd awi lkaɣeḍ-nni n nwaḍeṛ ik-ilaqen ad k-tent-id-xedmen anda niḍen."
"High-end brand-name frames available in such areas may have two problems; some may be knock-offs, and the real imported ones may be more expensive than at home.","Nwaḍeṛ n lmarkat n lɛali illan di temnaḍin-agi zemrent ad sɛunt sin wuguren ; kra izmer mačči d tineṣliyin, ma d tid n tidett id-ittwaceyyɛen si lbaṛṛani ɣlayent ahat kter n tmurt-ik."
"Coffee is one of the world's most traded commodities, and you can probably find many types in your home region.","Lqahwa d yiwet si tɣawsiwin ittnuzen s waṭas di ddunit, yarna tzemreḍ ad d-tafeḍ ahat aṭas n leṣnaf di temnaḍt anda tzedɣeḍ."
"Nevertheless, there are many distinctive ways of drinking coffee around the world that are worth experiencing.","Maca, llant waṭas n tarrayin yemgaraden n tissit n lqahwa di ddunit maṛṛa i yuklalen aɛṛaḍ."
"Canyoning (or: canyoneering) is about going in a bottom of a canyon, which is either dry or full of water.","Akanyuni d aṣubbu ɣer lqaɛ n wassif, ama iqquṛ ama iččur d aman."
"Canyoning combines elements from swimming, climbing and jumping--but requires relatively little training or physical shape to get started (compared to rock climbing, scuba diving or alpine skiing, for example).","Akanyuni isdukkul iferdisen id-yekkan si lɛum, talleyt n idurar akked ungaz--maca itteḥwiǧi ciṭ n usluɣmu neɣ cṭaṛa iwakken ad tebduḍ (mačči am talleyt n iẓṛa, aɣḍas neɣ aḥlucceg deg idurar n alb)."
"Hiking is an outdoor activity which consists of walking in natural environments, often on hiking trails.","Tikli d ccɣel ittilin baṛṛa n wexxam d tikli di twennaḍt tagamant, s umata deg ibardan ittwaxedmen i tikli."
Day hiking involves distances of less than a mile up to longer distances that can be covered in a single day.,Tikli n wass taɛna teɣzi n ibardan ur newwiḍ ara yiwen n lmil arma d tin ɣezzifen kter i yezmer umdan ad ilḥu deg yiwen n wass.
"For a day hike along an easy trail little preparations are needed, and any moderately fit person can enjoy them.","Tikli n wass deg ubrid isehlen teḥwaǧ kan ciṭ n uheggi, yarna yal win isɛan tazmert talemmast kan ad yaff iman-is deg-s."
"Families with small children may need more preparations, but a day outdoors is easily possible even with babies and pre-school children.","Tiwaculin isɛan igerdan imecṭaḥ zemrent ad ḥwiǧent aheggi akter, maca tuffɣa deg uzal teshel ula s igerdan ileqqaqen akked igerdan urɛad nekcim ɣer uɣerbaz."
"Internationally, there are nearly 200 running tour organizations. Most of them operate independently.","S wudem agreɣlan, llant wazal n 200 n tuddsiwin n tteḥwas. Amur ameqqran deg-sent xeddment s wudem amunan."
"The Global Running Tours successor, Go Running Tours networks dozens of sightrunning providers on four continents.","Tin yuɣalen deg umekkan n Glubal Rannin Tawerz, Gaw Rannin Tawerz teqqen aṭas n wid id-ittakken imeẓla n uḥewwes di ukkuz n imenẓawen."
"With roots in Barcelona's Running Tours Barcelona and Copenhagen's Running Copenhagen, it was quickly joined by Running Tours Prague based in Prague and others.","S iẓewṛan id-yekkan si Rannin Tawerz Barsuluna di Barsuluna akked Rannin Kubinhagen di Kubinhagen, ur iɛeṭṭel ara irna-d ɣuṛ-sen Rannin Tawerz Brag di Brag akked wiyiḍ."
There are many things you have to take into consideration before and when you travel somewhere.,Llan waṭas n lecɣal fayef i yelaq ad txemmemeḍ uqbel akked mi ara tinigeḍ ɣer walebɛaḍ n imukan.
"When you travel, expect things not to be like they are ""back home"". Manners, laws, food, traffic, lodging, standards, language and so on will to some extent differ from where you live.","Mi ara tinigeḍ, gmen ɣef lecɣal ad ilin mxalafen ɣef ""tmurt-ik"". Lexdayem, isuḍaf, lmakla, tikli n tkeṛṛusin, asensu, imenzayen, tutlayt akked wayen niḍen ad imxalaf ɣef anda tettidireḍ."
"This is something you always need to keep in mind, to avoid disappointment or perhaps even distaste over local ways to do things.","D taɣawsa i yelaqen ad teqqim i lbal-ik, iwakken ur tettneɣniḍ ara neɣ ur tkarreheḍ ara amek xeddmen lecɣal imezdaɣ idiganen."
"Travel agencies have been around since the 19th century. A travel agent is usually a good option for a journey which extends beyond a traveller's previous experience of nature, culture, language or low-income countries.","Tikebbaniyin n uḥewwes llant si lqaṛn wis 19. Axeddam n tteḥwas s umata d lxetyaṛ igerzen i yinig ara iɛeddin akkin i tirmit taqdimt n uḥewwas deg ugama, idles, tutlayt neɣ di tmura isɛan lmedxul amecṭuḥ."
"Although most agencies are willing to take on most regular bookings, many agents specialise in particular types of travel, budget ranges or destinations.","Xas akken amur ameqqran n tkebbaniyin n uḥewwes ttaqbalent amur ameqqran n uheggi n imukan, aṭas d timaẓlayin deg yiwen n ṣenf n yinig, n tedrimt neɣ imukan."
It can be better to use an agent who frequently books similar trips to yours.,Izmer ad ilhu usexdem n tkebbanit n uḥewwes i yezgan tettheggi-d inigen am win tebɣiḍ.
"Take a look at what trips the agent is promoting, whether on a website or in a shop window.","Wali acu n yinigen i tettdellil tkebbanit, ama di tansa-nes n anternet ama di ṭaq n tḥanutt-is."
"If you want to see the world on the cheap, for necessity, lifestyle or challenge, there are some ways to do that.","Ma tebɣiḍ ad twaliḍ ddunit s suma iṛxisen, i lmeḥwiǧat, aɣan n tudert neɣ i ucqiṛṛew, illa wamek ara txedmeḍ ay-agi."
"Basically, they fall into two categories: Either work while you travel or try and limit your expenses. This article is focused on the latter.","S wudem agejdan, bḍan ɣef sin leṣnaf : xeddem mi ara tettḥewwiseḍ neɣ egg tilas i uṣeṛṛef-ik. Amagrad-agi ilha-d d uneggaru-agi."
"For those willing to sacrifice comfort, time and predictability to push expenses down close to zero, see minimum budget travel.","I wid ibɣan ad sebblen astaɛfu, akud akked ugman i uṣubbu n uṣaṛṛef ɣer tama n yilem, wali inig n tedrimt taddayt."
"The advice assumes that travellers do not steal, trespass, participate in the illegal market, beg, or otherwise exploit other people for their own gain.","Aweṣṣi-agi iḥseb iminigen ur ttakren ara, ur tɛeddayen ara ɣef ayla n wiyiḍ, ur ttekkin ara di ssuq aruzrif, ur suturen ara, ur sexdamen ara wiyiḍ iwakken ad awḍen ɣer yeswi-nsen."
"An immigration checkpoint is usually the first stop when disembarking from a plane, a ship, or another vehicle.","Amekkan n uḥettec s umata d amekkan amezwaru ideg ara tḥebseḍ mi ara d-terseḍ si tmesrifegt, lbabuṛ, neɣ tkeṛṛust niḍen."
In some cross-border trains inspections are done on the running train and you should have valid ID with you when boarding one of those trains.,Di kra n tmacinin n ger-tlisa aḥettec ittili di tmacint-nni mi tleḥḥu s wakka ilaq ad tesɛuḍ lekwaɣeḍ iwatan yid-k mi ara tedduḍ di yiwet si tmacinin-agi.
"On night sleeper trains, passports may be collected by the conductor so that you do not have your sleep interrupted.","Di tmacinin n yiḍ, imsinigen izmer ad ten-ijmeɛ unehhar iwakken ur k-id-sakayen ara."
"Registration is an additional requirement for the visa process. In some countries, you must register your presence and address where you are staying with the local authorities.","Ajerred d cerṭ n zyada n ubiza. Di kra n tmura, ilaq ad tjerrdeḍ tilin-ik akked tansa anda ara tqimeḍ ɣer imsulta idiganen."
This might require filling out a form with the local police or a visit to the immigration offices.,Aya-gi izmer ad iḥwiǧ aɛemmer n lkaɣeḍ ɣer yimsulta idiganen neɣ tirza ɣer tnariyin n yinig.
"In many countries with such a law, local hotels will handle the registration (make sure to ask).","Deg waṭas n tmura isɛan aṣaḍuf-agi, xeddmen ajerred isensa idiganen (seqsi-d)."
"In other cases, only those staying outside of tourist accommodations need to register.  However, this makes the law much more obscure, so find out beforehand.","Di lḥalat niḍen, ḥala wid ara insen baṛṛa n isensa n iḥewwasen i yelaq ad jerrden. Akken ibɣu yili, ay-agi yarra aṣaḍuf-agi ur imefhum ara, ɣef ay-agi nadi isallen ɣef zik."
Architecture is concerned with the design and construction of buildings. The architecture of a place is often a tourist attraction in its own right.,Tasegda d unuɣ akked lebni n izadaɣen. Tasegda n wemkan weḥdes d ayen id-ijebbden iḥewwasen s umata.
Many buildings are quite beautiful to look at and the view from a tall building or from a cleverly-positioned window can be a beauty to behold.,Aṭas n izadaɣen cebḥen i umuqqel yarna tamuɣli seg uzadaɣ aɛlayan neɣ si ṭaq isɛan amekkan n lɛali izmer ad yili d ayen icebḥen i umuqqel.
"Architecture overlaps considerably with other fields including urban planning, civil engineering, decorative arts, interior design and landscape design.","Tasegda tekcem deg waṭas n innaren niḍen am usɣiwes n temdint, tajenyuṛt n temdint, taẓuṛi n ucebbeḥ, acebbeḥ n daxel n wexxam, acebbeḥ n ufrag."
"Given how remote many of the pueblos are, you won't be able to find a significant amount of nightlife without traveling to Albuquerque or Santa Fe.","Imi aṭas n tudrin baɛdent wa-gar-asent, ur tettafeḍ ara azal ameqqṛan n zzhu n yiḍ mebla ma truḥeḍ ɣer Abukurk neɣ Santa Fi."
"However, nearly all of the casinos listed above serve drinks, and several of them bring in name-brand entertainment (primarily the large ones immediately surrounding Albuquerque and Santa Fe).","Akken ibɣu yili, qrib akk ikazinuten id-ittwabedren uksawen sɛan tissit, yarna aṭas seg-sen ttawin-d isedhuyen n lmaṛkat tiɛlayanin (s wudem agejdan imeqqranen id-izzin i Abukurk akked Santa Fi)."
Beware: small-town bars here are not always good places for the out-of-state visitor to hang out.,Tamawt : lbaṛat n tudrin timecṭaḥ mačči d amekkan igerzen i tuffɣa i yinerzufen ibaṛṛaniyen.
"For one thing, northern New Mexico has significant problems with drunk driving, and the concentration of intoxicated drivers is high close to small-town bars.","Axaṭeṛ, Miksiku Tamaynut n ugafa tesɛa iɣeblan imeqqranen akked tnehhart n isekṛanen, yerna inehharen isekṛanen qwan tama n lbaṛat n tudrin timecṭaḥ."
Unwanted murals or scribble is known as graffiti.,Unuɣ ɣef leḥyuḍ neɣ tira ur nettwabɣa ara tettwassen s yisem n grafiti.
"While it's far from a modern phenomenon, most people probably associate it with youth vandalizing public and private property using spray paint.","Xas akken mačči d tumant tatrart, amur ameqqran n yemdanen ahat ttwalin-t d asexṛeb n wayla uslig akked uzayaz sɣuṛ yilmeẓyen s usexdem n sbiɣa n tqaṛɛett."
"However, nowadays there are established graffiti artists, graffiti events and ""legal"" walls. Graffiti paintings in this context often resemble artworks rather than illegible tags.","Akken ibɣu yili, tura llan inaẓuren n ugrafiti, tidyanin n ugrafiti akked leḥyuḍ ""uzrifen"". Unuɣen n ugrafiti di lḥalat-agi s umata ttemcabin ɣer lecɣal n tẓuṛi kter n tira ur nettwafham ara."
Boomerang throwing is a popular skill that many tourists want to acquire.,Aḍeggeṛ n ubumṛung d tamusni mucaɛen i bɣan aṭas n iḥewwasen ad sɛun.
"If you want to learn throwing a boomerang that comes back to your hand, make sure you have a suitable boomerang for returning.","Ma tebɣiḍ ad tiḥfiḍeḍ aḍeggeṛ n ubumrung ara ad d-yuɣalen ɣer ufus-ik, twekked belli tesɛiḍ abumrung iwatan i tuɣalin."
Most boomerangs available in Australia are in fact non-returning. It is best for beginners to not try throwing in windy,Amur ameqqran n ibumrungen illan i Ustralya mačči d wid id-ittuɣalen di tidett. Iḥafaḍen ur ilaq ara ad t-ḍeggṛen mi ara yili waḍu
A Hangi Meal is cooked in a hot pit in the ground.,Lmakla n Hangi ittewwa-d di tesraft taḥmayant di lqaɛa.
"The pit is either heated with hot stones from a fire, or in some places geothermal heat makes areas of ground naturally hot.","Tasraft tḥemmu s yeblaḍen tseḥma tmes, neɣ di kra n imukan anda tella lḥamu n ddaw tmurt, lḥamu-agi tseḥmuy imukan di lqaɛa s wudem agaman."
The hangi is often used to cook a traditional roast style dinner.,Asewwi n Hangi s umata ittusexdam i usewwi n imensi n ṣenf ccwa amensay.
"Several places in Rotorua offer geothermal hangi, while other hangi can be sampled in Christchurch, Wellington and elsewhere.","Aṭas n imukan di Ruturwa sɛan asewwi s lḥamu n lqaɛa, ma d lmakla niḍen n hangi tezmer ad tili di Kristčurč, Wilingtun akked wanda niḍen."
MetroRail has two classes on commuter trains in and around Cape Town: MetroPlus (also called First Class) and Metro (called Third Class).,MitruRil tesɛa sin iswiren di tmacinin n daxel akked wayen id-izzin i Kab Tawn: MitruBlus (iwumi qqaren daɣen Aswir Amezwaru) akked Mitru (iwumi qqaren Aswir wis Krad).
"MetroPlus is more comfortable and less crowded but slightly more expensive, though still cheaper than normal metro tickets in Europe.","MitruBlus isɛa astaɛfu akteṛ yarna ur ittaččaṛ ara maca iɣlay ciṭ, xas akken iṛxis kter n itikiyen n umiṭṛu di Uruba."
Every train has both MetroPlus and Metro coaches; the MetroPlus coaches are always on the end of the train nearest Cape Town.,Yal tamacint tesɛa MitruBlus akked Mitru di sin; tikeṛṛusin n MitruBlus zgant ɣer taggara n tmacint iqeṛben ɣer Kab Tawn.
"Carrying for others - Never let your bags out of your sight, especially when you are crossing international borders.","Awway i wiyiḍ - ur ttaǧǧa ara iqeṛban-ik ad fɣen tamuɣli-k, abaɛda mi ara tzegreḍ tilisa tigreɣlanin."
"You could find yourself being used as a drug carrier without your knowledge, which will land you in a great deal of trouble.","Izmer ad d-tafeḍ iman-ik tettwasexdameḍ i wawway n unehyuf mebla ma tfaqeḍ, ayen ara k-d-yawin iɣeblan imeqqranen."
"This includes waiting in line, as drug-sniffing dogs could be used at any time without notice.","Aya-gi iɛna araǧu n nuba di derra, imi izmer ad ttwasxedmen iqejjan ittesriḥin anehyuf mebla aɛeggen."
Some countries have exceedingly draconian punishments even for first time offenses; these can include prison sentences of over 10 years or death.,Kra n tmura sɛant lɛuqubat timeqqranin ula ma xas d tucḍa tamezwarut; gar-asent lɛuqubat n lḥebs n kteṛ n 10 n iseggasen neɣ leḥkem s lmut.
Unattended bags are a target for theft and can also attract attention from authorities wary of bomb threats.,Iqeṛban iqqimen mebla taɛsast sehlen i takerḍa yarna zemren ad d-jebden tamuɣli n imsulta i ttagaden amihi n tfezwayt.
"At home, due to this constant exposure to the local germs, odds are very high that you're already immune to them.","Deg uxxam, imi tezgiḍ twaɛɛaḍ imikruben idiganen, iban belli tesɛiḍ tamḥaddit mgal-nsen."
"But in other parts of the world, where the bacteriological fauna are new to you, you're far more likely to run into problems.","Maca deg imukan niḍen n ddunit, anda ṣenf n imikruben d amaynut ɣuṛ-k, izmer mliḥ ad tesɛuḍ uguren."
"Also, in warmer climates bacteria both grow more quickly and survive longer outside the body.","Yarna, di tegnewt yeḥman imikruben ttimɣuṛen s lemɣawla yarna ttaṭṭafen taṛwiḥt akteṛ baṛṛa n tfekka."
"Thus the scourges of Delhi Belly, the Pharaoh's Curse, Montezuma's Revenge, and their many friends.","Akka ihimeṛ n Delhi Belli, Daɛwessu n Farɛun, Tiririt n Ttaṛ n Muntizuma, akked waṭas n imdukkal-nsen."
"As with respiratory problems in colder climates, intestinal problems in hot climates are fairly common and in most cases are distinctly annoying but not really dangerous.","Am wuguren n uneffes di tegnewt taṣemmaḍt, uguren n iẓeṛman di tegnewt yeḥman mucaɛen yarna sefqaɛen deg umur ameqqran n lḥalat maca mačči d imihawen mliḥ."
If traveling in a developing country for the first time – or in a new part of the world – don't underestimate the potential culture shock.,Ma ad tinigeḍ ɣer tmurt ittnernin i tikkelt tamezwarut - neɣ ɣer uḥric amaynut n umaḍal - ur ḥeqqeṛ ara amgired izemren ad yili deg idles.
"Many a stable, capable traveler has been overcome by the newness of developing world travel, where many little cultural adjustments can add up quickly.","Aṭas n iminigen isɛan laɛqel akked tmusni isewhem-iten usmeynet n umerreḥ di tmura ittnernin, anda xilla n isenfalen imecṭaḥ n idles zemren ad d-ilin s lemɣawla."
"Especially in your initial days, consider splurging on Western-style and -quality hotels, food, and services to help acclimatize.","Abaɛda deg ussan-ik imezwura, xemmem ad txelṣeḍ isensa, lmakla akked imeẓla s waɣan akked tɣaṛa Imaluyen iwakken ad k-yishil lḥal."
Do not sleep on a mattress or pad on the ground in areas where you do not know the local fauna.,Ur ggan ara ɣef wussu neɣ tgertilt ɣef lqaɛa di temnaḍin anda ur tessineḍ ara iɣerṣiwen idiganen.
"If you are going to camp out, bring a camp cot or hammock to keep you away from snakes, scorpions and such.","Ma tebɣiḍ asder di baṛṛa, awi ameṭṛeḥ n baṛṛa neɣ ahamak iwakken ad teǧǧeḍ lehwayec, tiɣirdemiwin irkelli baɛden fell-ak."
Fill your home with a rich coffee in the morning and some relaxing chamomile tea at night.,Aččaṛ axxam-ik s lqahwa tanesbaɣuṛt sbeḥ akked ciṭ n latay n kamumi id-ittawin astaɛfu deg yiḍ.

maybe you'll discover a simple beverage that you can make for breakfast when you're back to your daily routine.,Ahat ad d-tafeḍ tissit isehlen i tzemreḍ ad d-txeddmeḍ i tiremt n sbaḥ mi ara tuɣaleḍ ɣer tudert-ik n yal ass.
"If you live in a city with a varied drinking culture, go to bars or pubs in neighborhoods you don't frequent.","Ma tzedɣeḍ di temdint isɛan idles n tissit yeqwan, ruḥ ɣer lbaṛat neɣ tiḥuna n tissit iqaṛben wuɣuṛ ur tettṛuḥuḍ ara."
"For those unfamiliar with medical jargon, the words infectious and contagious have distinct meanings.","Wid ur nwulef ara imeslayen n tujjya, awalen ittenfufud akked ittanṭaḍ mxalafen di lmaɛna."
"An infectious disease is one that is caused by a pathogen, such as a virus, bacterium, fungus or other parasites.","Aṭṭan ittenfufuden d win ixeddem imsehlek, am unfafad, tabaktiritt, tagerselt neɣ ijenṭiḍen niḍen."
A contagious disease is a disease which is easily transmitted by being in the vicinity of an infected person.,Aṭṭan ittanṭaḍen d lehlak ittanṭaḍen s tashuli mi ara tiliḍ tama n win ihelken.
"Many governments require visitors entering, or residents leaving, their countries to be vaccinated for a range of diseases.","Aṭas n inabaḍen suturen i yinerzufen ara ikecmen, neɣ imezdaɣ ara iffɣen, timura-nsen ad caṛḍen ɣef aṭas n lehlakat."
These requirements may often depend on what countries a traveller has visited or intends to visit.,Cuṛuṭ-agi zemren ad beddlen aɛlaḥsab n tmura wuɣuṛ yarza uminig neɣ wuɣuṛ yebɣa ad yerzu.
"One of strong points of Charlotte, North Carolina, is that it has an abundance of high-quality options for families.","Yiwen seg wagazen n tezmert n Čarlut, Karulina n Ugafa, d akken teččuṛ d tifranin n tɣaṛa εlayen i twaculin."
"Residents from other areas often cite family-friendliness as a primary reason for moving there, and visitors often find the city easy to enjoy with children around.","Imezdaɣ seg temnaḍin niḍen zgan ttaddren-d tifranin i twaculin d tamentilt tagejdant i unezduɣ dagi, yerna imerrayen zgan qqaren-d d akken yeshel zhu akked dderya di temdint."
"In the past 20 years, the amount of child-friendly options in Uptown Charlotte has grown exponentially.","20 n yiseggasen ɣer deffir, yerna wazal n tefranin i twaculin deg yegmamen ihuskayen n Čarlut s wudem yessewhamen."
"Taxis are not generally used by families in Charlotte, though they can be of some use in certain circumstances.","Ur ssexdament ara twaculin iṭaksiyen di Čarlut, ɣas akken zemren ad ilin d infa di kra n tegnatin."
"There is a surcharge for having more than 2 passengers, so this option might be more expensive than necessary.","Tella tmerna di tẓeṭṭaṭ ma yella llan ugar n 2 n yimessukal, ihi tafrant-agi tezmer ad tili ɣlayet ugar ɣef wayen ilaqen."
"Antarctica is the coldest place on Earth, and surrounds the South Pole.","Tanṭarktit d adeg asemmaḍ akk deg Umaḍal, yerna tezzi-d i Tezgelt n Wenẓul."
"Tourist visits are costly, demand physical fitness, can only take place in summer Nov-Feb, and are largely limited to the Peninsula, Islands and Ross Sea.","Tirziwin n yimerrayen ɣlayent, ssuturent-d tazmert taɣaṛant, ttilint-d kan deg unebdu n Wambeṛ-Furar, yerna gen tilisa ɣer Tazunegzirt, Tigzirin d Yilel Russ."
A couple of thousand staff live here in summer in some four dozen bases mostly in those areas; a small number stay over winter.,Kra n wagim n yixeddamen ttidiren dagi deg unebdu deg di kra n ukkuẓ n teẓẓinat n yezdaren s tuget deg yemḍiqen-nni; uṭṭun amecṭuḥ kan seg-sen i yettɣimin di tegrest.
Inland Antarctica is a desolate plateau covered by 2-3 km of ice.,TanṭarktitTagensit d agni ilem i yettwaɣummen s 2-3 n yikilumitren n ugris.
"Occasional specialist air tours go inland, for mountaineering or to reach the Pole, which has a large base.","Ttilint-d tikkwal tirziwin tignawiyin timeẓlayin yettruḥun ɣer daxel n tmurt, i wakken ad alin ɣef yidurar neɣ i wakken ad awḍen ɣer Tezgelt, yesεan azadur ameqqran."
The South Pole Traverse (or Highway) is a 1600 km trail from McMurdo Station on the Ross Sea to the Pole.,Abrid n Tezgelt n Unẓul (neɣ Abrid Arurad) d amecwaṛ n 1600 km si Teɣsert MakMurdu deg Yilel Russ ɣer Tezgelt.
"It's compacted snow with crevasses filled in and marked by flags. It can only be traveled by specialized tractors, hauling sleds with fuel and supplies.","D adfel yettwaskussmen s yimerǧan yeččuren s udfel ceṛḍen s wanayen. D itrakturen imuzzigen, irefden izzuɣṛen s tumast d dduzan."
These aren't very nimble so the trail has to take a long swerve around the Transantarctic Mountains to come onto the plateau.,Wigi ur llin d iruraden mliḥ dimi ad ibeddel tanila ɣezzifen n ubrid yezzin i Yidurar Transantarktik i wakken ad leḥqen ɣer ugni.
"The most common cause for accidents in winter is slippery roads, pavements (sidewalks) and especially steps.","Ssebba tamagnut akk n twaɣiyin deg tegrest d iberdan yettecgen, tineddiyin (itṛutwaṛen) yerna ladɣa tirkabin."
"At a minimum, you need footwear with suitable soles. Summer shoes are usually very slippery on ice and snow, even some winter boots are deficient.","Ma ulac maḍi, teḥwaǧeḍ isebbaḍen s temlixin iwulmen. Isebbaḍen n unebdu zgan ttecgen mliḥ ɣef ugris d udfel, ula d kra n isebbaḍen n tegrest ur mεinen ara."
"The pattern should be deep enough, 5 mm (1/5 inch) or more, and the material soft enough in cold temperatures.","Tamlixt ilaq ad tili d talqayant ddeqs-is, 5 mm (1/5 n yinčen) neɣ ugar, yerna arrum ilaq ad yili d aleggaɣ ddeqs-is di teẓɣal tiṣemmaḍin."
"Some boots have studs and there is studded add-on equipment for slippery conditions, suitable for most shoes and boots, for the heels or heels and sole.","Kra n yisebbaḍen n tegrest ilaq ad sεun imesmaṛen yerna yella warrum n tmerna ttsemmiṛen i tegnatin n tuccga, iwulmen i tuget n yisebbaḍen d isebbaḍen n tegrest, i yigerzan neɣ i yigerzan d temlixin."
"Heels should be low and wide. Sand, gravel or salt (calcium chloride) is often scattered on roads or paths to improve traction.","Ilaq ad ilin igerzan qerben ɣer tmurt yerna d ihrawanen. Amlal, agraraj neɣ tisent (akalsyum klurid) zgan llan ferqen deg ubrid neɣ tneddiyin i wakken ad sneflin tiddi."
"Avalanches are not an abnormality; steep slopes can hold only so much slow, and the excess volumes will come down as avalanches.","Adfel i d-yettegririben seg yidurar ur yelli d waramagnu; tikessarin yettecgen zemrent kan ad ṭṭfent ciṭ n umurḍes, yerna taččart n waṭas ad ɣlin d agrireb."
"The problem is that snow is sticky, so it needs some triggering to come down, and some snow coming down can be the triggering event for the rest.","Aɣbel yella d akken adfel yettmanṭaḍ, dimi akka yeḥwaǧ ciṭ n usenqer i wakken ad yegrireb, ma d ciṭ n udfel i d-yettegririben yezmer ad yili d aneḍru n usenqer i wayen niḍen."
"Sometimes the original trigging event is the sun warming the snow, sometimes some more snowfall, sometimes other natural events, often a human.","Tikkwal aneḍru n usenqer amenzu d iṭij yesseḥman adfel, tikkwal d kra n udfel i d-iɣellin igar, tikkwal d ineḍruyen igamayen niḍen, tikkwal d amdan."
"A tornado is a spinning column of very low-pressure air, which sucks the surrounding air inward and upward.","Tinifift d afeggag yettezzin n uzbu n waddad ineqsen, yettsummun azbu is-d-yezzin ɣer daxel akked ɣer d asawen."
"They generate high winds (often 100-200 miles/hour) and can lift heavy objects into the air, carrying them as the tornado moves.","Xellqen-d aḍu iǧehden (tikkwal 100-200 n yimaylen i usrag) yerna zemren ad refden tiɣawsiwin yeẓẓayen daxel n uzbu, ttawin-tent simmal tetteddu tnifift."
"They begin as funnels descending from storm clouds, and become ""tornadoes"" when they touch the ground.","Beddunt-d d inififen i d-iṣubben seg usigna n uzayaḍ, dɣa uɣalent d ""tinififiyin"" mi ttnalent tamurt."
Personal VPN (virtual private network) providers are an excellent way of circumventing both political censorship and commercial IP-geofiltering.,Iseɣzanen n AUU (aẓeṭṭa uhlis uslig) udmawan d tamamekt ifazen i wakken ad tsizedweḍ tadrest tasertit d umsizdeg-IB asenzan.
"They are superior to web proxies for several reasons: They re-route all Internet traffic, not only http.","D iminag ɣef iseɣzanen web s waṭas n tmental: Ttbeddilen abrid i yak tasnisnit Internet, mačči siwa httb."
They normally offer higher bandwidth and better quality of service. They are encrypted and thus harder to spy on.,Sεan s wudem anamay tamuli εlayen s tɣara n umeẓlu tamawayt. Ttwasneglen dɣa yewεer ugar ad sɣallayen fell-asen.
"The media companies routinely lie about the purpose of this, claiming that it is to ""prevent piracy"".","Tikebbaniyin n usneɣmes zgant skiddibent ɣef yiswi n waya, imi qqaren-d d akken yella-d i wakken ad ""qeḍeεen tudert tabaḍnit""."
"In fact, region codes have absolutely no effect on illegal copying; a bit-for-bit copy of a disk will play just fine on any device where the original will.","Di tilawt, ingalen n temnaḍin ur sεin ara akk asemdu ɣef tenɣelt taruzrift; tanɣelt n telɣut-s-telɣut n uḍebsi ad telḥu akken iwata deg yal tamacint anda ad ilḥu uẓaṛan."
The actual purpose is to give those companies more control over their markets; it's all about money spinning.,"Iswi n tidet d asiǧhed n tkebbaniyin-agi, ad sεunt ugar n tezmert ɣef wulzuzen-nsen; d tuzzya kan n yidrimen."
"Because calls are routed over the Internet, you do not need to use a phone company located where you live or where you travel.","Imi leḥḥun isawalen deg Internet, ur teḥwaǧeḍ ara ad tesxedmeḍ takebbanit n tiliɣṛi i d-yezgan anda tzedɣeḍ neɣ sani tettinigeḍ."
"There is also no requirement that you obtain a local number from the community in which you live; you can obtain a satellite Internet connection in the wilds of Chicken, Alaska and select a number which claims you're in sunny Arizona.","Ur d-ssuturen ara daɣen ad tesεuḍ uṭṭun adigan seg tmazdayt anda tzedɣeḍ; tzemreḍ ad tesεuḍ tuqqna Internet n ugensa deg tẓegwa n Uyaẓiḍ, Alaska yerna ad tferneḍ uṭṭun i d-yesbanayen d akken telliḍ ddaw n yiṭij n Arizuna."
"Often, you have to buy a global number separately that allows PSTN phones to call you. Where the number is from makes a difference for people calling you.","Tikkwal, ilaq ad taɣeḍ uṭṭun agraɣlan weḥdes yettaǧǧan tiliɣṛa Lweqt Ilaw n Ubrutukul Uɛassi i wakken ad ak-d-ssiwlen. Tella-d tmeẓla seg ansi yella wuṭṭun i yimdanen i ak-d-yessawalen."
Real-time text translator apps – applications that are capable of automatically translating whole segments of text from one language into another.,Isnasen n umsuɣel anbabbar n uḍris - isnasen izemren ad ssuɣlen s wudem awurman iḥricen ummiden n uḍris seg tutlayt ɣer tayeḍ.
Some of the applications in this category can even translate texts in foreign languages on signs or other objects in the real world when the user points the smartphone towards those objects.,Kra seg yesnasen deg taggayt-agi zemren ad ssuɣlen ula d iḍrisen deg tutlayin tibeṛṛaniyin ɣef yesɣilen neɣ tiɣawsiwin niḍen deg tilawt mi ara d-yessewεed usemras tiliɣṛi ɣer tɣawsiwin-nni.
"The translation engines have improved dramatically, and now often give more or less correct translations (and more seldom gibberish), but some care is due, as they still may have gotten it all wrong.","Iseɣzanen n usuɣel selhan nezzeh, yerna tura ttaken-d tikkwal tisuɣilin iṣeḥḥan akka ciṭ (drus mliḥ usexleḍ ur nettwafham), maca ilaq leḥder, imi mazal-iten zemren ad tt-rwin akk."
"One of the most prominent apps in this category is Google Translate, which allows offline translation after downloading the desired language data.","Yiwen seg yesnasen ixataren akk deg taggayt-agi d Asuɣel Gugle, yettaǧǧan asuɣel beṛṛa n tuqqna seld assider n usefku n tutlayt i k-yehwan."
Using GPS navigation apps on your smartphone can be the easiest and most convenient way to navigate when out of your home country.,Asexdem n yesnasen n ussilel GBS deg ufafus-ik amegzu d tamamekt isehlen akk d tin iwulmen akk i ussilel mi ra tiliḍ beṛṛa n tmurt-ik n tlalit.
"It can save money over buying new maps for a GPS, or a standalone GPS device or renting one from a car rental company.","Yezmer ad yejmeε idrimen s tiɣin n tkarḍiwin timaynutin i GBS, neɣ tamacint timanit GBS neɣ lekra n yiwen seg tkebbanit n lekra n tkeryas."
"If you don't have a data connection for your phone, or when it is out of range, their performance can be limited or unavailable.","Ma yella ur tesεiḍ ara tuqqna n yisefka i tiluɣṛi-inek, neɣ mi ur tzemmreḍ ara ad teṭṭfeḍ, aselḥu-nsen yezmer ad yesεu tilas neɣ ur yettili ara."
Every corner store is filled with a confusing array of pre-paid phone cards that can be used from pay phones or ordinary telephones.,Yal taḥanut n usellek teččur d tifelwiyin yessewhamen n tkarḍiwin n tiliɣṛi yettwaxellaṣen uqbel i tzemreḍ ad tesxedmeḍ si tiliɣṛi azayez neɣ tiliɣri umṛis.
"While most cards are good for calling anywhere, some specialise in providing favourable call rates to specific groups of countries.","Imi tuget n tkarḍin lhant i usiwel anda id ak-yehwa, kra muzzgen deg tikci n yifmiḍiyen imeεnen n ussiwel i yigrawen usdiden n tmura."
Access to these services is often through a toll-free telephone number that can be called from most phones without charge.,Anekcum ɣer yimeẓla-agi yezga yella seg uṭṭun n tiliɣṛi war idrimen uɣur tzemreḍ ad tessiwleḍ seg tuget n tiliɣṛa mebla axelleṣ.
"Rules regarding regular photography also apply to video recording, possibly even more so.","Ilugan yeεnan aṣewwer umṛis εnan ula asurret n ufidyu, ahat ugar n waya."
"If just taking a photo of something isn't allowed, then you shouldn't even think of recording a video of it.","Ma yella yettugdel ad teṭṭfeḍ tawlaft n tɣawsa, ihi ur k-ilaq ara ula d axemmem ɣef usurret n ufidyu fell-as."
"If using a drone, check well in advance as to what you are allowed to film and what permits or additional licensing are required.","Ma yella tessxedmeḍ adrun, selken mliḥ di tazwara d acu i tzemreḍ ad tessurteḍ akked wacu n ttesriḥat neɣ turagin n tmerna i d-ssutren."
"Flying a drone near an airport or over a crowd is almost always a bad idea, even if it's not illegal in your area.","Affug n udrun zdat n unafag neɣ nnig n lɣaci d tikti n diri s wudem qrib amezgi, ɣas akken ur yelli d aruzrif deg tmurt-ik."
Nowadays air travel is only rarely booked directly through the airline without first searching and comparing prices.,Ass am ass-a inig deg igenni drus maḍi ad yettwaḥeṛ srid si tkebbanit n isufag mebla ma yella-d unadi d userwes di tazwara n sswami.
Sometimes the same flight can have vastly differing prices at various agregators and it pays to compare search results and to also look at the website of the airline itself before booking.,Tikkwal yiwen n wafug yezmer ad yesεu sswami yemgaraden mliḥ ɣer waṭas n yismal yerna ilaq ad txellseḍ aserwes igemmaḍen n unadi akked uwali deg yismal web n tkebbanit n isufag s timmad-is send aḥeṛṛi.
"While you may not need a visa for short visits to certain countries as a tourist or for business, going there as an international student generally requires a longer stay than going there just as a casual tourist.","Γas akken ur tetteḥwiǧiḍ ara afiza i uḥewwes wezzilen ɣer kra n tmura d amerray neɣ i uxeddim, ma yella truḥeḍ d anelmad agraɣlan ad ak-d-ssutren s umata akud n yiɣimi ɣezzifen ɣef ma yella truḥeḍ d amerray kan umṛis."
"In general, staying in any foreign country for an extended period of time will require you to obtain a visa in advance.","S umata, iɣimi deg tmurt tabeṛṛanit i tallit n wakud ɣezzifen yessuter ad tawiḍ afiza uqbel."
Student visas generally have different requirements and application procedures from normal tourist or business visas.,Ifizaten n yinelmaden tikalayin-nsent n usuter d ujerred mgaradent s wudem amatu ɣef tid n yifisaten n umarray umṛis neɣ n uxeddim.
"For most countries, you will need an offer letter from the institution you wish to study at, and also evidence of funds to support yourself for at least the first year of your course.","Deg tuget n tmura, ad teḥwiǧeḍ tabṛat n ucekker seg tsudut anda tebɣiḍ ad tlemdeḍ, akked daɣen ttbut n yedrimen i wakken ad trefdeḍ iman-ik meqqar aseggas amenzu n ulmad-ik."
"Check with the institution, as well as the immigration department for the country you wish to study in for detailed requirements.","Wali akked tsudut, akked ugezdu n yinig ɣef tmurt anda tebɣiḍ ad tlemdeḍ i ugar n yissallen."
"Unless you are a diplomat, working overseas generally means that you will have to file income tax in the country you are based in.","Siwa ma telliḍ d adiblumaṭ, iqeddcen akkin i yilel ilaq-ak ad tesserseḍ acḥal n yidrimen i tettaɣeḍ deg tmurt anda i tzedɣeḍ."
"Income tax is structured differently in different countries, and the tax rates and brackets vary widely from one country to another.","Taẓeṭṭaṭ n yedrimen i tettaɣeḍ tebna s umgarad deg tmura yemgaraden, yerna ifmiḍiyen d wazalen n tẓeṭṭaṭ d anḍiyen mliḥ si tmurt ɣer tayeḍ."
"In some federal countries, such as the United States and Canada, income tax is levied both at the federal level and at the local level, so the rates and brackets can vary from region to region.","Di kra n tmura tifidiraliyin, am Yiwunak Yedduklen d Kanada, taẓeṭṭaṭ n yidrimen i tettaɣeḍ tettili-d ɣer uswir afidirali d uswir adigan di sin, ihi ifmiḍen d wazalen d anḍiyen si tama ɣer tayeḍ."
"While immigration check is usually absent or a formality when you arrive in your homeland, customs control can be a hassle.","Γas akken asefqed n yinig yezga iɣab neɣ yettili-d kan d lwajeb mi ad tawḍeḍ ɣer tmurt-ik, yezmer ad yili usefqed n tdawna d asawen."
Make sure you know what you can and cannot bring in and declare anything over the legal limits.,Tḥeq d akken teẓriḍ acu tzemreḍ d wacu ur tezmireḍ ara ad tawiḍ yerna mel-d kullec deg tilisa tuzrifin.
The easiest way to get started in the business of travel writing is to hone your skills on an established travel blog website.,Tamamekt isehlen akk i wakken ad tebduḍ deg leqdic n tira n yinig d asemsed n twezza-ik deg usmel web n tira n yinig ibedden.
"After you become comfortable with formatting and editing on the web, then later, you might create your own website.","Seld mi ara tissineḍ ad tsegmeḍ asebter yerna ad tjerdeḍ ɣef usmel, imir sakkin, tzemreḍ ad tesnulfuḍ asmel-ik web i yiman-ik."
Volunteering while travelling is a great way to make a difference but it's not just about giving.,Tiwizi deg yinig d tamamekt igerrzen i wakken ad teǧǧeḍ amgired maca ur d-yelli ɣef tikci kan.
"Living and volunteering in a foreign country is a great way to get to know a different culture, meet new people, learn about yourself, get a sense of perspective and even gain new skills.","Tudert d tiwizi deg tmurt tabeṛṛanit d tamamekt igerrzen i wakken ad tissineḍ adles yemgaraden, ad temlileḍ imdanen imaynuten, ad tlemdeḍ kra ɣef yiman-ik, ad tkesbeḍ tamuɣli niḍen yerna ad trebḥeḍ ula d tiwezza timaynutin."
It can also be a good way to stretch a budget to allow a longer stay somewhere since many volunteer jobs provide room and board and a few pay a small salary.,Tezmer ad tili daɣen d tamamekt yelhan i wakken ad tjemεeḍ ugar n yidrimen i wakken ad teqqimeḍ akud ɣezzifen anda tufiḍ imi aṭas n leqdicat n yiwaziwen ttaken taxxamt d wučči yerna kra ttxelliṣen ciṭ.
"Vikings used the Russian waterways to get to the Black Sea and Caspian Sea. Parts of these routes can still be used. Check possible need for special permits, which may be difficult to get.","Ifikingen llan ttaṭṭafen iberdan n ussilel Irussiyen i wakken ad awḍen ɣer Yilel Aberkan akked Yilel Akasbyan. Mazal zemren yemdanen ad awin iḥricen n yiberdan-agi. Walit acu n ttesriḥat imeẓliyen i tzemrem ad tiḥwiǧem, iweεren i wakken ahat ad ten-id-awiḍ."
"The White Sea–Baltic Canal connects the Arctic Ocean to the Baltic Sea, via Lake Onega, Lake Ladoga and Saint Petersburg, mostly by rivers and lakes.","Abrid Abalti n Yilel Amellal yeqqen Ilel Arktik ɣer Yilel Abalti, seg Ugelmim Unega, Agelmim Laduga d Saint Betersburg, s tuget seg isafen d yigelmimen."
"Lake Onega is also connected to Volga, so coming from the Caspian Sea through Russia is still possible.","Agelmim Unega yeqqen daɣen ɣer Fulga, ihi mazal tezmer ad tili tissin seg Yilel Akasbyan si Rrus."
Be assured that once you hit the marinas everything will be pretty obvious. You will meet other boat hitchhikers and they will share their information with you.,Ur ttagadet mi ara ad tawḍem ɣer tegriwa kullec ad awen-d-iban. Ad temlilem imseḥbas n yiɣeṛṛuba dɣa ad ferqen isallen-nsen yid-wen.
"Basically you'll be putting up notices offering your help, pacing the docks, approaching people cleaning their yachts, trying to make contact with sailors in the bar, etc.","S wudem anamay ad tesserseḍ ulɣu d akken tebɣiḍ ad tεiwneḍ, ad tnadiḍ akk ignennayen, ad tqerbeḍ ɣer yemdanen yessizdigen iɣeṛṛuba-nsen, ad tεerḍeḍ ad temmeslayeḍ akked yemsilal di ttberna, atg."
