"When a small group of living things (a small population) gets separated from the main population that they came from (like if they move over a mountain range or a river, or if they move to a new island so that they can't easily move back) they will often find themselves in a different environment than they were in before.","Mi akken agraw amecṭuḥ n imudar (kra imezdaɣ) tebḍa ɣef ugdud i deg d-tekka (am wakken zegren idurar neɣ assif, neɣ ruḥen ɣer tegzirt niḍen anda ur zmiren ara ad uɣalen ɣer deffir ), ad afen iman-nsen deg yiwet n twennaṭ yemgaraden ɣef tin i deg llan uqbel."
"This new environment has different resources and different competitors, so the new population will need different features or adaptations to be a strong competitor than what they had needed before.","Tawennaṭ-agi tamaynut tesɛa tiɣbula yemgaraden d yenmezgiyen yemgaraden, ɣef waya imezdaɣ iruḥen ad iḥwiǧin timahilin niḍen neɣ awalef niḍen i wakken ad ilin d inmezgiyen iǧehden s wassaɣ ɣer wayen ḥwajen zik."
"The original population hasn't changed at all, they still need the same adaptations as before.","Agdud-nsen anaṣli ur yettbeddil ara maḍi, mazal d awalem ḥwaǧen zik ara iḥiǧen tura."
"Over time, as the new population begins to adapt to their new environment, they start to look less and less like the other population.","Simmal ad Ittɛeddi wakud, simal imezdaɣ iruḥen ttwalafen tawennaṭ-nsen tamaynut simal ttuɣalen ur ttaken ara acbi ɣer ugdud-nsen anaṣli."
"Eventually, after thousands or even millions of years, the two populations will look so different that they can't be called the same species.","Di taggara, deffir igiman neɣ ahat imelyan n iseggasen , imezdaɣ iruḥen d wegdud-nsen anaṣli ad uɣalen mgaraden arma ur nettizmir ara ad nini fell-asen yiwet n ccetla."
"We call this process speciation, which just means the formation of new species. Speciation is an unavoidable consequence and a very important part of evolution.","Nessawal i ukala-agi anelmes, i yesɛan anamek asileɣ n telmas timaynutin. Anelmes d talkamt i ɣef ulac awexxer wa d aḥric s wazal-is di n temhazt."
"Plants make oxygen which humans breathe, and they take in carbon-dioxide which humans exhale (that is, breathe out).",Imɣan ttaken-d luksijin i yesnufus umdan wa ttjbident diyuksid karbun i d-suffuɣen yemdanen (d wagi mi ara d-rren nnefs)
Plants make their food from the sun by photosynthesis. They also provide shade.,"Imɣan xedmen učči-nsen s yiṭij, s ubdey n sḥed n tafat ɣer uferdis agmanan. Ttaken-d daɣen tili."
"We make our houses from plants and make clothes from plants. Most foods that we eat are plants. Without plants, animals could not survive.","Nbennu ixxamen-nneɣ s wa nettṣeniɛ iceṭṭiḍen-nneɣ s yemɣan. Aḥric ameqqran n učči-nneɣ itekk-d seg yemɣan. Ma ulac imɣan, iɣersiwen ur zmiren ara ad idiren."
"Mosasaurus was the apex predator of its time, so it feared nothing, except other mosasaurs.","Amuzasurus illa d lweḥc ameqqṛan di tallit-is, ulac acu ittaggad, ḥala imuzasuren-nniḍen."
"Its long jaws were studded with more than 70 razor-sharp teeth, along with an extra set in the roof of its mouth, meaning that there was no escape for anything that crossed its path.","Iɣesmaren-is iɣezfanen sɛan ugar n 70 n tuɣmas qeṭṭiɛen mliḥ, akked tṛemmuɛt-nniḍen n zyada deg ssqef n uqemmuc-is, lmeɛna-s ulac tarewla i wayen ara d-yaff deg webrid-is."
"We don't know for sure, but it may have had a forked tongue. Its diet included turtles, large fish, other mosasaurs, and it may even have been a cannibal.","Ur neẓṛi ara, maca ahat illa isɛa iles ibḍan ɣef sin. Lmakla-s deg-s ifekrunen, iselman imeqqranen, imuzasuren-nniḍen, yerna ahat yella d ameččemdan."
It also attacked anything that entered the water; even a giant dinosaur such as T. rex would be no match for it.,Ikkat daɣen ɣef yal taɣawsa ikeččmen s aman ; ula d adinuṣur ameqqṛan am T. Raks ur s-izmir ara.
"While most of their food would be familiar to us, Romans did have their share of strange or unusual feast items, including wild boar, peacock, snails, and a type of rodent called a dormouse","Γas akken tuget n wučči-nsen yettemcabi ɣer winna-nneɣ, Ṛuman sεan amur-nsen n yiferdisen n wučči yessewhamen d warunnimen, am yilef aweḥci, afrux n ṭawes, iεuṛas, d wanaw n temseɣẓaẓ i wumi qqaren iɣerdayen lwar"
"Another difference was that while the poor people and the woman ate their food while sitting in chairs, the rich men liked to have banquets together where they would lounge on their sides while they ate their meals.","Amgired niḍen yellan d akken mi tetten imdanen igellilen d tmeṭṭut učči-nsen s yiɣimi ɣef tesɣimin, irgazen inesbuɣar ḥemmlen ad asεun idrawen akken anda ad qnajjṛen ɣer tamiwin-nsen mi tetten tiram-nsen."
Ancient Roman meals couldn't have included foods that came to Europe from America or from Asia in later centuries.,Tiram n Ṛuman Iqburen ur sseddant ara učči d-yewwḍen ɣer Tuṛuft si Marikan neɣ si Asya deg tisutin tineggura.
"For instance, they didn't have corn, nor tomatoes, nor potatoes, nor cocoa, and no ancient Roman ever tasted a turkey.","D amedya, ur sεin ara akbal, neɣ ṭumaṭic, neɣ lbaṭaṭa, neɣ lkakau, yerna ur yelli Aṛumi aqbur iεerḍen adandu."
The Babylonians built each of their gods a primary temple that was considered the home of the god.,Ibabilyunen bnan i yal illu-nsen afakan amenzu iḥesben d axxam i yillu-nni.
People would bring sacrifices to the gods and the priests would try to attend to the needs of the gods through ceremonies and festivals.,Imdanen ttawin-d tiɣeṛsawin i yilluyen dɣa ibabaṣen εeṛṛḍen ad asen-fken ayen bɣan i yilluyen s tfulga d tfaskiwin.
Each temple had an open temple courtyard and then an inner sanctuary that only the priests could enter.,Yal afakan yesεa abṛaḥ n ufakan yeldin akked wadeg uɣṛis ḥala ibabaṣen izemren ad t-ikecmen.
"Sometimes special pyramid shaped towers, called ziggurats, were built to be a part of the temples.","Tikkwal tineḍḍafin timeẓliyin igan am tzumag, isem-nsent ziggurat, bnan-tent d aḥric n yifukan."
The top of the tower was special sanctuary for the god.,Taqacuct n tneḍḍaft d adeg uɣṛis imeẓli i yulli.
"In the warm climate of the Middle East, the house was not so important.","Deg unezwi yeḥman n Usamar Alemmas, axxam ur yelli d axaṭar."
Most of the life of the Hebrew family happened in the open air.,Tuget n tudert n twacult Tudayt tella-d di beṛṛa i yiṭij.
Women did the cooking in the yard; stores were just open counters looking into the street. Stone was used for building houses.,Tilawin sewwayent deg ubṛaḥ; tiḥuna d ṭṭwabel ifetḥen ɣef ubrid. Iẓra ssxedmen-ten di lebni n yexxamen.
"There were no large forests in the land of Canaan, so wood was extremely expensive.","Ur llint ara tẓegwa imeqqren di tmurt n Kanaan, dimi akka yeɣlay uṣɣaṛ mačči d izli."
"Greenland was settled sparsely. "If you have watched the movie National Treasure, you may think a treasure map was written on the back of the Declaration of Independence.","Ma yella tferǧeḍ asaru Agerruj Aɣelnaw, tzemreḍ ad tɣileḍ d akken takarḍa n ugerruj tettwajerred ɣer deffir n Tseɣṛut n Timunent."
"However, that is not true. Although there is something written on the back of the document, it is not a treasure map.","Maca, ur telli d tidett. Γas akken tella tɣawsa yettwajerden ɣer deffir n warrat, ur telli d takarḍa n ugerruj."
"Written on the back of the Declaration of Independence were the words ""Original Declaration of Independence dated 4th July 1776"". The text appears on the bottom of the document, upside down.","Ayen yuran ɣer deffir n Tseɣṛut n Timunent d awalen ""Taseɣṛut n Timunent tagejdant n wazemz 4 di Yulyu 1776"". Aḍris iban-d ddaw n urrat, yetti."
"While no one knows for certain who wrote it, it is known that early in its life, the large parchment document (it measures 29¾ inches by 24½ inches) was rolled up for storage.","Γas akken ur yelli win yetḥeqqen deg win i t-ijerrden, yettwassen d akken zik di tudert-is, arrat-nni tidsi ahrawan (yesket 29¾ n yinchen ɣef 24½ n yinchen) yerna yenneḍ i wakken ad yettwajmeε."
"So, it is likely that the notation was added simply as a label.","Ihi, yezmer lḥal tuggza-nni rnan-tt-id kan d tabzimt."
"The D-Day landings and the following battles had freed the north of France, but the south still wasn't free.","Azḍam n Wass-Nni d imennuɣen i d-yernan wwin-d tilelli i ugafa n Franṣa, maca anẓul urεad yelli d ilelli."
"It was ruled by the ""Vichy"" French. These were French people who had made peace with the Germans in 1940 and worked with the invaders instead of fighting them.","Ḥekmen-t Iṛumyen ""Fici"". "A civilization is a singular culture shared by a significant large group of people who live and work co-operatively, a society.","Taɣeṛma d adles asuf i yecrek ugraw n waṭas n yemdanen yettidiren yerna iqeddcen akken, timetti."
"The word civilization comes from the Latin civilis, meaning civil, related to the Latin civis, meaning citizen, and civitas, meaning city or city-state, and that also somehow defines the size of the society.","Awal taɣeṛma yekka-d si Tlatint cibilis, anamek-is aɣaṛim, yeqqnen ɣer Ulatini cibis, anamek-is aɣeṛman, d cibitas, anamek-is tiɣṛemt neɣ aɣaṛam, yerna aya isemmel s tmamekt azal n tmetti."
"City-states are the precursors of nations. A civilizational culture implies the passing on of knowledge across several generations, a lingering cultural footprint and fair dissemination.","Iɣuṛam d lejdud n yeɣlanen. Adles n tɣeṛma anamek-is asεeddi n tmussni seg tsuta ɣer tayeḍ, d later adelsan ad idummen yerna d asnezwi iεedlen."
Minor cultures often vanish without leaving relevant historic evidence and fail to be recognized as proper civilizations.,Idelsan imecṭaḥ zgan neggren mebla ma ǧǧan-d ttbut amazray ibanen dɣa ur ṣawaḍen ara ad ten-ḥesben d tiɣeṛmiwin n tidet.
"During the Revolutionary War, the thirteen states first formed a weak central government—with the Congress being its only component—under the Articles of Confederation.","Deg Trad Agrawlan, iwunak di mraw d kraḍ yid-sen ssilɣen anabaḍ alemmas anamum - akked Useqqamu i yellan d aferdis-is aywan- ɣef leḥsab n Yimagraden n Umqun."
"Congress lacked any power to impose taxes, and, because there was no national executive or judiciary, it relied on state authorities, who were often uncooperative, to enforce all its acts.","Aseqqamu txuṣ-it tezmert i wakken ad iqelled tiẓeṭṭaḍin, yerna, acku ur llint tnabaḍin tiselkamin neɣ tiɣedmanin tiɣelnawin, yebna ɣef tnabaḍin n uwanek, i yettagin ad εiwnent, i wakken ad sḥersent akk arraten-is."
It also had no authority to override tax laws and tariffs between states.,Ur yesεi ara ula d tissas i wakken ad isεeddi isuḍaf iẓeṭṭanen d tedrimt gar iwunak.
The Articles required unanimous consent from all the states before they could be amended and states took the central government so lightly that their representatives were often absent.,Imagraden ḥwaǧen aqbal anemzal sɣur akk iwunak uqbel ad izmiren ad tzn-beddlen yerna iwunak-nni ur ḥsiben ara anabaḍ alemmas dimi akka imgensasen zgan ulac-iten.

"Winter sports are most popular in the Northern regions, with Italians competing in international games and Olympic events.","Addalen n tegrest mechuren ugar di temnaḍin n Ugafa, akked timenyugert gar Iṭelyanen deg wuraren igraɣlanen d yineḍruyen Ulimbik."
"Japans holds nearly 7,000 islands (the biggest being Honshu), making Japan the 7th largest island in the world!","Jabu yeṭṭef tamudi n 7,000 n tegzirin (tameqqrant akk d Huncu), d ayen i yerran Jabu d tigzirt tis 7 imeqqren akk deg umaḍal!"
"Due to the cluster/group of islands Japan has, Japan is often referred to, on a geographical stance, as an ""archipelago""","Γef tmazdayt/ugraw n tegzirin i tesεa Jabu, Jabu zgan qqaren-as, s wudem arakalan, d ""agraw n tegzirin"""
"Taiwan beginning start way back in 15th century where European sailors passing by record the island’s name as Ilha Formosa, or beautiful island.","Tazwara n Taywan yella-d deg tasut tis 15 anda sεeddayen yemsilal Urufiyen si wa ɣer wa isem n tegzirt d Ilha Furmusa, neɣ tigzirt tahuskant."
"In 1624,Dutch East India Company establishes a base in southwestern Taiwan, initiating a transformation in aboriginal grain production practices and employing Chinese laborers to work on its rice and sugar plantations.","Di 1624, Takebbanit Tahullundit n Lhend Tasamrant tesbedd azadur deg unẓul amalu n Taywan, d ayen yebdan abeddel deg tamamkin n ufares n yimendi usrew d usexdem n yifellaḥen Icinwaten ad ixedmen deg urtiyen-is n ṛṛuz d skeṛ."
"In 1683, Qing dynasty (1644-1912) forces take control of Taiwan’s western and northern coastal areas and declared Taiwan as a province of the Qing Empire in 1885.","Di 1683, iɣallen n twacult tageldant Kwing (1644-1912) ḥekmen tamiwin taftisin n umalu d ugafa n Taywan yerna rran Taywan d Tmenkda Kwing di 1885."
"In 1895, after defeat in the First Sino-Japanese War (1894-1895), the Qing government signs the Treaty of Shimonoseki, by which it cedes sovereignty over Taiwan to Japan, which rules the island until 1945.","Di 1895, seld lexṣara di Trad Amenzu n Sinu-Ajabuni (1894-1895), anabaḍ Kwing yezmel Aɣan n Cimunuseki, d ayen yeǧǧan leḥkem n Taywan i Jabu, iḥekmen tigzirt alama d 1945."
"Machu Picchu consist of three main structures, namely Intihuatana, the Temple of the Sun, and the Room of the Three Windows.","Maču Biču yesεa kraḍ n tɣessiwin tigejdanin, isem-nsent Intihuatana, Afakan n Yiṭij, d Texxamt n Kraḍ n Ṭwiqan."
Most of the buildings on the edges of the complex have been rebuilt in order to give tourists a better idea of how they originally appeared.,Tuget n yizudaɣ i qrib ad ɣlin n wadeg εawden-asen lebni i wakken ad sεun imerrayen tikti tamawayt ɣef wamek i d-banen di laṣel.
"By 1976, thirty percent of Machu Picchu had been restored and restoration continues till today.","Di tazwara n 1976, afmiḍi n kraḍ n tmerwin n Maču Biču εawden-as yerna mazal as-ttεawaden er tura."
"For example, the most common still image photography format in the world is 35mm, which was the dominant film size at the close of the analog film era.","D amedya, talɣa n useknew n tugniwin tusbiḍin tamagnut akk deg umaḍal d 35mm, i yellan d azal agejdan n usaru ɣer taggara n tallit n usarug arwasan."
"It is still produced today, but more importantly its aspect ratio has been inherited by digital camera image sensor formats.","Mazal er tura ttfarasen-tent, maca s wudem axatar ugar timeẓri-ines n teɣzi d tehri yewwi-t-id si talɣiwin n yimaṭṭafen n tweṣṣafin tumḍinin."
"The 35mm format is actually, somewhat confusingly, 36mm in width by 24mm in height.","Talɣa n 35mm d tidet, ɣas akken d ayen yessewhamen, 36mm di tehri ɣef 24mm di teɣzi."
The aspect ratio of this format (dividing by twelve to obtain the simplest whole-number ratio) is therefore said to be 3:2.,Timeẓri n teɣzi d tehri n talɣa-agi (ẓun s mraw d sin i wakken ad ssawḍen uṭṭun ummid n ufmiḍi afessas akk) ihi nan-d d akken d 3:2.
"Many common formats (APS family of formats, for example) are equal to or closely approximate this aspect ratio.","Aṭas n talɣiwin timagnutin (Tawacult n talɣiwin ABS, d amedya) εedlen neɣ qrib ad yaweḍ timeẓri-agi n teɣzi d tehri."
The much-abused and often-ridiculed rule of thirds is a simple guideline creating dynamism while keeping a measure of order in an image.,Alugen n kraḍ yettuḥeqren d yettwabehdlen d amnir kan ixelqen abawal skud tella tasunḍa deg tugna.
It states that the most effective place for the main subject is at the intersection of lines dividing the image into thirds vertically and horizontally (see example).,Qqaren-d d akken adeg amellil akk i usentel agejdan d eg uzdiger n yizelman ibeṭṭun tugna ɣef kraḍ s wudem aratak d uglawan (muqel amedya).
"During this period of European history, the Catholic Church, which had become rich and powerful, came under scrutiny.","Deg tallit-agi n umezruy n Tuṛuft, Taklizt Takaṭulit, yuɣalen d tanesbaɣuṛt d tin izemren, rran-tt ddaw n ussekyed iḥersen."
For over a thousand years the Christian religion had bound European states together despite differences in language and customs. I,I wugar n wagim n yiseggasen asɣan Amasiḥi yeqqen akken iwunak n Tuṛuft ulamma yella umgired deg tutlayin d wansayen.
Its all-pervading power affected everyone from king to commoner.,Adabu-is amagdez iḥuza yal amdan seg ugellid ɣer uẓawali.
One of the main Christian tenets is that wealth should be used to alleviate suffering and poverty and that the monetary funds of the church are there specifically for that reason.,Yiwen seg yimenzayen igejdanen n Yimasiḥiyen yenna-d d akken ilaq ad tettwaṣeṛṛef tbaɣuṛt i wakken ad sulwin anegriref d tgellelt akked daɣen d akken idrimen n teglizt llan i wanect-nni s wudem ulmis.
The central authority of the church had been in Rome for over a thousand years and this concentration of power and money led many to question whether this tenet was being met.,Yella-d udabu alemmas n teglizt di Rum ugar n wagim n yiseggasen yerna arekkez-agi n leḥkem d yedrimen yeǧǧa aṭas ad cakken ma yella dɣa yeffeɣ umenzay ɣer tafat.
"Soon after the outbreak of hostilities, Britain initiated a naval blockade of Germany.","Ciṭ kan seld mi bdant tenṭagin, Briṭanya tergel-as abrid n tegriwa i Lalman."
"The strategy proved effective, cutting off vital military and civilian supplies, although this blockade violated generally accepted international law codified by several international agreements of the past two centuries.","Aɣawas yeffeɣ-d d amellil, s ugzam n tmerna n yiserdasen d iɣaṛimen ilaqen, ɣas akken argal-agi n ubrid yeffeɣ akk i uṣaduf agraɣlan iqeblen s umata i sneglen waṭas n yemsisan di snat n tsutin-agi yezrin."
"Britain mined international waters to prevent any ships from entering entire sections of ocean, causing danger to even neutral ships.","Briṭanya terra tifezwayin deg waman igraɣlanen i wakken ad yesseḥbes yal aɣeṛṛabu seg unekcum ɣer teḥricin tummidin n yilel, d ayen i d-ismentlen amihi ula i yiɣeṛṛuba yexḍan."
"Since there was limited response to this tactic, Germany expected a similar response to its unrestricted submarine warfare.","Imi tella-d tiririt yesεan tilas ɣef ttiknit-agi, Lalman turǧa tiririt am tagi i trad-nsen n tneṭṭabin ur nesεi tilas."
"During the 1920s, the prevailing attitudes of most citizens and nations was that of pacifism and isolation.","Deg yiseggasen n 1920, adduden icuεen n tuget n yiɣeṛmanen d yeɣlanen d talwit akked uεzal n yiman."
"After seeing the horrors and atrocities of war during World War I, nations desired to avoid such a situation again in the future.","Seld mi walan tiwaɣiyin d lmijrimat d-yellan di Trad Amaḍlan I, iɣlanen bɣan ad ssinfen tagnit am tinna daɣen deg yimal."
"In 1884, Tesla moved to the United States of America to accept a job with the Edison Company in New York City.","Di 1884, Tesla iguǧǧa ɣer Yiwunak Yedduklen n Marikan i wakken ad yeqbel axeddim akked Tkebbanit Edisun di Teɣṛemt n Nyu Yurk."
"He arrived in the US with 4 cents to his name, a book of poetry, and a letter of recommendation from Charles Batchelor (his manager in his previous job) to Thomas Edison.","Yewweḍ ɣer Yiwunak Yedduklen s 4 durru ɣef yisem-is, adlis n tmedyazt, d tabrat n uweṣṣi sɣur Čarls Bačlur (amsefrek-is deg uxeddim-is aqbur) ɣer Tumas Edisun."
Ancient China had a unique way of showing different time periods; each stage of China or each family that was in power was a distinctive dynasty.,Ccinwa taqburt tesεa tamamekt taselyant i wakken ad mlen talliyin n wakud yemgaraden; yal amecwaṛ n Ccinwa neɣ yal tawacult i yellan deg leḥkem d tallit tageldant tusdidt.
Also between each dynasty was an unstable age of divided provinces. The best-known of these periods was the Three Kingdoms epoch taking place for 60 years between the Han and the Jin Dynasty.,Daɣen gar snat n talliyin tigeldanin yella-d wakud ur nerkid n temnaḍin yebḍan. Tallit yettwassnen akk d tallit n Kraḍ n Tgeldiwin i d-yellan 60 n yiseggasen gar Tallit Tageldant n Han d Ǧin.
During these periods fierce warfare took place between many nobles fighting for the throne.,Di talliyin-agi yella-d ṭraḍ aqessḥan gar waṭas n yihaggaren yettnaɣen ɣef lεerc.
The Three Kingdoms was one of the bloodiest eras in Ancient China’s history thousands of people died fighting to sit in the highest seat in the grand palace at Xi’an.,Kraḍ n Tgeldiwin d tallit zewwaɣen seg yidammen deg umezruy n Ccinwa Taqburt igiman n yemdanen yemmuten s umennuɣ i wakken ad qqimen ɣef ufeqqim εlayen akk deg uɣṛem ameqqran di Ksi'an.

Also after the Revolution occupations were open to all male applicants allowing the most ambitious and successful to succeed.,Daɣen seld Tanekkra lexdami ldint-d akk i yergazen d ayen isen-yefkan tagnit i win yellan yettmalah yerna yebɣa rbeḥ i wakken ad yerbeḥ.
Same goes for the military because instead of army rankings being based on class they were now based on cailaber.,Ay-agi yella-d ula i tredsa acku amsizwer n yiserdasen yettili-d ɣef leḥsab n usmil tura akka yettili-d ɣef leḥsab n ukaylabr-nsen.
The French Revolution also inspired many other repressed working class people of other country's to began their own revolutions.,Tanekkra Tafranṣiṣt tella-d d tahrest i waṭas n yemdanen ixeddamen menwala yettwaqemḍen n tmura niḍen i wakken ad bdun tinekkriwin-nsen.
Muhammad was deeply interested in matters beyond this mundane life. He used to frequent a cave that became known as “Hira‘” on the Mountain of “Noor” (light) for contemplation.,"Muḥemmed yerra lwehla-s mliḥ ɣer isental beṛṛa n tudert-is n menwala. "he cave itself, which survived the times, gives a very vivid image of Muhammad’s spiritual inclinations.","Ifri-nni s timmad-is, yeṭṭfen iman-is deg wakud, yefka-d tugna tamuddirt d akken muḥemmed imal ɣer teflest."
"Resting on the top of one of the mountains north of Mecca, the cave is completely isolated from the rest of the world.","Imi d-yella ɣef tqacuct n yiwen seg yidurar n ugafa n Mekka, ifri tettwaεzel s wudem ummid seg umaḍal."

"Nothing can be seen other than the clear, beautiful sky above and the many surrounding mountains. Very little of this world can be seen or heard from inside the cave.","Ur yelli wayen tzemreḍ ad twaliḍ niḍen siwa igenni, yeṣfan ahuskan nnig-is d yidurar is-d-yezzin. The Great Pyramid at Giza is the only one of the seven wonders that is still standing today.,Tazamugt Tameqqrant di Giza d tawḥidt seg ṣa n texlafin i mazal tbedd er ass-a.
"Built by the Egyptians in the third century BCE, the Great Pyramid is one of many large pyramid structures built to honor dead Pharaoh.","Bnan-tt Imaṣriyen deg tasut tis kraḍ Uqbel Talalit n Tmasiḥit, Tazamugt Tameqqrant d yiwet seg tsukiyin n tzumag timeqqranin yettwabnan i wakken ad arren iseɣ i Uferεun yemmuten."
"The Giza Plateau, or ""Giza Necropolis"" in the Egyptian Valley of the Dead contains several pyramids (of which the great pyramid is the largest), several small tombs, several temples, and the great Sphinx.","Tabraḥt n Giza, neɣ ""Timeqbeṛt Giza"" deg Uẓaɣar Tamaṣrit n Wid Yemmuten yesεa aṭas n tzumag (anda tella tzamugt tameqqrant d tin imeqqren akk), aṭas n yiẓekwan imecṭaḥ, aṭas n yifakan, d Usfinks ameqqran."
"The great pyramid was created to honor the Pharaoh Khufu, and many of the smaller pyramids, tombs, and temples were built to honor Khufu's wives and family members.","Tazamugt tameqqrant tettwabna i wakken ad arren iseɣ i Uferεun Xufu, ma d waṭas n tzumag timecṭaḥ, iẓekwan, d ifakan ttwabnan i wakken ad arren iseɣ i tlawin d iεeggalen n twacult n Xufu."
"The ""up bow"" mark looks like a V and the ""down bow mark"" like a staple or a square missing its bottom side.","Ticreṭ n ""tganza n ufella"" tettban am V ma d ""ticreṭ n tganza n wadda"" tettban am txellalt neɣ amkuẓ i wumi ixuṣ yidis-is n wadda."
"Up means you should start at the tip and push the bow, and down means you should start at the frog (which is where your hand is holding the bow) and pull the bow.","D assawen anamek-is ilaq ad tebduḍ seg yixf dɣa ad tetekkiḍ ɣef tganza, ma d akessar anamek-is ilaq ad tebduḍ seg ugru (anda yeṭṭef ufus-ik taganza) tjebḍeḍd taganza."
"An up-bow usually generates a softer sound, while a down-bow is stronger and more assertive.","Taganza n usawen tesuffuɣ-d imesli axfifan, ma d tganza n wadda imesli-ines d azuran yerna yeǧhed ugar."
"Feel free to pencil in your own marks, but remember the printed bowing marks are there for a musical reason, so they should usually be respected.","Ur ttkukrut ara ɣas jerrdet ticraḍ-nwen s uɣanib, maca cfut d akken ticraḍ n tganza yettwassagzen llant i tmentilt tamẓawant, dimi akka ilaq ad sent-tgem udem s wudem unnim."
"The terrified King Louis XVI, Queen Marie Antoinette their two young children (11 year old Marie Therese and four year old Louis-Charles) and the King's sister, Madam Elizabeth, on the 6th October 1789 were forced back to Paris from Versailles by a mob of market women.","Agellid Lwis XVI, Tagellidt Mari Antwanet sin n warraw-nsen imecṭaḥ (Mari Terez yesεan di leεmeṛ-is 11 n yiseggasen d Lwis-Čarls yesεan 4 n yiseggasen di leεmeṛ-is) akked weltma-s n Ugellid, Massa Elizabet, imi ugaden di 6 Tuber 1789 rran-ten ugraw n tlawin n ulzuz si Fersay ɣer Bari."
"In a carriage, they traveled back to Paris surrounded by a mob of people screaming and shouting threats against the King and Queen.","Deg tcariṭ-nsen, mi unagen d tuɣalin ɣer Bari zzin-asen-d agraw n lɣaci yettuɣun yerna attεeggiḍen aggazen mgal Agellid d Tgellidt."
The mob of people forced the King And Queen to have their carriage windows wide open.,Agraw n lɣaci ḥerṣen Agellid d Tgellidt i wakken ad ldin mliḥ ṭṭiqan n tcariṭ-nsen.
At one point a member of the mob waved the head of a royal guard killed at Versailles in front of the terrified Queen.,Deg yiwen n wakud amaṣlaḍ n ugraw yesḥerrek aqaṛṛu n uεessan ageldan yettwanɣan di Fersay zdat n Tgellidt yugaden.
The war expenditures of U.S. imperialism in the conquest of the Philippines were paid for by the Filipino people themselves.,Aṣerref n Ṭrad n Umbiryalism Amarikani deg uẓḍam ɣef Lfilibbin yella-d si lǧyub n ugdud Afilibinu s timmad-nsen.
They were compelled to pay taxes to the U.S. colonial regime to defray a major part of the expenditures and the interest on bonds floated in the name of the Philippine government through the Wall Street banking houses.,Terra-ten tmara ad xelṣen tiwsiyin i unabaḍ amhersan Amarikani i wakken xellṣen amur ameqqran n useṛṛef n Ṭrad yerna akk afmiḍi n tmara yella-d ɣef yisem n unabaḍ Afilibbini seg yixxamen n tbanka n Wall Strit.
"Of course, the superprofits derived from the protracted exploitation of the Filipino people would constitute the basic gains of U.S. imperialism.","D ayen ibanen, ibaɣuren n tmerna i d-yekkan si tukerḍa idumen n ugdud Afilibinu swayes yerbeḥ akk umberyalism Amarikani."
To understand the Templars one must understand the context that prompted the creation of the order.,I wakken ad tfehmeḍ Imnayen Imasiḥiyen ilaq ad tfehmeḍ asatal i d-yeglan s usnulfu n umizzwer.
"The age where the events took place is commonly referred as the High Middle Ages the period of European history in the 11th, 12th, and 13th centuries (AD 1000–1300).","Tallit anda d-ḍran ineḍruyen qqaren-as s wudem amagnu Tallit Tanammat Ɛlayen i tallit n umezruy Aṛufi deg Tasut tis 11, tis 12, d tis 13 (1000-1300 Seld Tamasiḥt)."
"The High Middle Ages were preceded by the Early Middle Ages and followed by the Late Middle Ages, which by convention ends around 1500.","Tallit Tanammat Ɛlayen tezwar-itt-d Tallit Tanammat Tamenzut dɣa teḍfer-itt-id Tallit Tanammat Taneggarut, i yekfan s umsisi tamudi n 1500."
"Technological determinism is a term that encompasses a wide range of ideas in practice, from technology-push or the technological imperative to a strict sense that human destiny is driven by an underlying logic associated with scientific laws and their manifestation in technology.","Timḥettemt tatiknulujit d awal i yesdukklen agraw wessiɛen n tektiwin deg unnar n uṭebbeq, seg udegger-atiknuluji neɣ lmeḥwiǧat n tetiknulujit ɣer lmeɛna id-iqqaren belli lmektub n wemdan tselḥuy-it tmeẓla tagejdant iqqnen ɣer isuḍaf ussnanen akked ubani-nsen di tetiknulujit."
"Most interpretations of technological determinism share two general ideas: that the development of technology itself follows a path largely beyond cultural or political influence, and that technology in turn has ""effects"" on societies that are inherent, rather than socially conditioned.","Amur ameqqran n usmedya n temḥettemt tatiknulujit cerken snat n tektiwin timatuyin: belli anerni n tetiknulujit s timmad-is itabaɛ abrid ibaɛden s waṭas ɣef tezrirt n yidles neɣ n tsertit, yarna tatiknulujit-agi daɣen tesɛa ""isemda"" ɣef tmettiyin i yellan d igejdanen, mačči d wid ittucaṛḍen s wudem ametti."
"For example, one might say that the motor car necessarily leads to the development of roads.","Amedya, nezmer ad n-ini belli takeṛṛust ileḥḥun s umutur tegla-d s usnerni n iberdan."
"However, a nationwide road network is not economically viable for just a handful of cars, so new methods of production are developed to reduce the cost of car ownership.","Akken ibɣu yili, aẓeṭṭa n yiberdan aɣelnaw ur isɛi ara azal s wudem adamsan i tkemmict kan n tkeṛṛusin, ɣef aya tarrayin timaynutin n ufares ttusnulfant-d i usenqes n ssuma n sɛaya n tkeṛṛust."
"Mass car ownership also leads to a higher incidence of accidents on the roads, which leads to the invention of new techniques in healthcare for repairing damaged bodies.","Tilit n waṭas n tkeṛṛusin daɣen tgellu-d s tyita meqqren akter n yisehwa n yiberdan, ayen ara d-yeglun s usnulfu n tetwilin timaynutin di tujjya i useḥlu n tfekkiwin inṭeṛṛen."
"Romanticism had a large element of cultural determinism, drawn from writers such as Goethe, Fichte, and Schlegel.","Tallit n Trumansit tesεa aferdis ameqqran n uεewwel adelsan, d-yekkan seg imura am Gutu, Ficte, d Clegel."
"In the context of Romanticism, the geography molded individuals, and over time customs and culture related to that geography arose, and these, being in harmony with the place of the society, were better than arbitrarily imposed laws.","Deg usatal n Trumansit, tarakalt temsel imdanen, yerna s wakud insayen d yidles icudden ɣer trakalt banen-d, yerna wigi, imi sεan amekkan-nsen deg tmetti, ifen iṣudaf yettwaḥettmen kan akka."
"In the manner that Paris is known as the fashion capital of the contemporary world, Constantinople was regarded as the fashion capital of feudal Europe.","Akken tettwassen Paris d tamanaɣt n waɣan n umaḍal azi, Kunstantinubl ttwalin-tt d tamanaɣt n waɣan n Tuṛuft tabukalt."
Its renown for being an epicenter of luxury began in about 400 A.D. and lasted up until about 1100 A.D.,Tamelt-is imi tella d ammas n ulameɣ yebda akken di 400 mbaεd talalit n Sidna Ɛisa yerna tdum alamma d 1100 mbaεd talalit n Sidna Ɛisa.
Its status declined during the twelfth century mainly due to the fact that Crusaders had returned bearing gifts such as silks and spices that were valued more than what Byzantine markets offered.,Yeɣli uẓayeṛ-is deg tmiḍi tis tnac s wudem agejdan imi Inmidagen uɣalen-d wwin-d arazen am leḥrir d iεeqqaṛen yesεan ugar n wazal ɣef wayen i d-ttafen deg wulzuzen n Yibizenṭiyen.
It was at this time that the transfer of the title of Fashion Capital from Constantinople to Paris was made.,Deg akud-nni i d-yella ubeddel n uzwel n Tmanaɣt n Telkimt si Kunstantinubl ɣer Paris.
Gothic style peaked in the period between the 10th - 11th centuries and the 14th century.,Aɣan Aguti yewweḍ taqacuct deg tallit gar tasut tis 10 - d tis 11 d tasut tis 14.
At the beginning dress was heavily influenced by the Byzantine culture in the east.,Di tazwara yesεa udles Abizantini tazrirt meqqren ɣef lebsa deg usamar.
"However, due to the slow communication channels, styles in the west could lag behind by 25 to 30 year.","Maca, imi ẓayen imaṭṭafen n teywelt, aɣanen deg umalu ttεeṭṭilen s 25 ɣer 30 n yiseggasen ɣer deffir."
towards the end of the Middle Ages western Europe began to develop their own style. one of the biggest developments of the time as a result of the crusades people began to use buttons to fasten clothing.,ɣer taggara n Tallit Talemmast Tuṛuft n umalu tebda ad tesnulfuy aɣan n yiman-is. yiwen n usnulfu meqqren akk n tallit d ayen i yeǧǧan imdanen n yimidagen ad bdun ad ttarran tiqeffilin i wakken ad ṭṭfen iceṭṭiḍen-nsen.
Subsistence agriculture is agriculture carried out for the production of enough food to meet just the needs of the agriculturalist and his/her family.,Tafellaḥt n tudert d tafellaḥt i xeddmen i ufares n ddeqs n wučči i wakken kan ad ččen ifellaḥen d twaculin-nsen.
"Subsistence agriculture is a simple, often organic, system using saved seed native to the ecoregion combined with crop rotation or other relatively simple techniques to maximize yield.","Tafellaḥt n tudert d anagraw isehlen, tikkwal agaman, s usexdem n zzeriεa n tmurt-nni yettwajemεen i sdukkulen s tuzzya n yirden neɣ timamkin tiḥerfiyin icudden ɣer waya i wakken ad snernin lɣella."
Historically most farmers were engaged in subsistence agriculture and this is still the case in many developing nations.,Deg umezruy tuget n yifellaḥen ttekkan deg tfellaḥt n tudert yerna d ayen mazal ɣer tura deg waṭas n yiɣlanen deg ubrid n tneflit.
Subcultures bring together like-minded individuals who feel neglected by societal standards and allow them to develop a sense of identity.,Idelsan imecṭaḥ jemεen-d imdanen yesεan tidmiyin yettemcabin yettḥassan d akken ttwaεzalen seg yilugan imettiyen yerna fkan-asen tagnit i wakken sneflin anamek n tmagit.
"Subcultures can be distinctive because of the age, ethnicity, class, location, and/or gender of the members.","Nezmer ad d-neεqel idelsan imecṭaḥ s leεmeṛ, agraw atni, taserkemt, adeg, d/neɣ tuzzuft n yimaṣlaḍen."
"The qualities that determine a subculture as distinct may be linguistic, aesthetic, religious, political, sexual, geographical, or a combination of factors.","Tulmisin yesbanayen amek ad tεeqleḍ adles amecṭuḥ zemrent ad ilint d tisnilsanin, tifulkanin, tisɣanin, tisertiyin, tuzzufin, tirakalin, neɣ d asdukkel n yimgan."
"Members of a subculture often signal their membership through a distinctive and symbolic use of style, which includes fashions, mannerisms, and argot.","Imaṣlaḍen n udles amecṭuḥ zgan sbanayen-d attekki-nsen s usexdem azamulan n waɣan yettmaεqalen , am lebsa, tikli, d tmeslayt."
"One of the most common methods used to illustrate the importance of socialization is to draw upon the few unfortunate cases of children who were, through neglect, misfortune, or wilful abuse, not socialized by adults while they were growing up.","Yiwet si tarrayin timagnutin akk yettwasxedmen i wakken ad d-nesmedya azal n usmetti d tumla n kra n tejṛutin yettuɣaḍen n warrac imecṭaḥ i, s ustehzi, lexṣaṣ n zher, neɣ tameḥqranit s lebɣi, ur ten-smettin ara imengaḍen mi ttimɣuren."
"Such children are called ""feral"" or wild. Some feral children have been confined by people (usually their own parents); in some cases this child abandonment was due to the parents' rejection of a child's severe intellectual or physical impairment.","Arrac imecṭaḥ am wigi qqaren-asen d ""imulasen"" neɣ d iweḥciyen. Kra n warrac imecṭaḥ imulasen qqnen-ten deg uxxam yemdanen (s wudem imezgi d imawlan-nsen); di kra n tejṛutin n usinef n ugrud-agi yella-d imi imawlan ur qbilen ara iɣeblan n tdawsa taɣaṛant d taggagt iweεren n ugrud."
Feral children may have experienced severe child abuse or trauma before being abandoned or running away.,Igerdan iweḥciyen yezmer jerrben tamuḥqranit neɣ d tiyita qessiḥen uqbel ad ten-ǧǧen neɣ ad rewlen.
Others are alleged to have been brought up by animals; some are said to have lived in the wild on their own.,Llan wiyaḍ qqaren-d fell-asen d akken rebban-ten-id iɣersiwen; kra niḍen nnan-d fell-asen d akken dren deg teẓgi i yiman-nsen.
"When completely brought up by non-human animals, the feral child exhibits behaviors (within physical limits) almost entirely like those of the particular care-animal, such as its fear of or indifference to humans.","Imi tturebban-d s wudem ummid sɣur iɣersiwen war-alsiyen, igerdan iweḥciyen ttammalen-d tikli ( s tilisa tiɣaṛanin) qrib am tin n yiɣersiwen i ten-irebban, am tugdi-nsen neɣ tigurzent ɣer yilsiyen."
"While project based learning should make learning easier and more interesting, scaffolding goes a step beyond.","Imi almad yebnan ɣef usenfar yessishil almad yerna yettara-t yesεa azal, tasuki n leεḍil tεedda akkin i waya."
Scaffolding is not a method of learning but rather an aid that provides support to individuals whom are undergoing a new learning experience such as using a new computer program or beginning a new project.,Tasuki n leεḍil ur telli d tarrayt n ulmad maca d lemεawna i yettεawanen imdanen i yesεan tirmit n ulmad tamaynut am usexdem n useɣzan amaynut n uselkam neɣ tazwara n usenfar amaynut.
"Scaffolds can be both virtual and real, in other words, a teacher is a form of scaffold but so is the little paperclip man in Microsoft Office.","Wid-agi yettεawanen zemren ad ilin d uhlisen neɣ d ilawen, s wawalen niḍen, aselmad d talɣa n umεiwen maca ula d amessak n lkaɣeḍ n Lbiru Mikrusuft."
"Virtual Scaffolds are internalized in the software and are meant to question, prompt, and explain procedures that may have been to challenging for the student to handle alone.","Imεiwnen uhlisen llan deg useɣzan yerna llan i wakken ad steqsin, sḥercen, akked ad segzun tisekkirin iweεṛen i yinelmaden ad tent-fehmen s yiman-nsen."
"Children are placed in Foster Care for a wide variety of reasons that range from neglect, to abuse, and even to extortion.","Igerdan ttilin deg Ixxamen n Twaculin niḍen ɣef waṭas n ssebbat tanḍiyin seg ustehzi, tamuḥqranit, ula ɣer tukksa."
"No child should ever have to grow up in an environment that is not nurturing, caring, and educational, but they do.","Ur yelli ugrud ilaqen ad yimɣur deg uxxam anda ulac leḥmala, aseḥbiber, d usinen, maca nutni ddren akka."
We perceive the Foster Care System to be a safety zone for these children.,Nettwali d akken Anagraw n Twaculin Yettrebbin d adeg yesεan taɣellist i yigerdan-agi.
"Our foster care system is supposed to provide safe homes, loving caregivers, stable education, and reliable health care.","Anagraw-nneɣ n twaculin yettrebbin tiṭ-is ad yefk ixxamen yesεan taɣellist, imejjayen yesεan tayri, asinen irekden, d asejji bu taflest."
Foster care is supposed to provide all the necessities that were lacking in the home they were previously taken from.,Ixxamen n twaculin yettrebbin ilaq ad sεun akk ayen ixuṣṣen deg yixxamen seg ansi id ten-id-yekksen yakan.
The Internet combines elements of both mass and interpersonal communication.,Internet yesdukkel iferdisen n teɣwalt n waṭas n lɣaci d tin gar yemdanen.
The distinct characteristics of the Internet lead to additional dimensions in terms of the uses and gratifications approach.,Tulmisin tufṛizin n Internet ṣṣawaḍent ɣer tsektiwin timernanin deg wayen yeεnan tudsa n useqdec akked taḍfi.
"For example, “learning” and “socialization” are suggested as important motivations for Internet use (James et al., 1995).","D amedya, ""almad"" d ""wesmetti"" summren-ten am isguffden ixataren i useqdec n Internet (James d wiyaḍ., 1995)."
“Personal involvement” and “continuing relationships” were also identified as new motivation aspects by Eighmey and McCord (1998) when they investigated audience reactions to websites.,"""Attekki udmawan"" d ""wassaɣen imaɣlalen"" ula d nutni ukzen-ten d timeẓṛa timaynutin n wesguffed sɣur Aymi d MakKurd (1998) mi ḥettcen tisedmirin ɣef yismal web."
"The use of video recording has led to important discoveries in the interpretation of micro-expressions, facial movements which last a few milliseconds.","Asexdem n usekles ufidyu yegla-d s tegrutin tixatarin di lefhama n tenfaliyin-timecṭaḥ, imbiwlen n wudem i yettdummun kra n tasinin timecṭaḥ maḍi."
"In particular, it is claimed that one can detect whether a person is lying by interpreting micro-expressions correctly.","Ladɣa, qqaren-d d akken yezmer ad nẓer ma yella yeskiddib umdan s lefhama akken iwata n tenfaliyin timecṭaḥ maḍi."
"Oliver Sacks, in his paper The President's Speech, indicated how people who are unable to understand speech because of brain damage are nevertheless able to assess sincerity accurately.","Ulifer Saks, deg lkaɣeḍ-is Inaw n Uselway, yemla-d amek imdanen ur nezmir ad fehmen inaw acku yettwaɣ wallaɣ-nsen zemren ihi ad ssitgen tidet s tiseddi."
He even suggests that such abilities in interpreting human behavior may be shared by animals such as domestic dogs.,Yessumer daɣen d akken ikettaṛen am wigi deg usegzi n tikli talsit zemren ad ten-cerken akked yiqjan n wuxxam.
Twentieth century research has shown that there are two pools of genetic variation: hidden and expressed.,Anadi n tasut tis snat n tmerwin yemla-d d akken llan sin n yinawen n ubeddel ajini: udrig d aεinani.
"Mutation adds new genetic variation, and selection removes it from the pool of expressed variation.","Tiḍermas rnant-d abeddel ajini, ma d afran yettekkses-it seg unaw n ubeddel εinani."
Segregation and recombination shuffle variation back and forth between the two pools with each generation.,Beṭṭu d wallus n usdukkel rwin abeddel seg wanaw ɣer wayeḍ gar sin n wanawen s yal tasuta.
"Out on the savanna, it is hard for a primate with a digestive system like that of humans to satisfy its amino-acid requirements from available plant resources.","Beṛṛa di teẓgi, yewεeṛ lḥal i yebki s unagraw n uεebbuḍ-is yeẓẓaḍen am win n wulsiyen i wakken ad yeṣṣaweḍ ayen i d-yeḍleb aminu-acid s yemɣan yellan."
"Moreover, failure to do so has serious consequences: growth depression, malnutrition, and ultimately death.","Ernu ɣer waya, ma yella ur ṣṣawḍen ara ad xedmen ayagi ad yexleq inelkimen meqqren: anezgum n temɣer, laẓ, d taggara-nsen d tamettant."
"The most readily accessible plant resources would have been the proteins accessible in leaves and legumes, but these are hard for primates like us to digest unless they are cooked.","Imɣan yellan akk i zemren ad d-afen d ibrutinen yellan deg iferrawen d lxeḍra, maca wigi ur yezmir uεebbuḍ-nneɣ n yibkan am nukni ad ten-yexdem siwa ma yella wwan."
"In contrast, animal foods (ants, termites, eggs) not only are easily digestible, but they provide high-quantity proteins that contain all the essential amino acids.","D anemgal, učči n yiɣersiwen (tiweḍfin, ibaεεac, d tmellalin) mačči kan yeẓẓaḍ-iten uεebbuḍ s tefses, maca ččuren d yibrutinen n tɣara εlayen yesεan akk aminu-asids ilaqen."
"All things considered, we should not be surprised if our own ancestors solved their ""protein problem"" in somewhat the same way that chimps on the savanna do today.","Ma yella neṭṭef akk tiɣawsiwin, ur nwehhem ara ma yella lejdud-nneɣ ufan-d ixf i ""yiɣeblan-nsen n yibrutinen"" s yiwet n tmamekt akken xeddmen icambunziyen tura deg teẓgi."
Sleep interruption is the process of purposefully awakening during your normal sleep period and falling asleep a short time later (10–60 minutes).,Aḥbas n yiḍes d akala n tnekra s lebɣi deg tallit n yiḍes amagnu akked yiḍes ciṭ n wakud kan sakkin (10-60 n tesdatin).
This can be easily done by using a relatively quiet alarm clock to bring you to consciousness without fully waking you.,Ay-agi tzemreḍ ad t-xedmeḍ s usexdem n umsaki ur nxeddem ara aṭas n ṣṣut i wakken ad k-id-yawi ɣer tefrit mebla ma yessaki-k-id.
"If you find yourself resetting the clock in your sleep, it can be placed on the other side of the room, forcing you to get out of bed to turn it off.","Ma yella tufiḍ iman-ik tettalseḍ acεal n umsaki deg iḍeṣ-ik, tzemreḍ ad t-terreḍ deg yidis nniḍen n texxamt, d ayen ad k-yeǧǧen ad tekkreḍ i wakken ad t-tessexṣiḍ."
"Other biorhythm-based options involve drinking lots of fluid (particularly water or tea, a known diuretic) prior to sleep, forcing one to get up to urinate.","Tibdal niḍen yebnan ɣef tebyuritm d tissit n waṭas n waman (ladɣa aman neɣ latay, adyuritik yettwassnen) send iḍes, d ayen ad ak-yeǧǧen ad d-kkreḍ i wakken ad tbecceḍ."
The amount of inner peace a person possesses correlates oppositely to the amount of tension in one’s body and spirit.,Afmiḍi n talwit n daxel i yesεa umdan tcudd s wudem anmengal ɣer ufmiḍi n waddad deg tfekka n umdan d wallaɣ-is.
"The lower the tension, the more positive the life force present. Every person has the potential to find absolute peace and contentment.","Simmal yettenqas waddad, simmal tettili tudert d tilawt. Yal amdan yezmer ad yaf talwit d tumert."
Everyone can achieve enlightenment. The only thing standing in the way of this goal is our own tension and negativity.,Yal yiwen deg-neɣ yezmer ad yaweḍ ɣer tafat. Yiwet n tɣawsa kan ireglen abrid ɣer yiswi-agi d addad-nneɣ d tibawt-nneɣ.
"The Tibetan Buddhism is based on the teachings of Buddha, but were extended by the mahayana path of love and by a lot of techniques from Indian Yoga.","Abudi Atibitan yebna ɣef ulmad n Budda, maca swessεen-t s ubrid n tayri n mahayana d waṭas n ttekniyin seg Uyuga Ahendi."
"In principle the Tibetan Buddhism is very simple. It consists of Kundalini Yoga, meditation and the path of all-embracing love.","Di laṣel Abbudi Atibitan d aḥerfi mliḥ. D Ayuga Akundalini, ddeεwat d ubrid n yakk tayri i d-yezzin."
"With Kundalini Yoga the Kundalini energy (enlightenment energy) is awakened through yoga postures, breathing exercises, mantras and visualizations.","Akked Uyuga Akundalini ssehḍ Akurdalini (ssehḍ n tafat) yekker-d s tiɣimitin n Yuga, irmuden n uneffes, mantras d tmuɣliwin."
"The center of Tibetan meditation is the Deity Yoga. Through the visualization of various deities the energy channels are cleaned, the chakras are activated and the enlightenment consciousness is created.","Ammas n uweḥḥed Atibitan d Ayuga n Yillu. S tmuɣli n yilluten anḍiyen iberdan n ssehḍ zeddigen-d, icakraten ukin-d yerna tafrit n tafat tettwaxleq-d."
"Germany was a common enemy in World War 2, leading to cooperation between the USSR and USA. With the end of the war the clashes of system, process and culture led to the countries falling out.","Lalman d acengu icerken deg Trad Amaḍlan 2, d ayen i d-yeglan s tdukkli gar Russ d Yiwunak Yedduklen. Γer taggara n trad amennuɣ n unagraw, akala d yidles yeṣṣaweḍ timura ad nnaɣen."
"With two years of the end of the war, the former allies were now enemies and the Cold War began.","Sin n yiseggasen seld taggara n trad, imeddukal iqburen uɣalen tura d iεdawen dɣa tebda Traḍ Aṣemmaḍ."
"It was to last for the next 40 years and would be fought for real, by proxy armies, on battlefields from Africa to Asia, in Afghanistan, Cuba and many other places.","Idum 40 n yiseggasen-nni ɣer zdat yerna nnuɣen s tidet, s yiserdasen i d-juban, deg wannaren n umennuɣ si Tefṛiqt ɣer Asya, di Afɣanistan, Kuba d waṭas n yidgan niḍen."
"By September 17, 1939, the Polish defense was already broken, and the only hope was to retreat and reorganise along the Romanian bridgehead.","Di tazwara n 17 di Ctember, 1939, tamḥaddit Tabulunit tebḍa, yerna assirem kan i d-yegran d ajbad n yiman akked wallus n tuddsa deg ubrid n unekcum n usagen Aṛumani."
"However, these plans were rendered obsolete nearly overnight, when over 800,000 soldiers from the Soviet's Union Red Army entered and created the Belarussian and Ukrainian fronts after invading the eastern regions of Poland in violation of the Riga Peace Treaty, the Soviet-Polish Non-Aggression Pact, and other international treaties, both bilateral and multilateral.","Maca, iɣawasen-agi qedmen gar yiḍ d wass, anda 800,000 n yiserdasen seg Tredsa Tazewwaɣt n Tdukkla Tasufyit kecmzn yerna xelqen-d inekcumen n Belarussi d Ukren seld mi nebzen tamiwin n usamar n Buland s uεfas n Umsisi n Talwit Riga, Arkawal n War-takeṛṛiḍt n Sufyit-Buland, d yemsisiyen igraɣlanen niḍen, wid yesεan sin n yidisen d wid yesεan ugar n yidisen."
Using ships to transport goods is by far the most efficient way to move large amounts of people and goods across oceans.,Asexdem n yiɣeṛṛuba i wakken ad awin sselεa d tamamekt yelḥan akk i wakken ad zegren imdanen d sselεa ilel.
"The job of navies has traditionally been to ensure that your country maintains the ability to move your people and goods, while at the same time, interfering with your enemy's ability to move his people and goods.","Leqdic n tagriwa si zik ilaq ad tetḥeqq d akken tamurt-ik tezmer ad tawi imdanen-is d sselεa-nsen, ma yella deg yiwen n wakud, ad ger iman-is deg ukettaṛ n ucengu-ines ad yawi imdanen-is d sselεa-ines."
One of the most noteworthy recent examples of this was the North Atlantic campaign of WWII. The Americans were trying to move men and materials across the Atlantic Ocean to help Britain.,Yiwen seg yimedyaten imiranen akk i d-ibanen icudden ɣer waya d tawayt n Atlantik n Ugafa n Trad Amaḍlan II. Imarikaniyen εerḍen ad zegren irgazen d warrumen Ilel n Atlantik i wakken ad εiwnen Briṭanya.
"At the same time, the German navy, using mainly U-boats, was trying to stop this traffic.","Deg yiwen lweqt, iɣallen awlalen Almaniyen, s ttawil n tnebbaḍin s wudem agejdan, ɛaṛḍen ad ḥebsen tikli-agi."
"Had the Allies failed, Germany probably would have been able to conquer Britain as it had the rest of Europe.","Xas akken Imsisan ur as-sawḍen ara, Almanya ahat tezmer ad teẓdem ɣef Briṭanya akken texdem akked tamiwin niḍen n Uruba."
"Goats seem to have been first domesticated roughly 10,000 years ago in the Zagros Mountains of Iran.",Tiɣeṭṭen ttuṛebban-t i tikkelt tamezwarut qrib 10 000 n iseggasen ay-agi deg Idurar n Zagrus di Iran.
"Ancient cultures and tribes began to keep them for easy access to milk, hair, meat, and skins.","Idelsan iqdimen akked teqbilin bdan ttaǧǧan-tent i yifki, ccɛer, aksum akked uglim."
"Domestic goats were generally kept in herds that wandered on hills or other grazing areas, often tended by goatherds who were frequently children or adolescents, similar to the more widely known shepherd. These methods of herding are still used today.","Tiɣeṭṭen n ttṛebga ttaǧǧan-tent s umata di tqeḍɛiyin ittnadin di tɣaltin neɣ di temnaḍin niḍen n teksawt, ttɛassan-tent s umata imeksawen n tɣeṭṭen i yettilin s waṭas d igerdan neɣ d ilmeẓyen, ayen icuban ṣifa n umeksa ittwassen s waṭas. Tarrayin-agi n teksawt mazal ttusxedament ar ass-a."
Wagonways were built in England as early as the 16th Century.,Ibardan n tcaṛiḍin ttwabnan di Legliz di Lqaṛn wis 16.
"Although wagonways merely consisted of parallel planks of wood, they allowed horses pulling them to achieve greater speeds and pull larger loads than on the slightly more rough roads of the day.","Xas akken ibardan n tcaṛiḍin sɛan kan tilwiḥin n usɣaṛ imqabalen, ǧǧant iɛidiwen itent-ittseḥḥiben ad siwḍen ɣer tɣawla tameqqrant yarna ad seḥben taẓeyt tameqqrant kter n ibardan ur naɛdil ara deg wass."
"Crossties were introduced fairly early to hold the tracks in place. Gradually, however, it was realised that tracks would be more efficient if they had a stip of iron on the top.","Tilwiḥin n webrid kecment-d zik iwakken ad ṭṭfent iran n webrid deg umekkan-nsen. Ciṭuḥ ciṭuḥ, akken ibɣu yili, ufan-d belli iran-nni ad lhun kter lukan ad sɛun tissi n wuzzal s ufella."
"This became common practice, but the iron caused more wear on the wooden wheels of the wagons.","Aya-gi yuɣal d ccɣel imucaɛen, maca uzzal-nni isett rwadi n usɣaṛ n ticaṛiḍin."
"Eventually, wooden wheels were replaced by iron wheels. In 1767, the first full-iron rails were introduced.","Ɣer taggara, rwadi n usɣaṛ ttwabeddlent s rwadi n wuzzal. Di 1767, lulen-d ibardan n wuzzal s lekmal."
"The first known transportation was walking, humans began walking upright two million years ago with the emergence of Homo Erectus (meaning upright man).","Allal amezwaru ittwassnen n umesni d tikli, imdanen bdan leḥḥun s ibeddi sin imelyan n iseggasen ay-agi mi id-iflali Humu Eriktus (lmaɛna-s amdan ibedden)."
"Their predecessors, the Australopithecus did not walk upright as habitually.","Lejdud-nsen, Ustralubitaken ur leḥḥun ara s ibeddi am akken nuɣ tannumi."
"Bipedal specializations are found in Australopithecus fossils from 4.2-3.9 million years ago, although Sahelanthropus may have walked on two legs as early as seven million years ago.","Ufan timeẓliyin s sin iḍaṛṛen deg iɣuza n Ustralubitaken si 4.2-3.9 imelyan n iseggasen ay-agi, xas akken Sahelantrubus ahat lḥan ɣef sin iḍaṛṛen ṣa n imelyan n iseggasen ay-agi."
"We can start living more friendly to the environment, we can join to the environmental movement, and we can even be activists in order to reduce the future suffering in some degree.","Nezmer ad nebdu ad nettidir s wudem amdakkel akked twennaḍt, nezmer ad nttekki deg umussu n twennaḍt, yarna nezmer ad nili ula d imeɣnasen iwakken ad nessifses ciṭ anɛetteb id-iteddun."
"This is just like symptomatic treatment in many cases. However, if we do not only want a temporary solution, then we should find the root of the problems, and we should deactivate them.","Ta-agi am ddwa taskanant kan deg waṭas n lḥalat. Akken ibɣu yili, ma yella ur nebɣi ara kan tifrat n laɛḍil, ihi ilaq ad d-naf aẓar n iɣeblan, yarna ilaq ad ten-nekkes."
"It is obvious enough that the world has changed much because of humankind's scientific and technological advancements, and problems have become greater because of overpopulation and mankind's extravagant lifestyle.","D ayen ibanen belli ddunit tbeddel aṭas s sebba n unerni n tmusni akked tetiknulujit, dɣa iɣeblan ttimɣuṛen s sebba n temɣeṛ n wuṭun n imezdaɣ n ddunit akked wudmawen n tudert ittɛeddin tilas n yemdanen."
"After its adoption by Congress on July 4, a handwritten draft signed by the President of Congress John Hancock and the Secretary Charles Thomson was then sent a few blocks away to the printing shop of John Dunlap.","Mbeɛd mi yettwaqbel sɣuṛ Useqqamu di 4 Yulyu, asenfar yuran s ufus ittustenyan sɣur Uselway n Useqqamu Ǧun Hankuk akked Umaray Čarlz Tumsun ittuceyyeɛ umbeɛd ɣer tḥanutt n usiggez n Ǧun Dunlab."
"Through the night between 150 and 200 copies were made, now known as ""Dunlap broadsides"".","Deg yiḍ ger 150 ɣer 200 n telsuffeɣin i yettwaxedmen, tura ttwasnent s yisem n ""tewṛiqin n Dunlab""."
The first public reading of the document was by John Nixon in the yard of Independence Hall on July 8.,Leqraya tamezwarut zdat lɣaci n usenfar-agi tella-d sɣuṛ Ǧun Niksun deg ufrag n Tqaɛett n Tmunent di 8 Yulyu.
"One was sent to George Washington on July 6, who had it read to his troops in New York on July 9. A copy reached London on August 10.","Yiwet tettuceyyeɛ i Ǧurǧ Wacinṭun di 6 Yulyu, itt-id-iɣṛan i yiɣallen-is di Nyu Yurk di 9 Yulyu. Talsuffeɣt tewweḍ ɣer Lundun di 10 Ɣuct."
The 25 Dunlap broadsides still known to exist are the oldest surviving copies of the document. The original handwritten copy has not survived.,25 n telsuffeɣin n tewṛiqin n Dunlab i mazal ddrent d talsuffɣin iddren tiqdimin n usenfar. Asenfar amezwaru yuran s ufus ur iddir ara.
Many paleontologists today believe that one group of dinosaurs survived and is alive today. We call them birds.,Aṭas n imusnawen n iɣuza ass-agi ttwalin belli yiwen ugraw n idinuzuren imneɛ yarna mazal idder ar ass-a. Neqqar-asen ifrax.
Many people don't think about them as dinosaurs because they have feathers and can fly.,Aṭas n lɣaci ur ten-ttwalin ara d idinuzuren axaṭeṛ sɛan arric yarna ttfarfiren.
But there are a lot of things about birds that still look like a dinosaur.,Maca llan waṭas n lecɣal yaɛnan ifrax i yettemcabin ɣer udinuzur.
"They have feet with scales and claws, they lay eggs, and they walk on their two back legs like a T-Rex.","Sɛan iḍaṛṛen s tqecṛatin akked waccaren, srusun timellalin, yarna leḥḥun ɣef sin iḍaṛṛen n deffir am Ti-Reks."
Virtually all computers in use today are based on the manipulation of information which is coded in the form of binary numbers.,S wudem arillaway akk iselkimen ittwasexdamen ass-a bnan ɣef usexdem n isallen ittusenglen s wuṭunen imisinen.
"A binary number can have only one of two values, i.e. 0 or 1, and these numbers are referred to as binary digits - or bits, to use computer jargon.","Uṭun imisin izmer kan ad yili d yiwen wuṭun ɣef sin, lmaɛna-s 0 neɣ 1, yarna uṭunen-agi skanen ɣuṛ-sen s yisem n wuṭunen imisinen - neɣ ibiten, ma nessexdem imeslayen n uselkim."
"Internal poisoning may not be immediately apparent. Symptoms, such as vomiting are sufficiently general that an immediate diagnosis cannot be made.","Sem daxel n tfekka ahat ur d-ittban ara din din. Isekna, am iriran d imatuyen daymi ur izmir ara ad ittwaxdem usennefru din din."
The best indication of internal poisoning may be the presence of an open container of medication or toxic household chemicals.,Ayen ara d-iseknen s wudem amaway sem daxel n tfekka izmer ad yili d tilawt n tqerɛett n ddwa ildin neɣ tangawin takruranin isɛan sem.
Check the label for specific first aid instructions for that specific poison.,Wali itiki-nes i lewṣayat n lemɛawna tamezwarut yaɛnan sem-nni.
The term bug is used by entomologists in a formal sense for this group of insects.,Awal n lbeqq sexdamen-t imassanen n yibeɛɛac s lmeɛna alɣan i tegrawt-agi n yibeɛɛac.
"This term derives from ancient familiarity with Bed-bugs, which are insects highly adapted to parasitize humans.","Awal-agi ikka-d si tnummi taqdimt illan akked Lbeqq, d ibeɛɛucen i yellan d ijenṭiḍen ɣef yemdanen."
"Both Assassin-bugs and Bed-bugs are nidicolous, adapted to living in nest or housing of their host.","Di sin lbeqq amenɣaw akked lbeqq n wusu d ibeɛɛac, ittidiren di lɛecc neɣ di tmezduɣt n umesterḥeb-nsen."
"Across the United States of America, there are approximately 400,000 known cases of Multiple Sclerosis (MS), leaving it as the leading neurological disease in younger and middle aged adults.","Di Tmura Idduklen n Marikan, llant qrib 400 000 n lḥalat ittwassnen n lehlak n Multibl Sekliruziz (MS), ayen it-yarran d lehlak n wallaɣ agejdan di laɛmer ameẓyan akked ulemmas n imeqranen."
"MS is a disease that affects the central nervous system, which is made up of the brain, the spinal cord and the optic nerve.","MS d lehlak i yekkaten anagraw afeqɛan alemmas, i yesɛan allaɣ, lxiḍ bu isennanen akked lxiḍ n tmuɣli."
Research has found that females are two times more likely to have MS then males.,Anadi yufa-d belli tilawin helkent-tt sin ibardan kter n yergazen.
"A couple may decide it is not in their best interest, or in the interest of their child, to raise a baby.","Argaz d tmeṭṭut-is zemren ad ṭṭfen leqrar belli mačči di leṣlaḥ-nsen, neɣ i leṣlaḥ n mmi-tsen, ad d-ṛebbin agrud."
These couples may choose to make an adoption plan for their baby.,Argaz-agi d tmeṭṭut-is zemren ad xtiṛen ad fken mmi-tsen i ttṛebga.
"In an adoption, the birth parents terminate their parental rights so that another couple may parent the child.","Deg tikci n ugrud i ttṛebga, imawlan it-id-isɛan ad gen tilas i yizarfan-nsen s ṣifa-nsen d imawlan-is iwakken argaz d tmeṭṭut niḍen ad izmiren ad uɣalen d imawlan-is."
Science’s main goal is to figure out the way the world works through the scientific method. This method in fact guides most scientific research.,Iswi agejdan n tussna d afham amek tleḥḥu ddunit s tarrayt tussnant. Tarrayt-agi di tidett tettwellih amur ameqqran n inadiyen ussnanen.
"It isn’t alone though, experimentation, and an experiment is a test that is used to eliminate one or more of the possible hypotheses, asking questions, and making observations also guide scientific research.","Maca mačči uḥdes, tirmit, tirmit d aɛaṛeḍ i xeddmen iwakken ad sinfen yiwet neɣ kter n turdiwin, asteqsi n isteqsiyen, akked timawin daɣen ttwellihen anadi ussnan."
"Naturalists and philosophers focused on classical texts and, in particular, on the Bible in Latin.","Imusnawen n ugama akked ifiluzufen rran dehn-nsen ɣef tira taklasikit akked, abaɛda, ɣef Tira Iqedsen s Tlatinit."
"Accepted were Aristotle's views on all matters of science, including psychology.","Timuɣliwin n Aristu ɣef akk isental n tussna, gar-asen tussna n tnefsit, llant ttwaqeblent."
"As knowledge of Greek declined, the West found itself cut off from its Greek philosophical and scientific roots.","Mi tenqes tmussni n Lyunan, Amalu yufa-d iman-is igzem ɣef iẓewṛan-is Iyunaniyen ifiluzufiyen akked wussnanen."
Many observed rhythms in physiology and behavior often crucially depend on the presence of endogenous cycles and their production through biological clocks.,Aṭas walan lewqat di tfizyulujit akked ṭbiɛa tteklen s wudem agejdan ɣef tilin n talliyin n indujinen akked uxdam-nsen s saɛa tasnudrant.
"Periodic rhythms, which are not simply responses to external periodic cues, have been documented for most living beings, including bacteria, fungi, plants, and animals.","Talliyin, i yellan kan d tiririt i licarat n barra id-ittilin yal tallit, ttwajemɛen-d fell-asent isallen i umur ameqqran n lmexluqat ittidiren, gar-asen tabaktiritt, tiṛeɣla, imɣan, akked iɣerṣiwen."
Biological clocks are self sustaining oscillators which will continue a period of free-running cycling even in the absence of external cues.,Saɛa tasnudrant d taceṭaḥt ileḥḥun weḥdes i yettkemmilen tikli n tallit xas akken ulac licarat n baṛṛa.
The Hershey and Chase experiment was one of the leading suggestions that DNA was a genetic material.,Tirmit n Hercey akked Čays d yiwet id-iseknen belli ADN d tanga n lewrata.
"Hershey and Chase used phages, or viruses, to implant their own DNA into a bacterium.","Hercey akked Čays sxedmen infafaden, neɣ ibirusen, iwakken ad skecmen ADN-nsen di tbaktiritt."
They did two experiments marking either the DNA in the phage with a radioactive phosphorus or the protein of the phage with radioactive sulfur.,Xedmen snat n tirmitin anda ɛegnen ADN-nni daxel n unfafad s ufusfur ibaṛqen neɣ tabruntint n unfafad s usulfur ibaṛqen.
"Mutations can have a variety of different effects depending on the type of mutation, the significance of the piece of genetic material affected and whether the cells affected are germ-line cells.","Abeddel di ADN izmer ad isɛu aṭas n isemda yemgaraden aɛlaḥsab n ṣenf n ubeddel, azal i yesɛa uḥric-nni n tenga n lewrata taɛna temsalt akked ma tikwatin-agi d tikwatin n usefrurex."
"Only mutations in germ-line cells can be passed on to children, while mutations elsewhere can cause cell-death or cancer.","Ḥala abeddel di tekwatin n usefṛuṛex i yezemren ad ɛeddint ɣer igerdan, ma d abeddel anda niḍen izmer ad d-iglu s lmut n tekwatt-nni neɣ akunsir."
"Nature-based tourism attracts people interested in visiting natural areas for the purpose of enjoying the scenery, including plant and animal wildlife.","Aḥewwes ibnan ɣef ugama ijebbed-d imdanen ibɣan ad rzun ɣer temnaḍin tigamanin iwakken ad zhun s tmuɣli n imeẓṛiyen, isɛan imɣan akked iɣerṣiwen."
"Examples of on-site activities include hunting, fishing, photography, bird watching, and visiting parks and studying information about the ecosystem.","Imedyaten n lecɣal xeddmen deg umekkan gar-asen ṣyada, ṣyada n iselman, tuṭṭfa n tugniwin, tamuɣli n ifrax, akked tirza ɣer yelmaten akked leqraya n isallen yaɛnan anagraw n tudert-nsen."
"An example is visiting, photographing, and learning about organgatuangs in Borneo.","Amedya d aḥewwes, tuṭṭfa n tugniwin, akked unadi n isallen ɣef urgangatwang di Burnyu."
"Every morning, people leave small country towns in cars to go their workplace and are passed by others whose work destination is the place they have just left.","Yal taṣebḥit, imdanen ttefɣen si tuddar timecṭaḥ n tmurt s tkeṛṛusin iwakken ad ruḥen ɣer uxeddim ttmagaren-d wiyiḍ niḍen isɛan amekkan n uxeddim di taddart-nni ansi d-ruḥen."
"In this dynamic transport shuttle everyone is somehow connected with, and supporting, a transport system based on private cars.","Deg awi-err-agi yal yiwen iqqen ɣer, yarna ittḥami, anagraw n umesni ibnan ɣef tkeṛṛusin tusligin."
Science now indicates that this massive carbon economy has dislodged the biosphere from one of its stable states that has supported human evolution for the past two million years.,Tussna tura teskan-d belli tadamsa-agi tameqqrant n ukarbun tsembawel annar asnudran seg yiwet si lḥalat-is itrekden i yeḥuman anerni n wemdan i wazal n sin imelyan n iseggasen iɛeddan.
Everyone participates in society and uses transportation systems. Almost everyone complains about transportation systems.,Yal yiwen ittekki di tmetti yarna issexdam anagraw n umesni. Qrib yal yiwen ittcetki ɣef unagraw n umesni.
In developed countries you seldom hear similar levels of complaints about water quality or bridges falling down.,Di tmura innernan idrus mliḥ anda ara tesleḍ anect-agi n ucetki ɣef tezdeg n waman neɣ ɣelluy n tqenṭyar.
"Why do transportation systems engender such complaints, why do they fail on a daily basis? Are transportation engineers just incompetent? Or is something more fundamental going on?","Ayɣer inagrawen n umesni sɛan icetkiyen-agi, ayɣer gumman ad xedmen axeddim-nsen n yal ass? D ijenyuṛen n umesni i d ibujaden? Neɣ illa wacu illan niḍen d agejdan akter?"
Traffic Flow is the study of the movement of individual drivers and vehicles between two points and the interactions they make with one another.,Tikli n Tkeṛṛusin d tazrawt n umbiwel n inehharen akked tkeṛṛusin ger snat n tneqqiḍin akked wassaɣen ixeddmen wa-gar-asen.
"Unfortunately, studying traffic flow is difficult because driver behavior cannot be predicted with one-hundred percent certainty.","S usḥissef, tazrawt n tikli n tkeṛṛusin tewɛeṛ axaṭeṛ ṭbiɛa n unehhar ur tezmir ara ad d-ttucar s telkint n meyya ɣef meyya."
"Fortunately, drivers tend to behave within a reasonably consistent range; thus, traffic streams tend to have some reasonable consistency and can be roughly represented mathematically.","Ayen isefṛaḥen, lexdayem n inehharen ur ttemxalafent ara mliḥ; s wakka, tikli n tkeṛṛusin am akken tetabaɛ abrid ibanen i nezmer ad d-naf s leḥsab."
"To better represent traffic flow, relationships have been established between the three main characteristics: (1) flow, (2) density, and (3) velocity.","Iwakken ad d-nelhi akken ilaq d tikli n tkeṛṛusin, nesban-d assaɣen illan ger krad-agi n tulmisin: (1) amiri, (2) aṭuqqet, akked (3) tazzla."
"These relationships help in planning, design, and operations of roadway facilities.","Assaɣen-agi ttḥamin deg uheggi, lebni, akked lecɣal yaɛnan iberdan."
Insects were the first animals to take to the air. Their ability to fly helped them evade enemies more easily and find food and mates more efficiently.,Tibelɛucin ittferfiren d iɣerṣiwen imezwura i yeferfren. Tazmert-nsent ad ferfrent tḥuma-tent ad rewlent i yaɛdawen s tashuli yarna ad d-afent lmakla akked iḥbiben.
Most insects have the advantage of being able to fold their wings back along the body.,Amur ameqqran n tbelɛucin ittferfiren zemrent ad jemɛent iferrawen-nsent ɣef waɛrur-nsent.
This gives them a wider range of small places to hide from predators.,Aya-gi issefti imukan udyiqen anda zemrent ad frent ɣef yaɛdawen.
"Today, the only insects that cannot fold back their wings are dragon flies and mayflies.","Ass-agi, tibelɛucin kan ur nezmir ara ad jemɛent iferrawen-nsent d izḍi n tawla akked yizi n maggu."
"Thousands of years ago, a man called Aristarchus said that the Solar System moved around the Sun.","Luluf n iseggasen ay-agi, yiwen n urgaz isem-is Aristarkus inna-d belli Anagraw n Yiṭij ittezzi i Yiṭij."
"Some people thought he was right but many people believed the opposite; that the Solar System moved around the Earth, including the Sun (and even the other stars).","Kra n yemdanen umnen belli isɛa lḥeqq maca aṭas n lɣaci i yumnen anemgal n wa-yagi; belli Anagraw n Yiṭij ittezzi i Lqaɛa, gar-asen Iṭij (akked ula d itran niḍen)."
"This seems sensible, because the Earth doesn't feel as if it's moving, does it?","Ay-agi ittban-d iwha, axaṭeṛ ur nettḥulfu ara belli tettembiwil Lqaɛa, neɣ xaṭi?"
The Amazon River is the second longest and the biggest river on Earth. It carries more than 8 times as much water as the second biggest river.,Iɣẓer n Amazun d wis sin aɣezfan akk yarna d iɣẓer ameqqran akk di ddunit. Ittawi kter n 8 tikkal ayen ittawi iɣẓer ameqqṛan yakk wis sin n waman.
"The Amazon is also the widest river on Earth, at times six miles wide.","Amazun daɣen d iɣẓer ihrawen akk di ddunit, tikkwal seddis n lemyal di tehri."
A full 20 percent of the water that pours out of the planet's rivers into the oceans comes from the Amazon.,20 ɣef meyya n waman n iɣeẓṛan n ddunit ittmirin ɣer igarawen ttekken-d seg iɣẓer n Amazun.
"The main Amazon River is 6,387 km (3,980 miles). It collects water from thousands of smaller rivers.",Iɣẓer agejdan n Amazun isɛa di teɣzi 6387 km (3980 lemyal). Ittajmaɛ-d aman si luluf n iɣeẓṛan imecṭaḥ.
"Although pyramid-building in stone continued until the end of the Old Kingdom, the pyramids of Giza were never surpassed in their size and the technical excellence of their construction.","Xas akken lebni n tzumag s ublaḍ ikemmel armi d taggara n Tgelda Taqdimt, werǧin bnin xiṛ n tzumag n Ǧiza ama di temɣeṛ ama di lehhu atiknik n lebni-nsent."
"New Kingdom ancient Egyptians marvelled at their predecessors monuments, which were then well over a thousand year old.","Imaṣṛiyen iqdimen n Tgelda Tamaynut wehmen di lebni n lejdud-nsen, i yesɛan imar kter n walef n iseggasen."
Vatican City's population is around 800. It is the smallest independent country in the world and the country with the lowest population.,Uṭun n imezdaɣ n Batikan Siti 800. D tamurt tamunant tamecṭuḥt yakk di ddunit yarna d tamurt akk isɛan ciṭ n imezdaɣ.
Vatican City uses Italian in its legislation and official communications.,Batikan Siti tsexdam Taṭelyanit deg uṣaḍuf akked umeslay unṣib.
Italian is also the everyday language used by most of those who work in the state while Latin is often used in religious ceremonies.,Taṭelyanit d tutlayt n yal ass daɣen ittwasexdamen sɣuṛ umur ameqqran n wid ixeddmen di tmurt ma d Talatinit tettwasexdam s waṭas di tfugla n deyana.
All citizens of Vatican City are Roman Catholic.,Akk iɣeṛman n Batikan Siti d Ikatulikiyen Irumaniyen.
"People have known about basic chemical elements such as gold, silver, and copper from antiquity, as these can all be discovered in nature in native form and are relatively simple to mine with primitive tools.","Imdanen snen iferdisen akruranen igejdanen si teglest am dheb, lfeṭṭa, akked nḥas, imi wi-gi akk ttilin deg ugama s ṣifa-nsen tagamant yarna sehlen i tɣuzi s wallalen n zik."
"Aristotle, a philosopher, theorised that everything is made up of a mixture of one or more of four elements. They were earth, water, air, and fire.","Aristu, afiluzuf, ifka-d tamuɣli id-iqqaren belli kullec ittwaxdem s usdukkel n yiwen neɣ kter ger ukkuz n ifardisen. Akal, aman, abeḥri, akked tmes."
"This was more like the four states of matter (in the same order): solid, liquid, gas, and plasma, though he also theorised that they change into new substances to form what we see.","Aya-gi icuba ukkuz n lḥalat n tenga (s yiwen umyezwer) : d taqquṛant, d aman, d lgaz, akked blazma, xas akken tamuɣli-s teqqar-d belli ttuɣalent d tangawin timaynutin iwakken ad d-suffɣent ayen nettwali."
Alloys are basically a mixture of two or more metals. Don't forget that there are many elements on the periodic table.,Abumexluḍ n wuzzal s umata d asexleḍ n sin neɣ kter n wuzzalen. Ur ttettu ara belli llan waṭas n iferdisen di tfelwit n iferdisen.
"Elements like calcium and potassium are considered metals. Of course, there are also metals like silver and gold.",Ifardisen am ukalsyum akked ubutasyum ttuneḥsaben d uzzal. D ayen ibanen belli llan daɣen wuzzalen am lfeṭṭa akked dheb.
You can also have alloys that include small amounts of non-metallic elements like carbon.,Llan daɣen ibumexluḍen n wuzzal isɛan tikemmicin d timecṭaḥ n iferdisen war-uzzalen am ukarbun.
Everything in the Universe is made of matter. All matter is made of tiny particles called atoms.,Yal taɣawsa deg usedday tettwaxdem s tenga. Yal tanga tettwaxdem s tzelɣiwin timecṭaḥ iwumi qqaren ibelkimen.
Atoms are so incredibly tiny that trillions of them could fit into the period at the end of this sentence.,Ibelkimen mectuḥen mliḥ armi itrilyunen n ibelkimen zemren ad awin amekkan ara tawi tneqqiḍt illan ɣer taggara n tefyirt-agi.
"Thus, the pencil was a good friend to many people when it came out.","S wakka, imru yuɣal d amdakkel n waṭas n yemdanen mi d-yennulfa."
"Sadly, as newer methods of writing have emerged, the pencil has been relegated to lesser status and uses.","Ayen isseḥzanen, mi d-lulent tarrayin timaynutin n tira, imru yuɣal inqes usexdem-is."
"People now write messages on computer screens, never having to come close to a sharpener.","Imdanen tura uɣalen ttarun tibratin ɣef lmeryat n iselkimen, mebla ma qaṛṛben ɣer teṭayitt n imru."
One can only wonder what the keyboard will become when something newer comes along.,Amdan izmer kan ad iseqsi d acu ara s-iḍṛun i unasiw mi ara d-tennulfu tarrayt tamaynutt.
The fission bomb works on the principle that it takes energy to put together a nucleus with many protons and neutrons.,Tafezwayt n beṭṭu tebna ɣef umenzay id-yeqqaṛen belli tlaq tṣaṛeɣt i usdukkel n wul akked waṭas n ibrutunen d inutrunen.
Sort of like rolling a heavy cart up a hill. Splitting the nucleus up again then releases some of that energy.,Am uselḥu n tcaṛiṭ iẓẓayen s ufella n tiɣilt. Beṭṭu n wul-nni daɣen ad d-iserreḥ i kra di tṣaṛeɣt-nni.
Some atoms have unstable nuclei which means that they tend to break apart with little or no nudging.,Kra n ibelkimen sɛant ulawen ur nerkid ara lmaɛna-s zemren ad bḍun s ciṭ neɣ mebla lǧehd.
The surface of the Moon is made of rocks and dust. The outer layer of the Moon is called the crust.,Lqaɛa n Tziri tesɛa iblaḍen akked uɣebbaṛ. Tissi n baṛṛa n Tziri qqaren-as ticlemt.
The crust is about 70 km thick on the near side and 100 km thick on the far side.,Ticlemt tzur azal n 70 km si tama iqaṛben 100km si tama ibaɛden.
It is thinner under the maria and thicker under the highlands.,"D tabrarazt ddaw marya, yerna d tazurant ddaw tɣaltin."
There may be more maria on the near side because the crust is thinner. It was easier for lava to rise up to the surface.,Izmer ad yili ugar n marya ɣef tama axaṭeṛ ticlemt tabrarazt. Ishel i umenẓaṛ ad d-yali s ufella n lqaɛa.
Content theories are centered on finding what makes people tick or appeals to them.,Timuɣliwin n ugbur rrant dehn-nsent ɣef tifin n wacu ixeddmen lebɣi i yemdanen neɣ acu iten-ijebbden.
These theories suggest that people have certain needs and/or desires which have been internalized as they mature to adulthood.,Timuɣliwin-agi qqarent-d belli imdanen sɛan kra n lmeḥwiǧat akked/neɣ lebɣiwat i jemɛen asmi llan ttimɣuṛen armi bḍen d imeqqranen.
These theories look at what it is about certain people that make them want the things that they do and what things in their environment will make them do or not do certain things.,Timuɣliwin-agi ttwalint acu isen-ixeddmen lebɣi i yemdanen ad xedmen ayen xeddmen akked wacu illan di twennaḍt-nsen ara ten-ideggren ad xedmen neɣ ur xeddmen ara kra n lecɣal.
Two popular content theories are Maslow's Hierarchy of Needs Theory and Hertzberg's Two Factor Theory.,Snat n tmuɣliwin n ugbur imucaɛen d Tamuɣli n Umyezwer n Lmeḥwiǧat n Masluw akked Tmuɣli n Sinat Sebbat n Hertzberg.
"Generally speaking, two behaviors can emerge as managers begin to lead their former peers. One end of the spectrum is trying to remain “one of the guys” (or gals).","S umata, snat lexdayem tteflalint-d mi ara bdun inemhalen aselḥu n tnuda-nsen n zik. Yiwen idis ittɛaṛaḍ ad iqqim ""d yiwen seg yergazen-nni"" (neɣ tlawin-nni)."
"This type of manager has difficulty making unpopular decisions, performing disciplinary action, performance evaluations, assigning responsibility, and holding people accountable.","Ṣenf-agi n unemhal tettiwɛiṛ-as tuṭṭfa n leqṛaṛat inbuya, tuṭṭfa n leqṛaṛat n uɛaqeb, aktazal n uxeddim, tukci n tmasiyin, akked uḥaseb n imdanen."
"At the other end of the spectrum, one morphs into an unrecognizable individual that feels he or she must change everything the team has been doing and make it their own.","Si tama niḍen, amdan ad yuɣal d win ur nettwaɛqal ara i ttḥulfun belli netta neɣ nettat ilaq ad ibeddel akk ayen texdem terbaɛt n uxeddim yarna ad t-yerr d ayla-s."
"After all, the leader is ultimately responsible for the success and failure of the team.","Akken ibɣu yili, aqeṛṛu ɣer taggara d netta i d uksin n tarnawt akked lexṣaṛa n tarbaɛt."
This behavior oftentimes results in rifts between the leaders and the rest of the team.,Lexdayem-agi s umata gellunt-d s umennuɣ ger iqeṛṛa akked imedrawen n tarbaɛt.
"Virtual teams are held to the same standards of excellence as conventional teams, but there are subtle differences.","Tirebbuyaɛ tuhlisin ilaq ad qadrent ccuṛuṭ n lxedma igerzen am trebbuyaɛ timensayin, maca llan lxilafat imecṭaḥ."
Virtual team members often function as the point of contact for their immediate physical group.,Imedrawen n tarbaɛt tuhlist ttilin s umata d taneqqiḍt n temlilit n ugraw-nsen usrid.
They often have more autonomy than conventional team members as their teams may meet according to varying time zones which may not be understood by their local management.,S umata seɛɛun timanit kter n imedrawen n terbaɛt tamensayt imi zemrent trebbuyaɛ-nsen ad mlilent aɛlaḥsab n lxilaf n lweqt n temnaḍin ayen ahat ur tfehhem ara tmehla-nsent tadigant.
"The presence of a true “invisible team” (Larson and LaFasto, 1989, p109) is also a unique component of a virtual team.","Tilin n ""tarbaɛt tuffirt"" n tidett (Larsun akked LaFastu, 1989, asebter 109) d aferdis ixulfen n terbaɛt tuhlist."
The “invisible team” is the management team to which each of the members report. The invisible team sets the standards for each member.,"""Tarbaɛt tuffirt"" d tarbaɛt tanemhalt illan nnig n yal amedraw. Tarbaɛt tuffirt d nettat ara ad d-yefken ccuṛuṭ-is i yal amedraw."
Why would an organization want to go through the time consuming process of establishing a learning organization? One goal for putting organizational learning concepts into practice is innovation.,Ayɣer ara tebɣu tuddsa ad tḍeggeṛ lweqt deg usbeddi n tuddsa taḥafaḍt? Yiwen seg iswiyen n uṭebbeq n imenzayen n uselmed n tuddsa d asnulfu.
"When all available resources are effectively used across the functional departments of an organization, creativity and ingenuity can transpire.","Mi ara yili akk tiɣbula i wejden ttwasxedment akken ilaq deg igezda ixeddmen n tuddsa, asnulfu akked tmussni ad d-banen."
"As a result, the process of an organization working together to overcome an obstacle can lead to a new innovative process to serve the customer's need.","S wakka, amecwar n tuddsa ixeddmen lwaḥid iwakken ad sinfen aɛewwiq izmer ad d-yawi asnulfu amaynut ara d-ilhin d lmeḥwiǧat n umsaɣ."
"Before an organization can be innovative, leadership must create a culture of innovation as well as shared knowledge and organizational learning.","Uqbel ad tizmir tuddsa ad tili d tasnulfayt, aqeṛṛuy-is ilaq ad d-isker idles n usnulfu akked tmussni icerken akked uselmed n tuddsa."
"Angel (2006), explains the Continuum approach as a method being used to help organizations reach a higher level of performance.","Anǧel (2006), isefhem-d tikli n Ukuntinum am akken d tarrayt ittwasexdamen i uḥami n tuddsiwin iwakken ad awḍent ɣer uswir aɛlayan deg uxeddim."
Neurobiological data provide physical evidence for a theoretical approach to the investigation of cognition. Therefore it narrows the research area and makes it much more exact.,Isefka isnudranen yaɛnan allaɣ fkan-d anza i yiwet n tmuɣli n unadi ɣef ufiqi. S wakka samecteḥen tamnaḍt n unadi yarna erran-tt d tusdidt akteṛ.
