The correlation between brain pathology and behaviour supports scientists in their research.,Assaɣ illan ger lehlak n wallaɣ akked ṭbiɛa ittḥami imusnawen deg unadi.
"It has been known for a long time that different types of brain damage, traumas, lesions, and tumours affect behaviour and cause changes in some mental functions.","Ittwassen aṭas aya belli leṣnaf yemgaraden n lemḍaṛṛa iḍeṛṛun i wallaɣ, tuddza, aṭṭan, akked iwelsan sɛan tazrirt ɣef ṭbiɛa yarna gellun-d s ubeddel di kra n lexdayem n wallaɣ."
The rise of new technologies allows us to see and investigate brain structures and processes never seen before.,Anulfu n tetiknulujiyin timaynutin iǧǧa-yaɣ ad nwali yarna ad nenadi allaɣ d wayen id-ittilin deg-s ayen werǧin nwala uqbel.
This provides us with a lot of information and material to build simulation models which help us to understand processes in our mind.,Ay-agi ifka-aɣ-d aṭas n isallen akked tenga iwakken ad d-nebnu imedyaten ittcabin ara ad ɣ-iḥamin ad nefhem amek tteddun lecɣal deg wallaɣ-neɣ.
"Although AI has a strong connotation of science fiction, AI forms a very important branch of computer science, dealing with behavior, learning and intelligent adaptation in a machine.","Xas akken tiḥerci n tṣenniɛt teqqen ɣer uxayel ussnan, tiḥerci n tṣenniɛt d afurek agejdan di tsenselkimt, id-ilhan d lexdayem, d uḥfaḍ akked tserwest iḥercen di tṣenniɛt."
Research in AI involves making machines to automate tasks that require intelligent behavior.,Anadi di tḥerci n tṣenniɛt d aselmed i tmacinin ad xedment i yiman-nsent lxedma itteḥwiǧin tiḥerci.
"Examples include control, planning and scheduling, the ability to answer customer diagnoses and questions, as well as handwriting recognition, voice and face.","Ger imedyaten aselḥu, aheggi, tiririt i imsaɣen akked ɣef iseqsiyen, akked uɛqal n tira n ufus, n taɣect akked uqadum."
"Such things have become separate disciplines, which focus on providing solutions to real life problems.","Lecɣal am wi-gi uɣalen d innaren yebḍan, yarran dehn-nsen ɣef tifin n tifrat i wuguren n tudert n tidett."
"The AI ​​system is now often used in the fields of economics, medicine, engineering and the military, as has been built in several home computer and video game software applications.","Anagraw n tḥerci n tṣenniɛt tura ittusexdam s umata deg unnar n tdamsa, tujjya, tajenyuṛt akked tserdast, itteddu daɣen deg waṭas n wahhilen n uselkim n wexxam akked wuraren."
Field trips are a large part of any classroom. Quite often a teacher would love to take her students places to which a bus trip is not an option.,Tuffɣa ɣer wennar d aḥric agejdan di yal tasmilt. S umata aselmad ibeɣɣu ad yawi inelmaden-is ɣer imukan ur nesɛi ara amesni s lkaṛ.
"Technology offers the solution with virtual field trips. Students can look at museum artifacts, visit an aquarium, or admire beautiful art while sitting with their class.","Tatiknulujit tefka-d tifrat n tuffɣa tuhlist ɣer wennar. Inelmaden zemren ad d-ẓṛen asalay, ad rzun ɣer ukwaryum, neɣ ad walin talwiḥt n tẓuṛi nutni qqimen di tesmilt."
Sharing a field trip virtually is also a great way to reflect a on a trip and share experiences with future classes.,Attekki di tuffɣa ɣer wennar s wudem uhlis d tarrayt igerzen daɣen i uxemmem ɣer tirza akked tmenna n tirmit-agi di tesmilin id-iteddun.
"For example, each year students from Bennet School in North Carolina design a website about their trip to the State Capital, each year the website gets remodeled, but old versions are kept online to serve as a scrapbook.","Amedya, yal aseggas inelmaden n Uɣerbaz n Bennet di Karulina n Ugafa xeddmen-d tansa n anternet ɣef tirza-nsen ɣer Tmannaɣt n Lwilaya, yal aseggas tansa-agi snernayen-tt, maca ileqman iqdimen ttwajemɛen di anternet i udlis n usmekti."
"Blogs can also help improve student writing. While students often begin their blog experience with sloppy grammar and spelling, the presence of an audience generally changes that.","Ablug izmer daɣen ad isnerni tira n inelmaden. Xas akken inelmaden s umata beddun tirmit-nsen n ublug s tucḍiwin n tirawalt akked tjeṛṛumt, tilin n imsefliden s umata ittbeddil ay-agi."
"Since students are often the most critical audience, the blog writer begins to strive to improve writing to avoid criticism.","Imi inelmaden s umata d imsefliden id-ittakken tizeɣnin s watas, amyaru n ublug ibda iḥṛeṣ iman-is iwakken ad isnerni tira-s iwakken ad neqsent tzeɣnin."
"Also blogging ""forces students to become more savvy about the world around them."" The need to feed the interest of the audience inspires students to be clever and interesting (Toto, 2004).","Rnu-yas ablug ""ideggir inelmaden ad issinen kter amaḍal isen-d-izzin."" lmeḥwiǧat n usnerni n wazal isen-ttaken imsefliden ideggir-iten ad ilin ḥeṛcen yarna jebbden tamuɣli (Toto, 2004)."
"Blogging is a tool that inspires collaboration, and encourages students to extend learning well beyond the traditional school day.","Ablug d allal ideggiren ɣer lemɛawna, yarna isebɣas inelmaden iwakken ad swesɛen tamusni-nsen nnig n wass n uɣerbaz amensay."
"Appropriate use of blogs ""can empower students to become more analytical and critical; through actively responding to Internet materials, students can define their positions in the context of others' writings as well as outline their own perspectives on particular issues (Oravec, 2002).","Asexdem iwatan n ublug ""izmer ad iseǧhed inelmaden iwakken ad d-fɣen snen ad selḍen yarna ad d-fken tazɣent ; s tukci n tririyin mebla aḥbas i lecɣal n anternet, inelmaden zemren ad fken ṛṛay-nsen s usentel n tira n wiyiḍ yarna ad d-fken tamuɣli-nsen ɣef walebɛaḍ n temsal (Urabek, 2002)."
"Ottawa is Canada's charming, bilingual capital and features an array of art galleries and museums that showcase Canada's past and present.","Utawa d tamannaɣt n Kanada icebḥen, iheddṛen snat n tutlayin yarna i yesɛan aṭas n temziknin n tẓuṛi akked isalayen id-iskanen akud n amezruy akked wakud n tura n Kanada."
Farther south is Niagara Falls and the north is home to the untapped natural beauty of the Muskoka and beyond.,Akkin ɣer unẓul d Aceṛcuṛ n Nyagara ma deg ugafa tella cbaḥa tagamant ur nettwasexdem ara n Muskuka akked wayen illan deffir-s.
All these things and more highlight Ontario as what is considered quintessentially Canadian by outsiders.,Akk lecɣal-agi akked kter n way-a sbanayen-d Unṭaryu d ayen ittuneḥsaben d Akanadi n tidett sɣuṛ ibaṛṛaniyen.
Large areas further north are quite sparsely populated and some is nearly uninhabited wilderness.,Timnaḍin wessiɛen akkin ɣer ugafa ur sɛint ara aṭas n imezdaɣ ma d kra n temnaḍin d lexla qrib ur ttwazedɣent ara.
For a comparison of population that surprises many: There are more African Americans living in the US than there are Canadian citizens.,Yiwen userwes n imezdaɣ issewhamen : D Ifriqiyen Imarikaniyen izedɣen i Marikan i xilla wamma iɣeṛman Ikanadiyen.
The East African Islands are in the Indian Ocean off the eastern coast of Africa.,Tigzirin Tifriqiyin n Usamer llant deg Ugaraw Ahendi akkin yiran n Tefriqt.
"Madagascar is by far the biggest, and a continent on its own when it comes to wildlife.","Madagaskar d tameqqrant akk deg-sent, yarna d amenẓaw weḥdes deg wayen yaɛnan iɣerṣiwen d yemɣan."
"Most of the smaller islands are independent nations, or associated with France, and known as luxury beach resorts.","Amur ameqqran n tegzirin timecṭaḥ d leǧnas imunanen, neɣ iqqnen ɣer Fransa, yarna ttwasnent s yisem n imukan n ucucef n ulameɣ."
"The Arabs also brought Islam to the lands, and it took in a big way in the Comoros and Mayotte.","Ula d iɛraben wwin-d tineslemt ɣer tmura-agi, yarna telḥa mliḥ di Kumurus akked Mayut."
"European influence and colonialism began in the 15th century, as Portuguese explorer Vasco da Gama found the Cape Route from Europe to India.","Tazrirt Turubit akked temharsa bdant di lqaṛn wis 15, mi d-yufa uḥewwas Basku da Gama Abrid n Kab si Uruba ɣer Lhend."
"In the north the region is bounded by the Sahel, and in the south and west by the Atlantic Ocean.","Ɣer ugafa tamnaḍt izzi-as-d Saḥel, ɣer unẓul akked umalu izzi-as-d Ugaraw Aṭlanṭi."
"Women: It is recommended that any women travellers say that they are married, regardless of actual marital status.","Tilawin : ittuweṣa d akken akk tilawin timinigin ad d-inint belli zewǧent, akken tebɣu tili lḥala-nes n tidett."
It is helpful to also wear a ring (just not one that looks too expensive.,Ad telhu daɣen tmelsa n txatemt (mačči tin ara d-ibanen teɣlay mliḥ.
"Women should realize that cultural differences may result in what they would consider harassment and it is not uncommon to be followed, grabbed by the arm, etc.","Tilawin ilaq ad fehment belli lxilaf deg idles izmer ad d-yawi ayen ara ḥesbent d awwaḍ yarna mačči d ayen iffɣen i tnummi ad ttwatebɛent, ad d-ttwaṭfent si teɣṛuḍt, irkelli."
"Be firm in turning down men, and don't be afraid to stand your ground (cultural differences or not, it doesn't make it ok!).","Ilikent tǧehdemt mi ara tagimt irgazen, yarna ur ttagademt ara ad teṭfemt deg wawal-nkent (illa lxilaf deg yidles neɣ ulac, ay-agi ur ilaq ara!)"
"The modern city of Casablanca was founded by Berber fishermen in the 10th century BCE, and was used by the Phoenicians, Romans, and the Merenids as a strategic port called Anfa.","Tamdint tatrart n Kazablanka bnan-tt iṣeyyaden imaziɣen di lqaṛn wis 10 uqbel Lmasiḥ, umbeɛd tettwasexdem sɣuṛ Ifiniqiyen, Irumaniyen, akked Imiriniden d asagen isem-is Anfa."
"The Portuguese destroyed it and rebuilt it under the name Casa Branca, only to abandon it after an earthquake in 1755.","Iburtugiyen hudden-tt umbeɛd ɛawden bnan-tt semman-as Kaza Branka, uɣalen ǧǧan-tt mi tenguga lqaɛa di 1755."
The Moroccan sultan rebuilt the city as Daru l-Badya and it was given the name Casablanca by Spanish traders who established trading bases there.,Sselṭan Amarruki iɛawwed ibna-tt s yisem n Daru l-Badya umbeɛd ittunefk-as yisem n Kazablanka sɣuṛ imsenziyen Isbaniyen i yeṭṭfen imukan isenzanen din.
Casablanca is one of the least interesting places to shop in all of Morocco.,Kazablanka d yiwen seg imukan ur njebbed ara yakk deg wayen yaɛnan lqeḍyan di lmarruk kamel.
"Around the old Medina it's easy to find places selling traditional Moroccan goods, such as tagines, pottery, leather goods, hookahs, and a whole spectrum of geegaws, but it's all for the tourists.","Ɣer leryaf n Midina taqdimt teshel tifin n imukan iznuzun sselɛa tamensayt Tamarrukit, am ṭaǧin, leḥwal n taleɣt, sselɛa n weglim, cica, akked ugraw ikemlen n jigaw, maca ay-agi akk i iḥewwasen kan."
Goma is a tourist city of the Democratic Republic of Congo in the extreme east near Rwanda.,Guma d tamdint tamerrayt n Tegduda Tamagdant n Kungu akkin i usamar ɣer tama n Rwanda.
"In 2002 Goma was destroyed by lava from the Nyiragongo volcano which buried most of the town’s streets, particularly the town centre.","Di 2002 Guma thudd-itt iḥemmalen n tmes n teẓṛumest Nyiragungu i ymeḍlen tuget n yiberdan n temnaḍt, ladɣa ammas n temnaḍt."
"While Goma is reasonably safe, any visits outside of Goma should be researched to understand the state of the fighting that persists in the North Kivu province.","Γas akken Guma tesεa akka taɣellist s wudem attwadag, yal tirzi beṛṛa n Guma ilaq ad yili unadi i wakken ad nefhem addad n umennuɣ i d-mazal di tɣiwant n Kifu n Ugafa."
The city is also the base to climb the Nyiragongo volcano along with some of the cheapest Mountain Gorilla tracking in Africa.,Tamdint daɣen d lsas i uggafey ɣef teẓṛumest n Nyiragungu akked kra n uḍfar n Yiguriyen n Wedrar rxisen akk di Tefriqt.
You can use boda-boda (motorcycle taxi) to get around Goma. The normal (local) price is ~500 Congolese Francs for the short ride.,Tzemreḍ ad tesxedmeḍ buda-buda (ataksi s umuṭu) i wakken ad tḍewreḍ di Guma. Ssuma tamagnut (tadigant) d ~ 500 Ifranen Ikunguliyen i umecwaṛ amecṭuḥ.
"Combined with its relative inaccessibility, ""Timbuktu"" has come to be used as a metaphor for exotic, distant lands.","Imi tewɛeṛ i unekcum, ""Timbuktu"" tuɣal d amerwes i tmura tibeṛṛaniyin ibaɛden."
"Today, Timbuktu is an impoverished town, although its reputation makes it a tourist attraction, and it has an airport.","Ass-agi, Timbuktu d tamdint tigellilt, xas akken tamucaɛit-is terra-tt d amekkan id-ijebbden iḥewwasen, yarna tesɛa anafag."
"In 1990, it was added to the list of world heritage sites in danger, due to the threat of desert sands.","Di 1990, tettwarna ɣer wumuɣ n imukan n tgemmi n ddunit illan deg umihi, imi itt-id-iḥṛes ṛmel n ṣeḥṛa."
It was one of the major stops during Henry Louis Gates' PBS special Wonders of the African World.,D yiwen seg imukan igejdanen anda iḥbes Henri Lwis Gayts mi yexdem tadwilt n PBS Lɛaǧayeb n Umaḍal Afriqi.
"The city is in stark contrast to the rest of the country's cities, because it has more of an Arabic flair than of an African.","Tamdint temxalaf mliḥ ɣef temdinin niḍen n tmurt-agi, axaṭeṛ tesɛa rriḥa Taɛṛabt kter n Tefriqit."
"The Kruger National Park (KNP) lies in the north-east of South Africa and runs along the border of Mozambique in the east, Zimbabwe in the north, and the southern border is the Crocodile River.","Alma Aɣelnaw n Kruger izga-d ɣer ugafa-asamer n Tefriqt n Unẓul yarna iṛuḥ s teɣzi n tilist n Muzambiq ɣer usamer, Zimbabwi ɣer ugafa, akked tilist n unẓul d Iɣẓeṛ n Ukrukudil."
"The park covers 19,500 km² and is divided in 14 different ecozones, each supporting different wildlife.","Alma isɛa 19500 km² yarna ibḍa ɣef 14 n temnaḍin tisnazdaɣanin, yal yiwet tesɛa tudert n lexla yemgaraden."
It is one of the main attractions of South Africa and it is considered the flagship of South African National Parks (SANParks).,D yiwen seg imukan igejdanen ijebbden iḥewwasen di Tefriqt n Unẓul yarna ittuneḥsab d azamul n Ilmaten Iɣelnawen n Tefriqt n Unẓul.
"As with all South African National Parks, there are daily conservation and entry fees for the park.","Am Ilmaten Iɣelnawen n Tefriqt n Unẓul irkelli, tella suma n useḥbiber akked ukcam n yal ass ɣer ulma."
"It may also be beneficial for one to buy a Wild Card, which provides entry to either selections of parks in South Africa or all of the South African National Parks.","Izmer ad ilhu daɣen i umdan ad d-yaɣ Takarṭa Taweḥcit, i yesɛan tesriḥ n wekcam ɣer ugraw n ilmaten di Tefriqt n Unẓul neɣ ɣer yakk Ilmaten Iɣelnawen n Tefriqt n Unẓul."
Hong Kong Island gives the territory of Hong Kong its name and is the place that many tourists regard as the main focus.,Tigzirt n Hung Kung tefka i tmurt n Hung Kung isem-is yarna d amekkan ttwalin iḥewwasen s wudem agejdan.
The parade of buildings that make the Hong Kong skyline has been likened to a glittering bar chart that is made apparent by the presence of the waters of Victoria Harbour.,Derra n izadaɣen i yerran igli n Hung Kung icuba unuɣ imsiḍen s tḥucay id-tesban tilin n waman n Usagen n Bikturya.
"To get the best views of Hong Kong, leave the island and head for the Kowloon waterfront opposite.","Ma tebɣiḍ imeẓriyen imawayen n Hung Kung, effeɣ si tegzirt ruḥ ɣer idis iqublen aman n Kuwlun."
The great majority of Hong Kong Island's urban development is densely packed on reclaimed land along the northern shore.,Amur ameqqran n unerni n temdint n Tegzirt n Hung Kung ibna ɣef innaren id-ittwakksen s teɣzi n yiri n yilel n ugafa.
"This is the place the British colonisers took as their own and so if you are looking for evidence of the territory's colonial past, this is a good place to start.","D wa-gi i d amekkan ḥesben imhuras Ibriṭaniyen d ayla-nsen daymi ma tettnadiḍ anza ɣef yezri ahersan n tmurt-agi, d amekkan igerzen ad tebduḍ deg-s."
"The Sundarbans are the largest littoral mangrove belt in the world, stretching 80 km (50 mi) into the Bangladeshi and Indian hinterland from the coast.","Sundarbanz d taɣeggaḍt tameqqrant yakk di ddunit n tjuṛ n mangrub illan ɣef yiri n yilel, iẓẓlen ɣef 80 km (50 lemyal) ɣer temnaḍin n daxel n Bangladac akked Lhend seg yiri n yilel."
The Sundarbans has been declared a UNESCO World Heritage Site. The part of the forest within Indian territory is called Sundarbans National Park.,Sundarbanz ittuɛeggen d Amekkan n Tgemmi n Ddunit n Yunisku. Aḥric n teẓgi iddan ɣer tmurt n Lhend isem-is Alma Aɣelnaw n Sundarbanz.
The forests aren't just mangrove swamps though — they include some of the last remaining stands of the mighty jungles which once covered the Gangetic plain.,Maca tiẓegwa-agi mačči kan d tjuṛ n mangrub - sɛant kra n wayen id-iqqimen si tẓegwa timeqqranin i yeɣummen zik lewḍat n Ganǧ.
"The Sundarbans cover an area of 3,850 km², of which about one-third is covered in water/marsh areas.","Sundarbanz iɣumm tamnaḍt isɛan 3850 km², yiwen n umur ɣef krad deg-s iččuṛ d aman/timedwin."
"Since 1966 the Sundarbans have been a wildlife sanctuary, and it is estimated that there are now 400 Royal Bengal tigers and about 30,000 spotted deer in the area.","Si 1966 Sundarbanz d taɛezzult n tudert taweḥcit, llan wazal n 400 n iksilen igeldanen n Bengal akked wazal n 30000 n teɣzalin tibaṛṛeqmucin di temnaḍt-agi."
"Buses depart the inter-district bus station (across the river) throughout the day, though most, especially those heading to the east and Jakar/Bumthang leave between 06:30 and 07:30.","Ttaqlaɛent lkiṛan si teɣsert n lkiṛan n ger-tudrin (ad zegrent i yeɣẓer) s ṭul n wass, xas akken amur ameqqran, abaɛda tid ittruḥun ɣer usamer akked Jakar/Bumtang ttaqlaɛent ger 06:30 akked 07:30."
"As the inter-district buses are often full, it is advisable to purchase a ticket a few days in advance.","Imi zgant ttaččaṛent lkiṛan n ger-tudrin, tettuweṣṣa tiɣin n itiki kra n wussan uqbel."
"Most districts are served by small Japanese Coaster Buses, which are comfortable and sturdy.","Amur amuqqran n tuddar ttawint ɣur-sent isakalen imecṭaḥ Tijabuniyin n Kuster, i yesɛan astaɛfu yarna ǧehdent."
"Shared taxis are a quick and comfortable means to travel to nearby places, such as Paro (Nu 150) and Punakha (Nu 200).","Aṭaksi ucrik d allal aɣawal yarna isɛan astaɛfu i tirza ɣer imukan iqaṛben, am Baru (Nu 150) akked Bunaka (Nu 200)."
The Oyapock River Bridge is a cable-stayed bridge. It spans the Oyapock River to link the cities of Oiapoque in Brazil and Saint-Georges de l'Oyapock in French Guiana.,Tiqenṭeṛt n Yeɣẓer n Uyabuk d tiqenṭeṛt iṭṭfen s imurar. Tɛedda ɣef Iɣẓeṛ n Uyabuk iwakken ad teqqen tamdint n Uyabuk n Brazil ɣer San Ǧurǧ n Uyabuk di Tginit Taṛumit.
"The two towers rise to a height of 83 meters, it's 378 meters long and it has two lanes of 3.50 m wide.","Sin-nni lebṛuj ɛlayen 83 n lmitrat, sɛan di teɣzi 378 n lmitrat akked sin ibardan ihrawen 3.50 m."
"The vertical clearance under the bridge is 15 meters. Construction was completed in August 2011, it didn't open to traffic until March 2017.","Ilem ddaw n tqenṭeṛt isɛa 15 n lmitrat. Lebni-nes ikfa di Ɣuct 2011, ur yeldi ara i tikli n tkeṛṛusin armi d Meɣres 2017."
"The bridge is scheduled to be fully operational in September 2017, when the Brazilian customs checkpoints are expected to be finished.","Tiqenṭeṛt tettuhegga iwakken ad tili tleḥḥu akken ilaq di Cutember 2017, mi ara kfun aheggi n tneqqiḍin n uḥettec n Brazil."
"The Guaraní were the most significant indigenous group inhabiting what is now Eastern Paraguay, living as semi-nomadic hunters who also practised subsistence agriculture.","Gwaṛani d agraw n imezdaɣ ineṣliyen ameqqṛan yakk i yezedɣen ayen iwumi qqaren tura Baragway n Usamer, llan d iṣeyyaden ittinigen sya ɣer da i yexedmen daɣen tafellaḥt."
"The Chaco region was home to other groups of indigenous tribes such as the Guaycurú and Payaguá, who survived by hunting, gathering and fishing.","Tamnaḍt n Čaku daɣen d amekkan n tmezduɣt n igrawen niḍen n teqbilin tineṣliyin am Gwaykuru akked Bayagwa, i yeddren s ṣyada, agmar akked iselman."
"In the 16th century Paraguay, formerly called ""The Giant Province of the Indies"", was born as a result of the encounter of Spanish conquerors with the native indigenous groups.","Di lqaṛn wis 16 Baragway, iwumi qqaṛen zik ""Tamnaḍt Tameqqrant n Ihendiyen"", tlul-d mi myagaren imhuras Iṣbaniyen akked igrawen ineṣliyen."
The Spaniards started the colonization period which lasted for three centuries.,Isbaniyen bdan tallit n tsehrest i yekkan krad n leqṛun.
"Since the foundation of Asunción in 1537, Paraguay has managed to keep a lot of its indigenous character and identity.","Si lebni n temdint n Asunsyun di 1537, Baragway tsaweḍ ad teṭṭef deg waṭas n ṣifat-is tineṣliyin akked tnekkit-is."
Argentina is well known for having one of the best polo teams and players in the world.,Arjentin tettwassen s sɛaya n yiwet ger trebbuyaɛ akked imyuraren imawayen n bulu di ddunit.
The largest tournament of the year takes place in December at the polo fields in Las Cañitas.,Timzizzelt tameqqrant yakk n useggas tettili di Duǧember deg innaren n bulu di Las Kanyitas.
Smaller tournaments and matches can also be seen here at other times of the year.,Timzizlin akked temliliyin timecṭaḥ zemrent daɣen ad ilint da-gi di lewqat niḍen deg useggas.
"For news on tournaments and where to buy tickets for polo matches, check Asociacion Argentina de Polo.","I yisallen ɣef temzizlin akked wanda ttnuzen itikiyen i temliliyin n bulu, wali Tadukkla Tarjuntinit n Bulu."
The official Falklands currency is the Falkland pound (FKP) whose value is set equivalent to that of one British pound (GBP).,Idrimen unṣiben n Falklands d Falkland bawnd (FKP) i yesɛan azal iɛedlen akked win n Britic bawnd (GBP).
Money can be exchanged at the only bank in the islands which is located in Stanley across from the FIC West store.,Idrimen zemren ad d-ttubeddlen di lbanka tawḥidt illan di tegzirin tezga-d di Stanley ɣer tama id-iqublen taḥanutt n FIK West.
British pounds will generally be accepted anywhere in the islands and within Stanley credit cards and United States dollars are also often accepted.,Britic bawnd ittwaqbal s umata di yal amekkan ɣef tegzirin-agi yarna di Stanley ula d lkarṭat n lbanka akked udulaṛ Amarikani ttwaqbalen s waṭas.
"On the outlying islands credit cards will probably not be accepted, although British and United States currency may be taken; check with the owners in advance to determine what is an acceptable payment method.","Di tegzirin ibaɛden ahat ur ttaqbalen ara lkaṛṭat n lbanka, xas akken idrimen Ibriṭaniyen akked Imarikaniyen zemren ad ttwaqeblen; wali akked bab n tḥanutt ɣef zik iwakken ad k-d-yini d anta d tarrayt n lexlaṣ ittwaqbalen."
"It is nearly impossible to exchange Falklands currency outside of the islands, so exchange money prior to leaving the islands.","Qrib d awezɣi ad ttwabeddlen idrimen n Falklands baṛṛa n tegzirin, ɣef ay-agi beddel-d idrimen uqbel ad teffɣeḍ tigzirin."
"Since Montevideo is south of the Equator, it is summer there when it's winter in the Northern Hemisphere and vice versa.","Imi Muntibidyu tella di ttnaṣfa n unẓul n ddunit, d anebdu din mi ara yili d ccetwa di ttnaṣfa n ugafa akkina kan."
"Montevideo is in the subtropics; in the summer months, temperatures above +30°C are common.","Muntibidyu tezga-d di temnaḍt qrib-taṭrubikant; deg wagguren n unebdu, ttilint s waṭas tfesniwin n lḥamu nnig +30°C."
"The winter can be deceptively chilly: temperatures rarely go below freezing, but the wind and humidity combine to make it feel colder than what the thermometer says.","Ccetwa tezmer ad tili tsemmeḍ s wudem akellax: tifesniwin n lḥamu idrus anda ttṣubbunt ddaw yilem, maca aḍu akked ṛḍubga dukkulen dɣa ittuɣal lḥal isemmeḍ kter n wayen id-skanent tfesniwin n lḥamu."
"There are no particular ""rainy"" and ""dry"" seasons: the amount of rain stays roughly the same throughout the year.","Ulac talliyin n ""igefran"" akked ""takewt"" ibanen: acḥal id-ikkaten n ugeffur ur ittbeddil ara s teɣzi n useggas."
"Though many of the animals in the park are used to seeing humans, the wildlife is nonetheless wild and should not be fed or disturbed.","Xas akken aṭas n iɣerṣiwen deg ulma wulfen ttwalin imdanen, tudert taweḥcit ad teqqim d taweḥcit daymi ur ilaq ara ad s-tettunefk lmakla neɣ ad tettunǧeɛ."
"According to park authorities, stay at least 100 yards/meters away from bears and wolves and 25 yards/meters from all other wild animals!","Aɛlaḥsab n srabes n ulma, bɛed anda ma ulac 100 n yard/lmitrat ɣef ursan akked wuccanen 25 n yard/lmitrat ɣef akk iɣerṣiwen iweḥciyen niḍen!"
"No matter how docile they may look, bison, elk, moose, bears, and nearly all large animals can attack.","Akken ibɣu banen-d sehlen, ibizunen, elken, imuzen, ursan, akked qrib akk iɣerṣiwen imeqqranen zemren ad wwten fell-ak."
"Each year, dozens of visitors are injured because they didn't keep a proper distance. These animals are large, wild, and potentially dangerous, so give them their space.","Yal aseggas, aṭas n inerzufen i yettajraḥen imi ur ǧǧin ara lfiraq ilaqen gar-asen. Iɣerṣiwen-agi meqqren, d iweḥciyen yarna d imihawen, ɣef ay-agi beɛɛed fell-asen."
"In addition, be aware that odors attract bears and other wildlife, so avoid carrying or cooking odorous foods and keep a clean camp.","Yarna, ẓẓeṛ belli arriḥa tjebbed-d ursan akked iɣerṣiwen niḍen, ɣef ay-agi ur ttawi ara neɣ ur sewway ara lmakla isɛan arriḥa yarna seḥṛeṣ ɣef tezdeg n umekkan."
"Apia is the capital of Samoa. The town is on the island of Upolu and has a population of just under 40,000.",Abya d tamannaɣt n Samwa. Tamdint tezga-d di Tegzirt n Ubulu yarna tesɛa uṭun n imezdaɣ ur newwiḍ ara mliḥ 40000.
Apia was founded in the 1850s and has been the official capital of Samoa since 1959.,Abya tettwabna deg iseggasen n 1850 umbeɛd tuɣal d tamannaɣt tunṣibt n Samwa si 1959.
"The harbor was the site of an infamous naval standoff in 1889 when seven ships from Germany, the US, and Britain refused to leave the harbor.","Asagen d amekkan n iɣeblan awlalen mucaɛen s wudem n diri di 1889 mi yugint ṣa n teflugin n Almanya, Marikan, akked Briṭanya ad fɣent seg usagen."
"All the ships were sunk, except for one British cruiser. Nearly 200 American and German lives were lost.","Tiflugin akk zedrent, ḥala yiwet n teflugt Tabriṭanit. Qrib 200 Imarikaniyen akked Ilmaniyen i yemmuten."
"During the struggle for independence organised by the Mau movement, a peaceful gathering in the town resulted in the killing of the paramount chief Tupua Tamasese Lealofi III.","Deg umennuɣ i tmunent id-ihegga umussu n Mu, anejmuɛ ulwigan di temdint igla-d s tmenɣiwt n uqeṛṛuy ameqqṛan Tubwa Tamasisi Lyalufi III."
"There are many beaches, due to Auckland's straddling of two harbours. The most popular ones are in three areas.","Llant aṭas n teftisin, imi myekcamen sin isugan n Awkland wa deg wa. Wid yettwassnen akk llan deg kraḍ n yemḍiqen."
North Shore beaches (in North Harbour district) are on the Pacific Ocean and stretch from Long Bay in the north to Devonport in the south.,Tiftisin n Yiri n Ugafa (deg umḍiq n Usagen n Ugafa) llant deg Ilel Ulwigan yerna yejbed si Lung Bay deg ugafa ɣer Usagen Defun deg wenẓul.
"They are almost all sandy beaches with safe swimming, and most have shade provided by pohutukawa trees.","Qrib ad ilint akk d tiftisin n wemlal yesεan taɣellist i uεumu, yerna akk sεant tili i d-fkan isekla n buhutukawa."
"Tamaki Drive beaches are on the Waitemata Harbour, in the upmarket suburbs of Mission Bay and St Heliers in Central Auckland.","Tiftisin n Tamaki Drayb zgan-t-d deg Usagen n Waytimata, deg ṭṭrufat n temdint n ulameɣ n Misyun Bay d Sant Halyers deg tlemmast n Awkland."
These are sometimes-crowded family beaches with a good range of shops lining the shore. Swimming is safe.,Tigi d tiftisin yettačaṛen tikkwal d tiwaculin s waṭas n leṣnaf n tḥuna ikhedmen azlem ɣef yiri n yilel. Tella tɣellist i uεummu.

"Skiing is a major travelling activity with many enthusiasts, occasionally known as ""ski bums,"" planning entire vacations around skiing at a particular location.","Aḥlucceg deg udfel d ccɣel agejdan n tteḥwas n waṭas n wid iḥemmlen ay-agi, tikwal qqaren-asen ""wid iḥemmlen ski,"" ttheggin imuras s lekmal ɣef uḥlucceg deg udfel deg yiwen n umekkan."
The idea of skiing is very old — cave paintings depicting skiers date back as far as 5000 BC!,Tikti n uḥlucceg deg udfel d taqdimt mliḥ - unuɣen n ifran ttawṣafen-d wid itteḥluccugen deg udfel si 5000 iseggasen uqbel Lmasiḥ !

"Backpacking by ski: This activity is also called backcountry ski, ski touring or ski hiking.","Amerreḥ s uḥlucceg deg udfel : ccɣel-agi qqaren-as daɣen tikli d uḥlucceg ɣef udfel, neɣ aḥewwes d uḥlucceg ɣef udfel."
"It is related to but usually not involving alpine style ski touring or mountaineering, the latter ones done in steep terrain and requiring much stiffer skis and boots.","Iqqen maca s umata ur iseɛɛu ara amerreḥ d uḥlucceg ɣef udfel neɣ talleyt n idurar, tineggura-agi ttilint di tsaksart yarna tteḥwiǧint iskiyen akked libuṭ iqquṛen s waṭas."
Think of the skiing route as of a similar hiking route.,Wali abrid n uḥlucceg am win n tikli.

"The Schengen zone, however, works somewhat like one country in this respect.","Tamnaḍt n Cangan, akken ibɣu yili, tleḥḥu am yiwet n tmurt deg wayen yaɛnan ay-agi."
"As long as you stay in this zone, you can generally cross borders without going through passport control checkpoints again.","Skud telliḍ daxel n temnaḍt-agi, s umata tzemreḍ ad tzegreḍ tilas mebla asefqed n umsineg tikkelt niḍen."
"Similarly, by having a Schengen visa, you do not need to apply for visas to each of the Schengen member countries separately, hence saving time, money and paperwork.","Daɣen, ma tesɛiḍ abiza n Cangan, ur teḥwaǧeḍ ara ad tsutreḍ abiza i yal tamurt tamedrawt n Cangan, s wakka ad tḥerzeḍ akud, idrimen akked lekwaɣeḍ."
There is no universal definition for which manufactured items are antiques. Some tax agencies define goods older than 100 years as antiques.,Ulac tabadut tamaḍlant id-yeqqaṛen melmi ara tuɣal tɣawsa ittwaxedmen d taglest. Kra n tnariyin n tebzert ḥesbent tiɣawsiwin iɛeddan 100 n iseggasen di laɛmeṛ-nsent d tigelsin.
"The definition has geographic variations, where the age limit might be shorter in places such as North America than in Europe.","Tabadut-agi tettemxalaf s wudem arakalan, anda tilist n laɛmeṛ izmer ad tili twezzil deg imukan am Marikan n Ugafa kter n Uruba."
"Handicraft products might be defined as antiques, though they are younger than similar mass-produced goods.","Tiɣawsiwin imexdumen s ufus zemren ad ttuneḥsabent d tigelsin, xas akken meẓẓyit ɣef tɣawsiwin ittemcabin ittwaxeddmen s waṭas."
Reindeer husbandry is an important livelihood among the Sámi and the culture surrounding the trade is important also for many with other professions.,Ttṛebga n teɣzalin d lxedma tagejdant swayes ttidiren Iṣamiyen yarna idles izzin i tnezzut d agejdan daɣen ɣer waṭas n yemdanen ixeddmen ayen niḍen.
"Even traditionally, though, not all Sámi have been involved in big scale reindeer husbandry, but lived from fishing, hunting and similar, having reindeer mostly as draft animals.","Ula s wudem amensay, akken ibɣu yili, mačči akk Iṣamiyen ttṛebbin tiɣzalin s ṭaqa, maca ddren s ṣyada n iselman, ṣyada akked wayen icuban, sexdamen tiɣzalin s wudem agejdan i useḥḥeb."
"Today many Sámi work in modern trades. Tourism is an important income in Sápmi, the Sámi area.","Tura aṭas n Iṣamiyen xeddmen lxedma tatrart. Aḥewwes d lmedxul agejdan di Sabmi, tamnaḍt n Ṣami."
"Though it is widely used, especially among non-Romani, the word ""Gypsy"" is often considered offensive because of its associations with negative stereotypes and inaccurate perceptions of Romani people.","Xas akken ittusexdam s waṭas, abaɛda ger war-Arrum, awal n ""Ǧibsi"" ittuneḥsab s umata d tineɛɛal imi isɛa tiktiwin n diri akked tmuɣli ur nṣeḥḥi ara n ugdud n Arrum."
"If the country you will be visiting becomes subject to a travel advisory, your travel health insurance or your trip cancellation insurance may be affected.","Ma tamurt wuɣuṛ ara tṛuḥeḍ tuɣal tesɛa ttewṣayat n lemḥadra, ṭmana tadawsant n yinig-nni neɣ ṭmana n tukksa n yinig zemrent ad beddlent."
"You may also wish to consult the advice of governments other than your own, but their advice is designed for their citizens.","Tzemreḍ daɣen ad tebɣuḍ ad teẓṛeḍ ttewṣayat n inabaḍen niḍen baṛṛa n unabaḍ-ik, maca ttewṣayat-nsen aɛnant iɣaṛman-nsen."
"As one example, American citizens in the Middle East might face different situations from Europeans or Arabs.","Yiwen n umedya, iɣaṛman Imarikaniyen deg Usamer Alemmas zemren ad qablen tignatin yemgaraden ɣef Yurubiyen neɣ Waɛṛaben."
Advisories are merely a brief summary of the political situation in one country.,Ttewṣayat-agi d agzul kan amecṭuḥ n lḥala tasertant deg walebɛaḍ n tmura.
"The views presented are often cursory, general and oversimplified compared to the more detailed information available elsewhere.","Timuɣliwin id-ittunefken deg-sent s umata d tijummanin, d timatuyin yarna ttusasehlent mliḥ mačči am isallen iččuren d ttfaṣil i yellan anda niḍen."
"Severe weather is the generic term for any dangerous weather phenomenon with the potential to cause damage, serious social disruption, or loss of human life.","Tignewt iwaɛṛen d isem amatu n yal tumant n tegnewt tamihawt i yezemren ad d-tawi lemḍaṛṛa, iɛewwiqen meqqren imettanen, neɣ lmut."
"Severe weather can occur anywhere in the world, and there are different types of it, which can depend on geography, topography, and atmospheric conditions.","Tignewt iwaɛṛen tezmer ad tili di yal amekkan di ddunit, yarna tesɛa aṭas n leṣnaf, aɛlaḥsab n tarakalt, taṭubugrafit, akked lḥala n tegnewt."
"High winds, hail, excessive precipitation, and wildfires are forms and effects of severe weather, as are thunderstorms, tornadoes, waterspouts, and cyclones.","Aḍu iǧehden, abruri, aṭas n ugeffur, akked tmes n teẓgi d udmawen akked isemda n tegnewt iwaɛṛen, am daɣen igusifen, tibuciṭanin, tibuciṭanin deg yilel, akked tbuciṭanin timeqqranin."
"Regional and seasonal severe weather phenomena include blizzards, snowstorms, ice storms, and dust storms.","Ger tumanin n tegnewt iwaɛṛen tamnaḍant yarna n tallit tibuciṭanin n wedfel, tibuciṭanin n wegris, akked tbuciṭanin n uɣebbaṛ."
Travellers are strongly advised to be aware of any risk of severe weather affecting their area as they may affect any travel plans.,Iminigen ttuweṣṣan ad ḥadren iman-nsen ɣef imihiyen n tegnewt iwaɛṛen ara iḥazzen tamnaḍt-nsen imi izmer ad isɛu tazrirt ɣef uɣawas n uḥewwes.
Anyone planning a visit to a country that could be considered a war zone should get professional training.,Yal win ibɣan ad irzu ɣer tmurt i yezemren ad tettuneḥsab d annar n ṭṛad ilaq-as usluɣmu amsadur.
A search of the Internet for 'Hostile environment course' will probably provide the address of a local company.,Anadi deg anternet ɣef 'temsirt ɣef twennaḍt tamihawt' ahat ad k-d-yefk tansa n tkebbanit tadigant.
"A course will normally cover all the issues discussed here in far greater detail, usually with practical experience.","Tamsirt s umata ad tɛeddi akk ɣef temsal id-nuder da-gi s ttfaṣil akteṛ, s tirmit deg unnar."
"A course will normally be from 2-5 days and will involve role play, a lot of first aid and sometimes weapons training.","Tamsirt ad tekk si 2-5 n wussan yarna tesɛa urar n ddur, aṭas n usluɣmu ɣef ulawi amezwaru di tegnitt n lḥaṛs akked tikwal asluɣmu s leslaḥ."
"Books and magazines dealing with wilderness survival are common, but publications dealing with war zones are few.","Idlisen akked tesɣunin iheddṛen ɣef tudert di lexla mucaɛen, maca wid iheddṛen ɣef innaren n ṭṛad drusen."
Voyagers planning sex reassignment surgery abroad must ensure they're carrying valid documents for the return trip.,Iminigen ibɣan ad xedmen abaṛasyun n ubeddel n tuzzuft di tmurt tabaṛṛanit ilaq ad twekkden belli wwin lekwaɣeḍ iwatan i umecwar n tuɣalin.
The willingness of governments to issue passports with gender not stated (X) or documents updated to match a desired name and gender varies.,Ittemxalaf lebɣi n inabaḍen i uxdam n imsinigen s tuzzuft ur d-nettwadder ara (X) neɣ i uɛiwwed n lekwaɣeḍ iwakken ad wafqen isem akked tuzzuft ittwabɣan.
Willingness of foreign governments to honour these documents is just as widely variable.,Lebɣi n inabaḍen ibaṛṛaniyen ad qadren lekwaɣeḍ-agi ittemxalaf daɣen s wudem wessiɛen.
"Searches at security checkpoints have also become far more intrusive in the post-September 11, 2001 era.",Inadiyen deg imukan n uḥettec daɣen uɣalen d ineẓdamen akter deg wakud n mbeɛd 11 Cutember 2001.
Pre-operative transgender people should not expect to pass through the scanners with their privacy and dignity intact.,Imdanen imbeddlen n tuzzuft uqbel-abaṛasyun ur ilaq ara ad ɣidden belli zemren ad ɛeddin aḥettec mebla awwaḍ n serrya-nsen akked yiseɣ-nsen.
"Rip currents are the returning flow from waves breaking off the beach, often at a reef or similar.","Lemwaji n tuɣalin d tuɣalin n lemwaji ittruẓen di teftist, s umata ɣef iblaḍen neɣ ayen iten-icuban."
"Due to the underwater topology the return flow is concentrated at a few deeper sections, and a fast current to deep water may form there.","S sebba n lxilaf n lqaɛ n yilel tuɣalin n lemwaji teqwa di kra n iḥricen ilqayen, s wakka tezmer ad d-tlal din tikli taɣawalt ɣer waman lqayen."
"Most deaths happen as result of fatigue trying to swim back against the current, which may be impossible.","Amur ameqqran n lmuta iḍeṛṛu-d s sebba n ɛeggu si lɛum mgal tikli n waman, ayen ara yilin d awezɣi."
"As soon as you get out of the current, swimming back is no more difficult than normally.","Mi d-teffɣeḍ kan i tikli-nni n waman, lɛum ad yuɣal ur iwɛiṛ ara."
"Try aiming somewhere where you are not caught again or, depending on your skills and on whether you have been noticed, you might want to wait for rescue.","Ɛṛeḍ ajbad ɣer wanda ur tettwaṭṭafeḍ ara tikkelt niḍen neɣ, aɛlaḥsab n tmussni-nek akked ma walan-k-id, ahat ad tebɣuḍ ad teṛǧuḍ lemɛawna."
"Re-entry shock comes on sooner than culture shock (there's less of a honeymoon phase), lasts longer, and can be more severe.","Tiyita n tuɣalin n unekcum tettas-d zik mliḥ lḥal ɣef tiyita n udles (drus-itt tallit n waggur n tament), tettdumu ugar n wakud, yerna tezmer ad tili qessiḥet ugar."
Travellers who had an easy time adjusting to the new culture sometimes have a particularly hard time readjusting to their native culture.,Iminigen yufan tefses deg usezg ɣer udles amaynut tikkwal seεεun akud iwaεren i wakken ad sezgen ɣer udles-nsen aneṣli.
"When returning home after living abroad, you've adapted to the new culture and lost some of your habits from your home culture.","Mi d-nuɣal s axxam seld tudert di lɣerba, tsezgeḍ ɣer udles amaynut yerna tesruḥeḍ kra n tanumi seg udles-ik aneṣli."
"When you went abroad at first, people were probably patient and understanding, knowing that travellers in a new country need to adapt.","Ma yella truḥeḍ yiwen n ubrid kan ɣer lɣerba, imdanen zemren ahat ad sebren wa ad fehmen, zran d akken iminigen deg tmurt tabeṛṛanit ḥwaǧen ad sezgen."
People may not anticipate that patience and understanding are also necessary for travellers returning home.,Imdanen zemren ur ttarran ara ddehn-nsen d akken sber d umsefhem d iḍulliyen i yimsukal i d-yuɣalen s axxam.

You can see the pyramids in the dark and you can see them in silence before the show begins.,Tzemreḍ ad twaliḍ tizumag di tilas yerna tzemreḍ ad tent-twaliḍ di tsusmi send ad ibdu wahil.

"South Shetland Islands, discovered in 1819, are claimed by several nations and have the most bases, with sixteen active in 2020.","Tigzirin n Cetland n Unẓul, i d-ufan di 1819, ssutren-tent-id waṭas n yeɣlanen yerna deg-sent tuget n yezdaren, s mraw d seddis gar-asen d aganen di 2020."
The archipelago lies 120 km north of the Peninsula. The largest is King George Island with the settlement of Villa Las Estrellas.,Agraw n tegzirin yezga-d 120 km ɣer ugafa n Tzegzirt. Tameqrant seg-sent d Tigzirt Ugellid Ǧurǧ akked taddart n Filla Las Estrellas.
"Others include Livingston Island, and Deception where the flooded caldera of a still-active volcano provides a spectacular natural harbour.","Tiyaḍ d Tigzirt Lifintun, d Lehzima anda d-yesbedd uḥemmal kaldera n teẓrumest mazal d tagant asagen agaman yessewhamen."
"Ellsworth Land is the region south of the Peninsula, bounded by the Bellingshausen Sea.","Tamurt Ellswurt d tamnaḍt yellan deg unẓul n Tzegzirt, i wumi d yezzi Ilel Bellingshawsen."
"The mountains of the Peninsula here merge into the plateau, then re-emerge to form the 360 km chain of the Ellsworth Mountains, bisected by the Minnesota Glacier.","Idurar n Tzegzirt kecmen deg ugni, dɣa mlalen-d daɣen i wakken ad ssilɣen azrar n Yidurar Ellswurt n 360 km, yebḍan ɣef sin s Ugris Minnesuta."
"The northern part or Sentinel Range has Antarctica's highest mountains, the Vinson Massif, peaking at 4892 m Mount Vinson.","Aḥric n ugafa n Uzrar Sentinel yesεa idurar εlayen akk n Antarktika, Agraw n Yidurar Finsun, taqacuct-is d 4892 m Taqacuct Finsun."
"In remote locations, without cell phone coverage, a satellite phone may be your only option.","Deg idgan ibeεden, mebla tduli n yifafusen, yezmer ad yili tiliɣṛi n ugensa d tafrant-ik taselyant."
"A satellite phone is not generally a replacement for a mobile phone, as you have to be outdoors with clear line of sight to the satellite to make a phone call.","Tiliɣṛi n ugensa ur d-yelli deg adeg n ufafus s wudem amatu, imi ilaq ad tiliḍ beṛṛa s uzlem yeṣfan n tuṭṭfa n ugensa i wakken ad tessiwleḍ."
"The service is frequently used by shipping, including pleasure craft, as well as expeditions who have remote data and voice needs.","Ameẓlu zgan ssexdamen-t iɣeṛṛuba, ladɣa iɣeṛṛuba n unecṛaḥ, akked iɣeṛṛuba yesεan isriyen n yisefka d taɣuct ɣer lebεid."
Your local telephone service provider should be able to give more information about connecting to this service.,Aqeddac n umeẓlu-ik adigan n tiliɣṛi ilaq ad yizmir ad yefk ugar n yisallen ɣef tuqqna ɣer umeẓlu-agi.

"This is especially popular with school leavers, allowing them to take a year out before university, without compromising their education.","Ayagi mechur ladɣa ɣer yinelmaden yekfan tasnawit, d ttesriḥ i wakken ad awin yiwen n useggas i yiman-nsen, mebla ma surdan asinen-nsen."
"In many cases, enrolling on a gap-year course abroad can actually improve your chances of moving into higher education back in your home country.","Deg waṭas n tejṛutin, ajerred deg temsirin n yiwen n useggas beṛṛa n tmurt yezmer ad yesselhu tignatin n unekcum ɣer usinen εlayen s tuɣalin ɣer tmurt."

"Finland is a great boating destination. The ""Land of a thousand lakes"" has thousands of islands too, in the lakes and in the coastal archipelagos.","Finland d adeg igerrzen i yinig s uɣeṛṛabu. "Although the coastal archipelagos and the biggest lakes are indeed big enough for any yacht, smaller boats or even a kayak offer a different experience.","Γas akken irexbilen n wafay d yigelmimen imeqranen d wid imeqqren s tidet i yal yaxt, iɣeṛṛuba imecṭaḥ neɣ ula d akayak ttbuddun tarmit yemgaraden."
"Boating is a national pastime in Finland, with a boat to every seven or eight people.","Asilel d amzel aɣelnaw deg Finland, s uɣeṛṛabu i yal ṣa neɣ ṭam n yemdanen."
"This is matched by Norway, Sweden and New Zealand, but otherwise quite unique (e.g. in the Netherlands the figure is one to forty).","Aya-agi yella-d ula di Nuṛwiǧ, Sswid akked Ziland Tamaynut, maca d ayiwen (amedya, deg Tmura n Wadda, uṭṭun d yiwen ɣer ṛebɛin)."
"Most of the distinct Baltic Cruises feature an extended stay in St. Petersburg, Russia.","Tuget n Tmaggirin Tibaltiyin timeẓliyin sḍuluyent iɣimi di San Betersburg, Rrus."
This means you can visit the historic city for a couple of full days while returning and sleeping on the ship at night.,Anamek-is tzemreḍ ad tḥewwseḍ deg teɣṛemt tamazrayt i kra n wussan ummiden ɣas akken ad tuɣaleḍ yerna ad tegneḍ deg uɣeṛṛabu deg iḍ.

"Courier companies are well paid for delivering things quickly. Frequently, time is very important with business documents, merchandise or spare parts for an urgent repair.","Tikebbaniyin n tnazant ttwaxellaṣent akken iwata i wakken ad ceggεen tiɣawsiwin s urured. "On some routes, the larger companies have their own planes, but for other routes and smaller firms there was a problem.","Di kra n yinigen, tikebbaniyin timeqqranin sεant tinafagin-nsent, maca i yinigen niḍen d tkebbaniyin timecṭaḥ yella-d uɣbel."
"If they sent things by air freight, on some routes it may have taken days to get through unloading and customs.","Ma yella ceggεent tiɣawsiwin s wafug, di kra n yinigen ttawint ussan i wakken ad εeddint akk tarusi d tedwana."
"The only way to get it through faster was to send it as checked luggage. "The obvious way of flying in first or business class is to fork out a thick wad of money for the privilege (or, better yet, get your company to do it for you).","Tamamekt ibanen i wafug deg taggayt tamenzut neɣ tin n lecɣal d aṣeṛṛef n waṭaṣ n yedrimen i uglam (neɣ, xir akk, ad teǧǧeḍ takebbanit ad t-texdem deg umekkan-ik)."
"However, this does not come cheap: as rough rules of thumb, you can expect to pay up to four times the normal economy fare for business, and eleven times for first class!","Maca, ay-agi ur yettili ara rxis: d alugen iqburen, tzemreḍ ad tarǧuḍ lexlaṣ n ugar n ukkuẓ n yiberdan afeqqim adamsan amagnu ɣef win n lecɣal, d mraw d yiwen n yiberdan ɣef taggayt tamenzut!"
"Generally speaking, there is no point in even looking for discounts for business or first-class seats on direct flights from A to B.","Ma yella nmeslay-d s wudem amatu, ur telli lfayda deg tmuɣli ula deg usenqes di ssuma n yifeqqimen i taggayt n lecɣal neɣ taggayt tamenzut deg wafug usrid si A ɣer B."

"The capital of Moldova is Chişinău. The local language is Romanian, but Russian is widely used.","Tamanaɣt n Muldufa d Chişinău. Tutlayt tadigant d Tarumanit, maca Tarusit tettusexdem s waṭas."
Moldova is a multi-ethnic republic that has suffered from ethnic conflict.,Muldufa d tagduda agtiriten yesεeddan amennuɣ n yiriten.
"In 1994, this conflict led to the creation of the self-proclaimed Transnistria Republic in eastern Moldova, which has its own government and currency but is not recognised by any UN member country.","Di 1994, amennuɣ-agi tegla-d s asnulfu n Tegduda Transnistria iseɣṛan iman-is deg usamar n Muldufa, i yesεan anabaḍ-is d yedrimen-is maca ur tt-teḥsib ula d tamurt tamaṣlaḍt n UN."

"All nouns, alongside the word Sie for you, always begin with a capital letter, even in the middle of a sentence.","Akk ismawen, akked wawal Sie anamek-is kunwi, zgan beddun s usekkil ameqqran, ɣas ma llan di tlemmast n tefyirt."

"If you visit the Arctic or Antarctic areas in the winter you will experience the polar night, which means that the sun doesn't rise above the horizon.","Ma terziḍ ɣer temnaḍin n Arktik neɣ n Antarktik di ccetwa ad tjaṛṛbeḍ iḍ n tqumam n ddunit, anda iṭij ur d-ittali ara nnig yigli."

Japanese work culture is more hierarchical and formal that what Westerners may be used to.,Idles n uxeddim Ajabuni d amyellalan yarna d unṣib kter n wayen fayef uɣen tanummi At n Umalu.
"Suits are standard business attire, and coworkers call each other by their family names or by job titles.","Iselsa d iselsa n uxeddim ilugan, yarna wid ixeddmen lwaḥid ttemsawalen s nekwa neɣ s yisem n lxedma."
"Workplace harmony is crucial, emphasizing group effort rather than praising individual accomplishments.","Tadukkli deg umekkan n uxeddim d tagejdant, ayen issifriren axeddim n ugraw ɣef ucekkeṛ n ternawin n yal yiwen uḥdes."
